/ /rgyud sde rin po che kun las btus pa'i thob yig de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba ma lus pa gcig tu 'dus pa rdo rje rin po che'i za ma tog ces bya ba bzhugs so//

oM swa sti/ bzod nas rnam dag 'dus ma byas dbyings rdo rje nam mkha'i dkyil lta bur/ /longs spyod rdzogs dang kha sbyor bde chen sprin gyi bla bre bshams pa las/ /sprul pa'i
gru char rtag tu bsnyil ba'i dge mtshan 'gog pa med pa yi/ /snying rjes yongs gang dpal ldan bla ma rdo rje snyems ma'i bdag pos skyongs/ /bskal bzang 'dren pa stong dbus
thugs bskyed kyi/ /lhun po mngon 'phags bcom ldan shA kya'i rgyal/ gang zhabs la chags rdul cha re res kyang / /nyes pa'i dri sbyong nam yang gtsug na mchod/ /yid can
blo yi ra ri 'khrud pa'i phul/ /lung rtogs dam pa chos kyi bdud rtsi ste/ /byang chub lang tsho ma rdzogs de srid du/ /snying la bcud len gcig tu gus pas 'dzin/ /zhi ba'i
btung ba la spyod rig grol gyi/ /yal 'dab rdzogs gyur tshogs mchog dpag bsam dbang / /rgyal ba'i lam zhugs rgyud la 'dod sbyin pa/ /dus gsum

gshegs pa kun la rab tu btud/ /sde snod rgyud sde'i lam srol gsal byed pa'i/ /blo ldan paNDi ta dang grub pa'i dbang / /'phags pa'i zhabs sen bkod pa'i yul ljongs su/ /ji snyed
byon pa'i rnam thar dran bzhin 'dud/ /gangs ljongs mig gcig thugs rje'i brtul zhugs gyis/ /lung rtogs snang ba 'dren pa'i lo paN dang / /chos rgyal bstan pa'i rtsa lag
gyur kun gyi/ /bka' drin dad pa'i snod du shor bar dka'/ /khyad par gsang chen rdo rje'i rgyud zab mo/ /'chad dang bsgrub pa'i bka' babs gang dag las/ 'khrul pa spangs
pa'i lam gyi shing rta pa/ /dpal ldan sa skya'i 'jam dbyangs rnams la 'dud/ sdug bsngal zhi byed bdud rtsi'i lto khengs pa'i/ /grub pa'i bum bzang dam pa sangs rgyas dang
/ /mkha' 'gro'i zhal gyi gdams pas mchog brnyes pa/ /khyung po brgyud par bcas la yid rab gus/ /

nA ro ta pa'i man ngag za ma tog /mnga' bdag sras dang slob mar bcas rnams kyi/ /grub pa'i 'tsho bar phog pa don ldan pa'i/ /mkhyen rtogs 'byung gnas de dag phyag gi yul/ /gangs
can rgyud sde rgya mtshos gtams gyur kyang / /mtha' dag bzhes pa khyad las ma dmigs pas/ /rig pa 'dzin pa yongs kyi ston pa mchog /kun mkhyen bu yi zhabs la phyag bgyi'o/
/rgyud sde bshad pas rdo rje 'chang ba dang / /lung brtan brnyas pas gzhan las 'phags pa dang / /phrin las zab pas kun dga' bzang po zhes/ /grags pa'i gdugs dkar mtho
la phyag 'tshal lo/ /shes bya rab 'byams khyad par gsang don la/ /skyes thob spobs pas dbang 'byor kun gzigs che/ /zab rgyas rgyud sde tshad ma'i lung thob pa/ /rje btsun
chen po yab sras zhabs la'ang 'dud/ /rnam grol lam gyi gzhi rtsa brtan byed pa'i/ /mnyam med jo bo'i bka' srol skyong rnams dang / /'jam dpal dbyangs kyi gsang ba'i
snying 'byin po/ /smra ba zla med brgyud par bcas la gus/ /bstan pa yongs rdzogs 'chad dang sgrub pa la/ /phyogs su lhung min mkhyen dang brtse ba'i gter/ /zab rgyas rgyud
sde'i nyin byed gcig bu pa/ /dkyil 'khor gtso bo gang la gus phyag 'tshal/ /mdo sngags chos kyi khri la dbang bsgyur te/ /rgyal ba'i dgongs pa smra la bsnyengs bral ba/
/phyis dus rgyud sde'i srol 'byed kun dga'i rje/ /bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan zhabs pad spyi bor len/ /rnam par snang mdzad sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i rol/ /mdzod chen lnga yi shing
rta'i srol chen btod/ /grub pa'i rgyal mtshan srid rtser bsgreng pa yi/ /yon tan rgya mtshos byang chub bar du

skyongs/ /'jam dpal dbyangs dang gnyis su mi phyed pa'i/ /shes bya rab 'byams mkhyen pa'i rnam dpyod can/ /sum ldan rdor 'dzin rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag cher/ /bsam bzhin dad
pa'i lha phyag ri ltar brtseg /dpal ldan yon tan tshogs kyi byed po yis/ /mi 'jigs gdong lnga'i khri la dbang bskur zhing / /mtha' klas skye rgur blo gros dpal ster ba/
/bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan srid rtser bsgreng la 'dud/ /rin chen byang chub sems kyis thugs rgyud gtams/ /rtse gcig sgom pa'i ting 'dzin bdud rtsi yis/ /'gro la phan bde'i
ngal 'tsho sbyin mkhas pa/ /rdo rje 'chang dngos dpal ldan bla mar 'dud/ /brtse chen kun dga'i lam srol ji snyed pa/ /thugs rgyud za ma tog tu 'khyil ba yis/ /zab gsang smin
grol rgya mtsho'i srog mthud mkhas/ /kun dga' 'jam dbyangs bka' drin dran bzhin dad/ /rnam kun mchog ldan rdo rje nam mkha'i dbyings/ /bslab gsum nor bu'i chu 'dzin bshams
pa las/ /mkhas tshul gsum gyis 'dod rgu 'jo ba'i dpal/ /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin la 'dud/ /rdo rje rnal 'byor ma yis rjes su bzung / rgyud gsum dregs
pa'i tshogs rnams bran du 'khol/ /snyan brgyud bstan pa'i srog shing gdong khar ba/ /'jam dpal bstan 'dzin bzang por snying nas gus/ /nges 'byung byang chub sems spyod
mchog rnam par dag /rim gnyis ting 'dzin 'od gsal mngon du gyur/ /mkhas tshul gsum gyis bstan pa gsal mdzad pa/ /ngag la dbang 'byor dam chos ragaya mtshor 'dud/ /nges
'byung tshul khrims rtsa ba rab brtan cing / /byang chub spyod pa'i lo 'dab phyogs brgyar grol

gsang chen 'bras bu'i snye ma g.yur za ba/ /legs bshad bzang po'i 'dod rgu sbyin la 'dud/ /shes bya rab 'byams mkhyen pa'i rnam dpyod can/ /mang thos mkhas grub ragaya mtshos
rjes su bzung / /mdo sngags rgya mtsho smra la zla med pa'i/ /'jam dpal dbyangs dngos rnam 'dren zhabs la 'dud/ /rdo rje 'chang gis rigs can so so la/ /'chams par bstan
pa'i 'jug sgo dang po ni/ /rigs gsum la sogs khyab bdag gtsor ston pa'i/ /rgyud sde'i lha tshogs kun la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rnam par snang mdzad chen po'i ting 'dzin dang
/ /gtsang ma'i kun spyod snyoms par bsgrubs nas ni/ /rig pa 'dzin pa'i go 'phang stsol mdzad pa'i/ /rgyud sde'i lha tshogs kun la phyag 'tshal lo/ /mchog gi sprul pa'i mngon
rtogs lam byed cing / /mkha' khyab ting 'dzin bsam mi khyab pa'i 'phrul/ /rnal 'byor mchog gi rgyud du bsrel ba las/ /grub ster lhag pa'i lha la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thabs
dang shes rab zung 'jug rol par bcas/ /gang gis 'dul la de dang der ston pa'i/ /bla na med pa'i rgyud sde rgya mtsho yi/ /yi dam lha tshogs rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/
/rgyal bas ji ltar bsgos pa'i g.yar dam las/ /mi 'da' rdo rje'i rgyud kyi mdzod srung ba/ /dpal ldan nag po che sogs rgyud gsum gyi/ /dam chos skyong mdzad kun la'ang gus
btud nas/ /thugs rjes rdo rje 'chang gi skur bzhengs nas/ /thub pas rdo rje theg pa bstan pa'i gzhung / /mkhas rnams rdo rje'i gsung las nos pa'i tshul/ /'di na rdo rje'i
blo yis btu bar bya/ /zhes bsngags par 'os pa ji bzhin brjod pa'i me tog dkar po 'thor bas shis par byas te 'dir gleng bar bya ba/ nges pa'i don du gsang chen rdo rje theg
pa'i nye rgyu'i lam la

brten nas phyi nang gi mngon par byang chub pa lngas sgrib gnyis spangs shing / /sku dang ye shes gnyis su med par mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te bral smin gyi yon tan
bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i bdag nyid du bzhugs pa yin na'ang / /tshur mthong gdul bya'i snang ngor tshul khrims dang mang du thos shing bsam sgom rnam par dag pas ting nge
'dzin dang shes rab rdzogs te/ rang don phun sum tshogs shing / mdo sngags kyi lam 'chad pa dang / /rtsod pa dang / rtsom pa'i tshul la gzhan dring mi 'jog par rgyud dang
man ngag gi gnad mkhyen cing / zang zing med pa'i byams pa dang snying rje chen pos rgyud phyug pa/ /rdo rje slob ma'i rgyud byin gyis rlob pa dang smin grol la 'god pa'i
rdo rje slob dpon gyi mtshan nyid thams cad yongs su rdzogs shing nus pa mchog dang ldan pa bstan pa'i sgron me chen po dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo'i mgon po'i ngo bor bzhugs
pa rnams kyi zhal sgo nas theg chen mdo sde las khyad chos du ma'i sgo nas khyad par du 'phags pa/ bdag cag gi ston pa thugs rje can 'di nyid kyis bstan pa las gzhan
du 'byung dka' bas na sangs rgyas las kyang dkon pa'i rdo rje theg pa zhes bya ba/ gnas tha dad pa rnams su/ 'khor rig pa 'dzin pa mchog phal gyi gzugs bzung ba rnams la/
dus nges pa dang ma nges par/ gang zag rigs dang / dus/ nyon mongs la dgongs te/ rgyud sde chen po bzhis bsngas pa'i rdo rje theg pa'i lam rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod mtha'
klas pa bka' stsal pa/ rdo rje chos dang / rdo rje snying po dang / gsang ba'i bdag po la sogs pas bsdus shing / 'phags yul gyi paN grub rnams la rim par bka'

babs te/ bod gangs can gyi ljongs su skad gnyis smra ba'i dbang po rnams kyi bka' drin las bsgyur bshad 'chad nyan gyis gtan la phab pa'i smin grol deng dus 'dzam bu'i gling
'dir rgyun bzhugs so cog rtsol sgrub shugs chen pos nye bar bsags shing rang nyid la phyogs gcig tu zlum pa'i skal bzang bla na med par gyur pa de na'ang / brtan g.yo'i
dus kyi stobs las bshad sgrub kyi bgyi ba je phrar gyur pa'i dbang gis 'ga' zhig gi rgyun bag la zha bar phyogs pa na/ lhag bsam brtson pa'i stobs kyis 'thor ba rnams bsdus/
chad pa rnams bsabs/ mi gsal ba rnams gsal bar byas/ /'khrugs pa rnams legs par sbyar ba sogs kyi sgo nas thar 'dod kyi skye bo rdo rje theg pa don du gnyer ba dag gzhal
med khang du tshegs med par 'jug chog pa'i skal ba dge ba la sbyor ba'i skabs 'dir yid ches bskyed pa'i slad du so so'i brgyud khungs smos pa la/ spyir smin byed kyi
sngon du so byang gi sdom pas rgyud legs par bsdoms pa zhig byung na phun sum tshogs pa'i yan lag tsam du ma zad/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che 'jug pa'i go rim nges par
rjes su 'grub par 'gyur bas thog ma kho nar skyabs gsum 'dzin pa'i dge bsnyen nas brtsams te so sor thar pa ris bdun gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa nod/ de nas theg pa chen
por 'gyur ba'i slad du shing rta chen po'i srol gnyis las byon pa'i smon pa dang 'jug pa'i bdag nyid can gyi byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa'i cho ga rnam par dag pas
rgyud sbyangs pa la rdo rje theg pa chen po nas bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor chen por gzhug cing mngon par dbang bskur ba bsgrubs na bdag cag gi ston pa 'di nyid kyi bstan pa
la gya tshom du zhugs

pa'i nyes pas mi gos shing / dbang po'i spyod yul la mi ltos par lam la tshul bzhin du bslab pa zhes bya ba de'ang 'gyur ba'i phyir cis kyang 'os la/ rgyud sde rnams las kyang
de ltar bstan pa dang / rgyud sdom pa gsum dang ldan pa'i tha snyad kyang 'dis thob par 'gyur bas/ rdo rje 'dzin pa rab 'gring tha mar gsungs pa'i mchog rab tu'ang chud
pa'i phyir dbang bskur ba'i sngon du so byang gi sdom pa 'gro dgos pa rgyu mtshan de dag gi phyir don dang 'bras bu khyad par du 'dogs mod/ gal te yul dus gnas skabs kyis
sdom pa rim bzhin nod pa ma byung yang / gsang sngags dad pa'i lam gyi phyir na rdo rje theg pa nas bshad pa'i sdom pa dang dam tshig la gces sbras su cher byed pa rnams
kyang gcig tu rung zhing / thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa'i sdom pa 'bogs pa'i skabs de dang der ldan pa'i gang zag tu 'gyur la/ des so byang gi sdom pa dmigs bsal
ba'i dod kyang cho ga'i sgo nas nges par 'thus mod/ bsrung sdom ni gang gi skabs su'ang rang nyid kho na la rag las pa'i phyir 'phags bod kyi rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad
kyis don de la dgongs te mtha' gcig tu dogs pa ma mdzad pa de lta na'ang / deng gi dus su ni gong du bshad pa ltar bstan pa rin po che'i 'jug sgo dang mthun pa'i so so'i
cho ga las thob pa'i nges 'byung gis sdom par gnas pa gzhir bzhag nas/ bka' srol gnyis las byung ba'i byang chub sems bskyed kyi sdom pa la/ thog mar dpal mgon 'phags pa
klu sgrub dang / zhi ba lha sogs kyis bkral zhing / dpal ldan sa skya pas dar rgyas su mdzad pa'i dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed

sbyor ba yan lag bdun pas rgyud sbyangs nas/ dngos gzhi smon 'jug gnyis stabs gcig tu blangs te/ mjug rang gzhan gyi dga' ba bsgom pa dang / gtang rag gi mchod pa sogs tshang
phrugs su zhu chen rin po che dang / smin gling lo chen sogs kyi yig steng nas lan grangs su thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/thub dbang / 'jam dpal/ klu sgrub/ 'phags pa lha/ zla
grags/ slob pa'i rdo rje/ dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ bsod nams dpal/ ba ri lo tsA/ sa chen gong ma lnga/ 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston/ byang sems
rin chen mgon po/ rgyal sras thogs med dam/ yang na/ sa paN nas bo dong pa brtson 'grus rdo rje/ khro phu bsod nams seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ rgyal sras thogs med/
yang na/ sa paN nas 'phags pa rin po che/ rin chen dpal bzang / rin chen mgon po/ rgyal sras thogs med do/ /gang ltar yang de nas/ tshul khrims dpal/ gzhon nu rgyal mchog
dpal ldan grags pa/ rin chen grags pa/ sangs rgyas bkra shis/ dbang phyug dpal bzang / grags pa rgya mtsho/ ngag dbang chos grags/ lo pa spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ 'jam
mgon a mes zhabs/ mkhan chen blo gros brtan pa/ dol chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub/ gnas gsar ba ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa
chen kun dga' blo gros/ rje btsun ma 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma/ ngag dbang rdo rje rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'am/ yang na/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos
grags nas/ mkhan chen bsod nams bkra shis/ rje sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas

phun tshogs/ byang sems bkra shis bzang po/ zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen/ de'i dbon dge legs lhun grub/ ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phrin las/ byams pa bstan 'dzin snyan grags/
rdo rje 'chang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ gnyis kas bdag 'jam dbyangs blo gter dbang po'am/ theg mchog 'jam dbyangs blo gros chos
kyi nyi ma la bka' drin du stsal ba'o// !//bka' srol gnyis pa 'phags pa thogs med dang / mnyam med jo bo rje sogs kyis legs par bkral zhing / bka' gdams pa rnams kyis
phyag len du mdzad pa'i theg pa chen po shin tu rgyas pa'i mdo'i lugs kyi byang chub sems bskyed kyi sdom pa la/ sbyor ba yan lag bdun pas rgyud sbyangs nas/ dngos gzhi
smon 'jug so sor 'phral te len pa dang / gong 'og gi thog mtha' bar gsum du phyag len thun mong ma yin pa rang rang gi gzhung nas bshad pa ltar rje mkhyen brtse'i yig steng
nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/rnam 'dren thub pa'i dbang po/ rgyal tshab byams pa mgon po/ 'phags pa thogs med/ mkhas pa dbyig gnyen/ 'phags pa rnam grol sde/ btsun pa grol
ste/ mchog gi sde/ dul ba'i sde/ rnam par snang mdzad/ seng ge bzang po/ ku sA li che ba rin chen bzang po/ ku sA li chung ba rin chen 'or zer/ jo bo gser gling pa chen
po chos kyi grags pa/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha 'brom ston rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ spyan snga ba/ bya yul ba/ mus sman pa/ gro ston bdud rtsi grags/ sangs rgyas sgom
pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims ston/ seng ge skyabs/

bsod nams ye shes/ bsod nams grags pa/ rgyal sras thogs med/ sangs rgyas dpal/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ dpal ldan rdo rje/ rin chen tshul khrims/ sgo rum kun dga' legs
pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse/ dbang phyug rab brtan/ ngag dbang chos grags/ sa chen kun dga' bsod nams/ sa chen bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen don grub legs bzang / ngag
dbang kun dga' lhun grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs 'byung / sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ mus chen bsod nams dpal bzang / mus chen chos nyid ye shes/ ye shes rgyal mchog
blo gros rgya mtsho/ rdo rje rin chen nam/ yang na/ byang sems bsod nams grags pa nas/ bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen grub pa shes rab/
paN chen dge 'dun grub/ 'dul 'dzin blo gros sbas pa/ paN chen lung rig rgya mtsho/ rje skyabs mchog dpal bzang / dben sa ba blo bzang don grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas ye
shes/ paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ drung pa brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ rta phug pa dam chos rgyal mtshan/ sgrub khang dgelegs rgya mtsho/ phur bu cog ngag dbang
byams pa/ yongs 'dzin ye shes rgyal mtshan/ bshes gnyen blo bzang rgyal mtshan/ zhwa lu blo gsal bstan skyong / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'am/ blo gros rgya
mtsho dri ma med pa'i 'od/ des kun dga' 'jam dpal grags pa/ de gnyis kas bdag byang chub sems dpa' 'jam dbyangs blo gros chos kyi nyi ma la'o/ /yang na/ thogs med nas re
mda' ba gzhon nu blo gros/ shar tsong kha pa/ rtogs dan 'jam dpal rgya mtsho/ ba so chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ grub

chen chos kyi rdo rje/ dben sa ba blo bzang don grub man 'dra'o/ /de ltar na rgyud sdom pa gnyis dang ldan pa de nyid la de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba ma lus pa
gcig tu 'dus pa'i rdo rje rin po che'i za ma tog chen po rgyud sde rin po che kun las btus pa 'di nyid ston par byed pa la/ khams drug dang ldan pa'i rdo rje'i lus skyon
med pa nyid la 'bras bu sku bzhi la sogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sa bon 'debs pa'i phyir rgyud ma smin pa smin par byed pa'i thabs dbang / dbang las thob pa'i ye shes kyi rgyud
bskyang zhing gong nas gong du 'phel bas 'bras bu'i go 'phangs la sbyor bar byed pa'i thabs rim pa gnyis kyi lam zab mo yan lag dang bcas pa'i khrid/ de dag kyang sgra
dang yi ge lhan cig byed rkyen la ltos pa'i slob ma rnams kyis chos la dbang za mi dgos par ji dgar spyad chog pa'i lung / gang las 'phro ba'i gzhi'am 'byung gnas rdo
rje 'chang chen po'i gsung rdo rje 'chang gi rgyud sde rnams la khungs gtugs te nges shes mi 'phrogs par ster zhing / rnam gzhag thams cad khong du chud pa'i slad du rgyab
brten rgyud kyi bshad bka' ste bzhi las/ dang po smin byed kyi skor la'ang zur bka' so sor phye ba dang / spyi bka' bsdoms su smos pa gnyis/ dang po la'ang rgyud sde dngos
dang / gdams ngag las byung ba gnyis las/ dang po rgyud sde chen po bzhi'i bzhugs tshul/ rdo rje'i slob ma rig pa 'dzin pa rnams ji ltar 'jug pa'i go rim/ rigs thams
cad kyi khyab byed du gyur pa sogs bya ba'i rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor chen po nas rim gyis bla med gsang mtha' zab pa'i gnyis med kyi mthar thug par 'chad par 'dod de/ de la
rgyud sde chen po bzhi las/ thog

mar rig sngags 'chang gi sde snod thams cad kyi rtsa bar gyur pa bya ba'i rgyud kyi mtshan nyid ni/ bltas pas bde ba lam du byas nas yid mtshan ma rtog las bde myur gyis skyob
par byed pa'i thabs 'khor dang bcas pa'o/ nges tshig gam sgra don ni/ kr-i ya taTatar zhes pa'i sgra las drangs na/ phyi lus ngag gi bya ba khrus dang gtsang sbra gtso
bor ston pas na de skad ces bya'o/ dbye na bya ba spyi dang so so'i rgyud gnyis las/ dang po la'ang spyod pa bzhi po'i don 'dus shing ma tshang ba med par ston pa dpung
pa bzang po'i rgyud/ 'jug pa'i spyod pa smin byed gtso bor ston pa gsang ba spyi'i rgyud/ sbyor ba'i spyod pa lha'i rnal 'byor gtso bor ston pa legs par grub pa'i rgyud/
sgrub pa'i spyod pa mtshan med kyi rnal 'byor gtso bor ston pa bsam gtan phyi ma'i rgyud de bzhi yod pa las/da lan 'dir thog mar dge ba'i dbang du btang nas dkyil 'khor
chen po bkod pa'i rgyud dam/ gsang ba spyi rgyud kyi rjes su 'brangs nas grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po kha che ye shes rdo rjes cho ga'i yan lag 'ga' zhig spyod rgyud dang
mthun par bkral ba'i bcom ldan 'das rigs gsum spyi'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/rgyal ba
rdo rje 'chang chen po/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po indra bhu ti/ ma dhyi ma/ mr-i tyu/ slob dpon 'phags pa klu sgrub/ slob dpon klu'i byang chub kha che ye shes
rdo rje/ lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po cha e bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya
paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis ka las dol pa dkar ston shAkya grags/

de nas bde lung ba kun bzang dpal 'byor/ gung pa dar ma ye shes/ snar thang pa bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ snar thang pa bla ma tshul khrims rgyal ba/ bla ma ngag dbang
mtshan can/ gnyags ston byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug/ yongs 'dzin
dkon mchog 'phel ba/ lha mchog seng ge/ sangs rgyas seng ge/ thar paN nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang pa dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen
lhun grub dpal ldan/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ rje bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ thar rje nam mkhar bsam 'grub/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med/
byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ rje bla ma mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ kun dga' 'jam dpal grags pa/ de gnyis kas bdag 'jam dbyangs blo gter dbang por ram/ yang na/ byams
pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin nas/ mkhas grub kun dga' dpal ldan/ ngor mkhyen rab nga drug pa rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ thub bstan legs bshad bzang po/ des
so////gnyis pa da lan 'dir bar du dge ba'am so so'i rgyud la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi rgyud/ padma'i rigs kyi rgyud/ rdo rje'i rigs kye rgyud/ lngas rtsen gyi rigs
kyi rgyud/ nor bu'i rigs kyi rgyud/ 'jig rten pa'i rigs kyi rgyud dang drug dang po la'ang / rigs kyi gtso bo/ bdag po/ yum/ gtsug tor/ khro bo khro mo/ pho nya sogs drug
las/ dang po la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo thul ba dam tshig sum bkod lha lnga'i

dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba sngags chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ston pa shAkya'i rgyal po/ 'phags pa kun dga' bo/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/
a wa dhU ti pa/ 'jigs med 'byung gnas/ gser gling pa chos kyi grags pa/ jo bo rje dI paM ka ra/ 'brom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas/ po to ba rin chen gsal/ shar pa yon tan
grags/ rgya dpe sgom pa/ grub thob hU 'bar/ zhang rin chen ye shes/ 'khon ston gzhon nu/ tang pa dkon mchog 'bar/ mkhan po dbang phyug rin chen/ khams pa sa phug pa shA
kya rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba gzhon nu 'od/ don ri grags chen pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ gzhon nu tshul khrims/ sngags 'chang tshul khrims
rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' smon lam/ lo grags chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ stag lung ngag dbang grags pa/ rje rnam rgyal grags pa/ tshul khrims mchog grub/ stag lung rnam rgyal bkra
shis/ jo nang kun dga' snying po'am tA ra nA tha/ rgyud chen sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ sngags chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ paN
chen blo bzang ye shes/ bya btang ye shes bstan 'dzin/ kun spangs ye shes dpal 'byor/ yongs 'dzin blo bzang bzod pa/ paN chen dpal ldan ye shes/ yongs 'dzin blo bzang bstan
'dzin/ paN chen bstan pa'i nyi ma/ spang lung ngag dbang chos 'dzin/ sog po tho yon bla ma lha btsun ye shes don grub rgyal mtshan/ kun gzigs 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang po/ des bdag blo gter dbang po la'o/ /yang na/ thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs/ rab gsal zla ba/ ye shes

rdo rje/ kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA bo dhi/ mukti ko Sha/ shraddhA ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ sum ston ye shes 'bar/ 'or ston lha
dbang / 'or ston sangs rgyas 'bar/ lho pa ting 'dzin bzang po/ rje chos kyi seng ge rje chos kyi mgon po/ dbus pa bla ma sangs rgyas 'bum/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog legs
blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge/ bu ston rin chen grub/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ /lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/ bo dong paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal/ rje 'jam
dbyangs grags pa/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog/ chos sku lha dbang grags pa/ jo nang kun dga' snying po man gong ltar ro// //ston mchog nyi ma'i gnyen gyi bka' mdo brgyad
brgya pa la brten nas slob dpon zhi ba 'tshos bkral ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo bder gshegs sman lha mched brgyad lha zhe bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang
bskur ba 'khon ston bsod nams dpal 'byor lhun grub kyi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston mchog thub pa'i dbang po shAkya seng ge 'phags pa 'jam dpal dbyangs/
mkhan chen po bo dhi sa twa'am zhi ba 'tsho/ chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan/ chos rgyal sad na legs 'jing yon/ mnga' bdag khri ral pa can/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje/
mnga' bdag 'od srung / khri dpal 'khor btsan/ skyid lde nyi ma mgon/ mnga' bdag bkra shis lde/ lha bla ma ye shes 'od/ mnga' bdag lha lde'am lha btsun byang chub 'od/ mnga'
bdag 'od lde/ mnga' bdag rtse lde/ mnga' ris dgra bcom byang chub tshul khrims/ zhu lhan pa shes rab

grags pa/ ra sa chu lhad pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ gro mo che'am gro ston bdud rtsi grags/ sangs rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ dgra bcom gzhon nu/ bla
ma 'dul mdzad pa/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs/ dbang ston rgyal mtshan dpal/ 'dul nag pa dpal ldan bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs dge 'dun 'phel/ rgyud chen bkra shis 'phags/ rgyud chen
brtson 'grus 'phags/ sras khang bzang po rnam rgyal/ 'khon ston dpal 'byor lhun grub/ zur chos dbyings rang grol lam dpal 'byor phrin las rab rgyas/ rgyal dbang lnga pa
chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ rdor brag pa padma phrin las/ ho ra tshang 'jigs med rig pa'i seng ge/ ha la ha slob dpon blo bzang rab rgyas/ rje tshe ring rdo
rje/ rab 'byams pa grags pa lhun grub/ er ti ni ngag dbang blo bzang don grub/ tho yon bla ma lha btsun don grub rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag
blo gter dbang po la'o/ /yang na/ mkhan chen bo dhi sa twa nas/ de'i dbon bo dhi satwa chung ba/ za hor rgyal po dge ba dpal/ mnyam med jo bo chen po mar me mdzad/ lha
btsun byang chub 'od/ mnga' bdag 'od lde man 'dra'o// //de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtso bo 'od zer dri ma med pa rnam par dag pa'i 'od kyi gzungs la gtso bor brten nas
slob dpon zhi ba 'tsho sogs kyis bkral ba'i 'phags pa 'od zer dri med lha drug gi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong gi yig steng nas thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun 'phags pa 'jam dpal/ mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho

chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan/ lha sras mu ne btsad po/ lha sras sad na legs 'jing yon/ lha sras gtsad ma khri ral pa can/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje/ mnga' bdag 'od srung
/ mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan/ skyid lde nyi ma mgon/ khri lde bkra shis mgon/ lha bla ma ye shes 'od/ lha btsun byang chub 'od/ pho brang zhi ba 'od/ mnga' bdag 'od sde/
mnga' bdag rtse lde/ mnga' ris dgra bcom byang chub tshul khrims/ zhu lhan pa shes rab grags/ ra sa chu lhad pa dar ma rgyal mtshan/ gro mo che ba bdud rtsi grags/ sangs
rgyas sgom pa seng ge skyabs/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ tshad pa'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon po/ kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/
sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub/ sngags 'chang rin chen don grub legs pa/ 'khrul zhig tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ byang gling pa rin chen rgyal po/
dge bshes rin chen bkra shis/ gnubs ston spas pa'i rnal 'byor smon lam rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ zhwa lu mkhan
chen rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ bla chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ byang gling pa 'jam dpal tshul khrims/ lce btsun bstan 'dzin phrin las/ rin chen skal bzang / byang
gling pa rin chen lhun grub/ zhwa lu rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong / kun mkhyen 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ zhwa lu mkhan
chen nas/ zhwa lu rin chen bzang po/ lo chen ngag dbang chos dpal/ rgyal sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rab 'byams pa 'gyur med bslab gsum/ tshe dbang

rig 'dzin bzang po/ 'gyur med mthu stobs rnam rgyal/ rdo rje 'chang chen po 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des so/ yang na/ mkhan chen zhi ba 'tsho/ rgyal po dge ba
dpal/ jo bo a ti sha nag tsho tshul khrims rgyal ba/ rong pa phyag sor ba shes rab 'bar 'phan yul gong kha pa/ shangs kyi rgya phug pa can/ g.yag sde'i zhang ye shes rgyal
mtshan/ slob dpon dbang phyug rin chen/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston rin chen grub man 'dra'o/ yang na/
mchims nam mkha' grags nas/ bla ma mkhan zi pa/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston man 'dra'o/ dbang gi brgyud pa ni jo lugs 'di gtso che'o// //de bzhin gshegs pa'i
rigs kyi yum srung ba lha lnga'i gzungs la brten nas dzai tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas bkral ba'i srung ba lha lnga gtso bor bzhugs pa'i lha lnga bcu rtsa drug gi dkyil
'khor du dbang bskur ba zhwa lu blo gsal bstan skyong gi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ dzai tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/
rdo rje gdan pa che ba mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ chung ba don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ dpal sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po
che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya pa paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ chos rgyal 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ dga' ldan
pa bkra shis dpal/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ de gnyis ka las sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub/ dka' bzhi pa rin chen
rgyal mtshan/ rin chen mkhyen rab mchog grub/ sku zhang

bsod nams mchog grub/ byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ thar gling 'og pa bsod nams dpal 'byor/ ri phug dbu mdzad rin chen rgya mtsho/ zhwa lu mkhan chen rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub/ chen po rin chen bzang po/ khri zur bkra shis don grub/ gong dkar ba chos dbang rgya mtsho/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ thar rtse nam mkha' 'chi med/ rnam
'dren kun dga' ye shes/ des thar rtse byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin dang / rdor 'dzin dpal ldan phrin las gnyis/ gnyis kas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ 'khor lo'i
mgon po kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ phyi ma gnyis kas bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/
gnyen ston grags pa/ gnyen rin chen ldan/ lha sa'i gnas brtan dkon mchog seng ge sras rngog ston byang chub rgyal po/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug rong
pa sher ser/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ thugs sras/ nam mkha' mchog grub/ rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ shAkya don grub/ kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba rab
mdzosamadzes zla ba/ mchog legs rdo rje/ bstan 'dzin bzang po/ ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor chen/ gnas gsar ba/ kun blo man 'dra'o/ yang na/ byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal
mtshan las/ rje dbang phyug rab brtan gyis lan brgyar gsan/ de nas 'jam dbyangs chos skyong dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rin chen/ chos lung mkhan chen don yod rgyal
mtshan/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ thar rtse nam mkha' 'chi med man 'dra/ yang na/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub nas/ rdo ring kun dga' rgyal mtshan

tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse/ dbang rab/ mkhan chen bsod nams mchog grub man 'dra/ yang na/ bu ston nas/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma don yod pa/ bsod nams rin chen/ don
yod rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' blo gros/ bshes gnyen bkra shis/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug man 'dra'o// //de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi yum
gza' thams cad kyi yum gyi gzungs la brten nas slob dpon bi rwa pas bkral zhing / paNDi ta zhi ba 'tsho nas 'khon klu dbang srung ba sogs 'khon gong mar bka' babs pa'i
rje btsun rig pa chen mo lha bcu bzhi rgyal chen bzhi dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba rje ngag dbang legs grub kyi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug bi rU pa/ mkhan chen bo dhi sa twa'am zhi ba 'tsho/ 'khon klu dbang srung ba/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen/ 'khon shes rab yon tan/
'khon tshul khrims rgyal po/ 'khon rdo rje gtsug tor/ 'khon dge skyabs/ 'khon dge mthong / 'khon bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo gros/ 'khon shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog
rgyal po/ 'khon brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtsortse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/
'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ bla ma e pa 'jam dbyangs/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul
khrims rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' 'od zer/ stag tshang lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/

mkhan chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ 'bras spungs tshe dbang bkra shis/ bla ma o rgyan rgyal po/ mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal po/ nyi ma gling pa tshul khrims bkra shis/ chos rje
dge ba'i dbang po/ rje phrin las rnam rgyal/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rje rin chen rgya mtsho/ grwa thang mkhan chen snyan mkhar ba/ 'bras gling ngag dbang kun dga'
chos dar/ de'i dbon kun dga' bstan dar/ yangs pa can kun dga' dbang rgyal/ po ta la'i gong dkar mkhan chen bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ tho yon lha btsun don grub rgyal mtshan/
de gnyis kas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ rje kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ de gnyis kas bdag blo gter ba'o/ /yang phye 'gyur ltar na/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo
rje/ dzai tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ sa chen man sngar ltar ro// //rigs kyi gtsug tor gdugs dkar po can gyi gzungs la brten
nas grub dbang dzai tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal gyis bkral ba'i gdugs dkar po can lha nyer bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba shAkya dpal gyi dkyil chog bsod nams mchog
grub kyi lhan thabs/ blo gsal zhabs kyi dbang chog bcas pa'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thub pa'i dbang po/ gtsug tor gdugs dkar can/
phyag na rdo rje/ bsam gtan bcu pa/ tsandra go mI/ gi ra wa ti/ rdo rje rnon po/ padma lcags kyu/ bram ze rin chen rdo rje/ dzai tA ri pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/
ba ri lo tsA ba/ 'dan ma kyur a skyabs/ sa chen kun snying / slob dpon bsod rtse/ rje btsun

grags rgyam/ des stod lung gang ser ba dang / pho rog mdo sde mgon gnyis/ gnyis kas rgan mo lhas pa byang chub dpal/ bla ma ye shes rin chen/ bla ma rin chen rgyal mtshan/
bla ma cha gan pa/ bla ma grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od yon rgyam/ bu ston rin chen grub/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ shAkya dpal ba/ dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rgyal mtshan bkra shis/
dbang chen rgyal po/ byang chub bzang po/ rin chen kun ldan/ kun dga' don grub/ kun dga' 'byung gnas/ bsod nams mchog grub/ rje bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho/ bstan pa rgyal mtshan
yang 'dug blo gros dbang phyug chos dbang rgya mtsho/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ mi nyag pa ri khug sprul sku kun dga' mkhas grub dbang po/ byams pa kun dga' bstan
'dzin/ rdo rje 'chang mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ ngor mkhan chen dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /nye brgyud ni/ gdugs dkar nas/ shAkya dpal ba man
'dra'o// //gshegs rigs kyi gtsug tor gzhan gyis mi thub pa mchog tu grub pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs la brten nas grub pa'i slob dpon shrA rig warma dang / ghi ti wa ta bi ma
la mi tra sogs kyis bkral ba'i gdugs dkar po can lha bcu bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gyi sgrub dkyil steng nas thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ kun dga' 'byung gnas yan gdugs dkar lha nyer bdun ma ltar la/ de nas/ blo mchog rdo rje/ bsod nams mchog ldan/ rgyal dbang lnga pa/ phrin las rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang
bstan 'dzin phrin las/ khri byang chub chos 'phel/ rgyud stod blo bzang dar rgyas/ brag yab gdong kaM rdo rje 'dzin pa ngag dbang dam chos rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter
la'o// //

de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi gtsug tor kun nas sgor 'jug pa 'od zer gtsug tor dri ma med par snang ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs la brten nas mnyam med jo bo chen pos bkral ba'i
gtsug tor dri med lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba ngag dbang legs grub kyi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ mnyam med jo bo chen po mar
me mdzad/ nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba/ rong pa phyag sor ba shes rab 'bar/ bya yul ba gzhon nu 'od/ skar chung sbyin pa/ gze pa don grub ye shes/ khams pa shAkya
rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon po/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ mes ston grags pa 'od zer/ bla chen
grags pa rin chen/ kun mkhyen nam mkha' 'od zer/ chos rje nam mkha' tshul khrims/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ rdo ring pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya
mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ chen po bsod nams rgya mtsho/ thar gling 'jam dpal tshul khrims/
byang gling smon lam bsam gtan/ byang gling rin chen skal bzang / byang gling rin chen lhun grub/ zhwa lu ri phug sprul sku blo gsal bstan skyong rje 'jam dbyangs mkhyen
brtse'i dbang po/ ngor zhabs drung 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub nas/ chen po rin chen bzang po/
lo chen ngag dbang chos dpal rgya mtsho/ 'gyur med rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'gyur med bslab gsum/ mkhan chen rig 'dzin bzang po/ 'gyur med mthu stobs

rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ des so// //padma'i rigs kyi nang tshan mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa'i gzungs dang tshe
mdo oM gnyis ma la brten nas slob dpon dzai tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas bkral ba'i bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag tu med pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dkon
mchog lhun grub kyi sgrub dkyil dang / zhu chen gyi mtshams sbyor bcas pa'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba tshe dpag med mgon/ slob dpon snying po'i zhabs/ dzai
tA ri ste dgra las rnam rgyal/ slob dpon byang chub bzang po/ slob dpon ting 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ sa chen kun
dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ bla ma bkra shis 'od/ e pa 'khon ston
thugs rje rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ spang khang pa grags pa dpal/ spro lung pa kun dga' smon lam/ brag phug pa bsod nams
dpal/ mtshungs med blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ gnyis
kas rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug dkon mchog 'phel/ lha mchog seng ge sangs rgyas seng ge thar paN nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub/ de
gnyis kas nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ des hor nam mkha' dpal bzang dang / thar rtse nam mkha' rin chen gnyis/ gnyis kas shes rab rgya mtsho/ de gnyis kas mkhan chen

sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ des tshul khrims lhun grub dang / bsod nams dpal ldan gnyis/ gnyis kas thar rtse nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ byams pa nam mkha'
'chi med/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ dpon slob shes rab rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gtar la'o/ /yang na/ dkon mchog 'phel nas/ sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo kun dga' bsod
nams/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen/ de sras bsod nams dbang po/ grags pa blo gros mched/ de sras a mes zhabs kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras bsod nams dbang phyug de sras
kun dga' bkra shis/ de sras bsod nams rin chen/ de sras kun dga' blo gros/ de sras dbang sdud snying po'am dpal ldan chos skyong / yongs 'dzin kun dga' bkra shis/ dbang
sdud snying po'i sras kun dga' rin chen/ de gnyis kas ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis sam padma bdud 'dul dbang phyug mched/ des snga ma'i sras ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams
dang / ri khug dbon po byams pa kun dga' bstan skyong dang / ri khug sprul sku byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i nyi ma gsum/ gsum gas rje byams pa kun dga' lhun grub/ des
thub bstan legs bshad bzang po/ des so/ /yang na/ kun dga' rin chen sras ngag dbang rdo rje rin chen/ de'i lce rje btsun ma skal bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ thub bstan legs bshad
bzang po/ des so/ yang na/ thar paN nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ sgrub khang dpal ldan don grub/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ lnga pa blo bzang rgya mtsho/ rje bzang po
sbyin pa/ rje blo bzang rin chen/ khri chen ngag dbang mchog ldan/ rgyal ba skal bzang

rgya mtsho/ paN chen dpal ldan ye shes/ yongs 'dzin blo bzang bstan 'dzin/ paN chen bstan pa'i nyi ma/ rgyud smad mkhan chen grags pa brtson 'grus/ lha btsun don grub rgyal
mtshan/ dge bshes 'jam dbyangs phrin las/ rje blo bzang mkhyen rab dpal 'bar/ rje thub bstan legs bshad bzang po/ des so/ /yang na/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/ sangs rgyas
bstan 'dzin/ bkra shis lhun grub/ sangs rgyas ye shes/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros man 'dra'o/ /yang na/ ba ri lo tsA nas/ rgya zhang phug pa/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/
bla ma cha gan pa/ spang khang grags pa dpal man 'dra/ yang na/ rgya zhang phug pa nas/ 'jad pa rin chen shes rab/ e pa 'khon ston/ shar pa 'jam dbyangs/ rin chen rgyal
mtshan/ rgyal ba ye shes/ spang khang grags pa dpal/ snur tshos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ shar
chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po man 'dra/ yang na/ brag phug pa nas/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ sa bzang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ theg chen
kun dga' bkra shis/ kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan chos grags/ mus sras pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ rgya gar ba shes rab rgyal mtshan/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ des sngags
'chang kun dga' rin chen dang / kun dga' dpal ldan gnyis/ gnyis kas thar paN man 'dra'o// //padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo 'chi med rnga sgra'i gzungs la brten nas slob dpon
dzai tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas bkral ba'i bcom ldan 'das 'chi med rnga sgra lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thar rtse paN chen gyi sgrub dkyil gyi tho yig
steng nas

thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ba ri lo tsA yan tshe dpag med lha dgu ltar la/ de nas/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge rgya ston zhang phug pa/ 'jad pa shes rab rin chen/ e pa 'khon ston/
shar pa 'jam dbyangs/ gzhi thog pa rin chen rgyal mtshan byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ spang khang pa grags pa dpal/ snur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ yang rtse ba rin chen
seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ gnyis kas sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub/ rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub/ lo chen chos skyong bzang po/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ dbon dkon mchog dpal ldan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / sngags 'chang
grags pa blo gros/ a mes zhabs 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams/ shar pa ye shes bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ shar chen blo gros grags pa/ thar rtse nam
mkha' bsam 'grub/ ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros/ byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter la'o//
//padma'i rigs kyi gtso bo 'chi med rnga sgra'i gzungs la brten nas slob dpon snying po'i zhabs kyis bkral ba'i bcom ldan 'das 'chi med mgon po lha bcu bdun ma'i dkyil
'khor du dbang bskur ba rje grol mchog zhabs kyi sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub yan rnga sgra lha dgu ltar la/ de nas/ 'brog
khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ rin chen rgya mtsho/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal

ldan chos bzang / rje btsun tA ra TA tha/ rgyal tshab ye shes rgya mtsho/ rin chen rgya mtsho/ blo gros rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang phrin las/ kun bzang dbang po/ rig 'dzin tshe
dbang nor bu/ si tu chos kyi 'byung gnas/ karma tshe dbang kun khyab/ mchog sprul karma rin chen/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/
des bdag blo gter la'o// //padma'i rigs kyi bdag po don yod zhags pa'i rgyud la brten nas slob dpon i ra ba tis bkral ba 'don yod zhags pa lha nyer brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor
du dbang bskur ba kun mkhyen bu ston rin po che'i dkyil chog byang gling pa'i lhan thabs/ blo gsal zhabs kyi dbang chog bcas pa'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo
rje 'chang chen/ jo bo spyan ras gzigs/ slob dpon e ra ba ti/ lho phyogs rigs ngan gyi rnal 'byor pa/ rdo rje gdan pa don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags/ des
bla ma lho pa/ mkhan po thang pa/ snur chos 'phags gsum la gnang / gsum gas nyi phug pa chos grags/ grang pho lung pa grags pa tshul khrims/ slob dpon tshul khrims grags
pa/ kun rab bsod nams rgyal mtshan mgon/ slob dpon bsod nams grub pa/ slob dpon kun dga' tshul khrims/ chos lung byang sems bsod nams grags pa/ bu ston rin chen grub/ slob
dpon gzhon nu 'bum/ mtshams pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams 'phel ba/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal
mtshan/ byang gling pa bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ rje dpal ldan chos bzang / lha bo rin chen rgya mtsho/ zhwa lu bsod nams mchog grub/ dkar po chos rje klu sgrub rgyal mtshan/
byang gling pa smon lam lhun grub

byang gling pa rin chen brtson 'grus/ 'jam dpal chos mchog rje gsung rab rgya mtsho/ rje byams pa chos 'phel/ byang gling pa ye shes dpal 'byor/ zhwa lu blo gsal bstan skyong
/ rje mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ rje kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ yang na/ grags pa tshul khrims nas/ dkon mchog grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs rgyal mtshan/ mkhan
chen klu sgrub/ grags pa gzhon nu/ chos lung byang sems bsod nams grags pa man 'dra/ yang na/ gsung rab rgya mtsho nas/ dge 'dun tshangs dbyangs/ legs bshad chos 'phel/
rin chen lhun grub/ blo gsal bstan skyong man 'dra/ yang na/ spyan ras gzigs/ shI la ka ra/ bai ro tsa na ra kShi ta/ ba ri rin chen grags man 'dra/ yang na/ spyan ras
gzigs/ dharma ka pA la/ ma hA pu Nyai/ don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA man 'dra/ yang na/ spyan ras gzigs/ skal ldan byang sems/ paNDi ta shrI dha na/ byang sems zla ba rgyal
mtshan/ nyi phug pa chos kyi grags pa/ grags pa tshul khrims/ 'gro ba'i mgon po/ mchims ston chen po/ bsod nams ye shes/ grags pa gzhon nu/ bsod nams grags pa/ gnyis
kas bu ston man 'dra'o// //padma'i rigs kyi bdag po 'phags pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi gzungs la brten nas 'phags pa klu sgrub zhabs kyis bkral ba'i spyan ras gzigs bcu
gcig zhal lha so bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge'i sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'phags
pa spyan ras gzigs/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ 'phags pa lha/ zla ba grags pa/ rig pa'i khu byug a wa dhU ti pa/ ku

sA li che ba rin chen bzang po/ chung ba rin chen 'od zer/ dpal ldan a ti sha 'brom ston pa/ spyan snga pa tshul khrims 'bar/ bya yul ba gzhon nu 'od/ bshes gnyen mus sman
pa/ phyar chen pa/ dpal ldan gro mo che bdud rtsi grags/ stag lo shes rab 'od zer/ rgya ston bsod nams 'od zer/ dmar ston bsod nams 'phel/ mkhan chen grags pa 'bum/ don mo
ri pa sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen grags pa tshul khrims/ mkhan rgyal ba bzang po/ mkhas btsun byang chub seng ge 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang
/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ rin chen mkhyen rab mchog grub/ kun mkhyen shAkya don grub/ dbon kun dga' legs grub/ she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags/ ngag dbang
mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ de'i dbon mkhyen brtse rab brtan/ mchod dpon kun dga' rab brtan/ lho drung kun dga'
rin chen/ chos rje tshul khrims dbang phyug zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen/ zhu dbon dge legs lhun grub/ rje dpal ldan phrin las/ bla ma dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ byams pa kun
dga' bstan 'dzin/ thar rtse zhabs drung 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ grags pa tshul khrims nas/ nam mkha' 'od zer/ dus zhabs pa
kun dga' don grub/ spyan snga ba bsod nams lha dbang / spyan snga ba bag dbang chos grags/ she'u lo tsA ba kun dga' chos grags man 'dra'o// //rdo rje'i rigs kyi gtso bo
'phags pa las kyi sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba'i gzungs la brten nas dzai tA ri dgra las rnam par rgyal bas bkral ba'i rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa lha dgu'i dkyil

'khor du dbang bskur ba dkon mchog lhun grub kyi sgrub dkyil dbang chog dang bcas pa'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs/
ye shes snying po/ ye shes zhi ba/ sangs rgyas zhi ba/ sangs rgyas gsang ba/ ku sA li che ba rin chen bzang po/ chung ba rin chen 'od zer ram dge ba can/ gser gling
pa chos kyi grags pa/ dpal ldan a ti sha go mI sgom chen/ dznyA na shrI/ nyag ston lom bu ba/ sbrug ston grags pa/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bya ston rin chen 'od zer/ glo
chen sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can ba ye shes mgon po/ seng ge rgyal mtshan/ bra 'or mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ lo tsA ba nor dpal ye shes/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo
gros/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis kas rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ sa lo kun dga'
bsod nams/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / sgrub khang dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung
gnas/ shar chen ye shes bzang po/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mkhan chen bsod nams dpal ldan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ byams
pa nam mkha' 'chi med/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ sprul sku shes rab rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ jo bo rje nas/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa skya gong ma rnam
lnga/ snor ye shes rgyal mtshan/ snur chos 'phags/ gar thig pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje man 'dra/ yang na/ rdo rje

'chang / 'jam dpal/ dzai tA ri/ ye shes rdo rje/ lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ sa skya gong ma rnam lnga man 'dra/ yang na/ dkon mchog 'phel nas/ kun dga' mchog ldan/ lha
mchog seng ge gnyis kas sangs rgyas seng ge/ nam mkha' dpal bzang / ratnA rtha sidha shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas man 'dra'o// //'phags pa las kyi sgrib pa rnam par sbyong
ba'i gzungs la brten nas mnyam med jo bo chen po'i bka' srol las byung ba'i bcom ldan 'das rdo rje mi 'khrugs pa mchog gi sprul sku gtso bor bzhugs pa'i lha dgu'i dkyil
'khor du dbang bskur ba rje dbang phyug rdo rje'am chos dbang phyug gi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ kun dga' bo/ 'di la 'jam dpal yod pa'ang
'dug klu sgrub/ A RYa de wa/ a wa dhU ti pa/ a bhyA ka ra/ gseng gling pa chos kyi grags pa/ jo bo rje/ 'brom ston pa/ po to ba rin chen gsal/ shar ba yon tan grags/ rgya
ye shes sgom pa/ grub thob hU 'bar/ zhang dge slong / dkon mchog ye shes/ bla ma 'khun ston/ rong pa dkon mchog 'bar/ g.yag sde dbang phyug rin chen/ shAkya rdo rje dbus
pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma chos 'od/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ zhwa lu zla ba dpal/ rje mthong ba don ldan/
ban sgar 'jam dpal bzang po/ rje chos grags rgya mtsho/ sangs rgyas gnyan pa grub chen/ karma phrin las mi bskyod rdo rje/ dkon mchog yan lag dbang phyug rdo rje/ chos kyi
dbang phyug karma nyi ma/ karma phrin las/ ku shrI don yod snying po/ chos kyi don grub/ si tu bstan pa'i nyin byed/ rje bdud 'dul rdo rje/ si tu padma nyin byed/ ngag
dbang yon nyan rgya mtsho/ thub bstan legs

bshad bzang po/ des bdag bla gter la'o// //rdo rje'i rigs kyi khro bo rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs la brten nas slob dpon sa wA ri pas bkral ba'i bcom ldan 'das rdo rje
rnam par 'joms pa dkar po lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba zhwa lu pa'i yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i gdong
can/ grub chen sa wA ri pa/ grub chen dza wA ri pa/ paNDi ta de ba pu tyai ma ti/ mgar lo tsA ba chos bzang / gshis ston rin chen grub/ dmar ston chos kyi rgyal mtshan/
sgang ston shes rab bla ma/ sgang ston shes rab 'bum/ grags pa rdo rje/ dar ma byang chub/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge kun mkhyen bu ston/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub bsod nams chos 'phel/ byang sems rin chen chos dpal/ mkhan chen rig 'dzin rgyal po/ bla chen chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bsod nams
dpal 'byor/ byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ chen po bsod
nams rgya mtsho/ dge slong 'jam dpal blo 'phel/ mtshungs med 'jam dbyangs chos mchog grub dbang byams pa rgyal po/ rje gsung rab rgya mtsho/ byang gling byams pa chos 'phel/
grub dbang ye shes dpal 'byor/ rin chen blo gsal brtan skyong / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan
nas/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub

dge slong phrin las rnam rgyal/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub man 'dra/ yang na/ mus chen nam dpal nas/ ngor nam mkha' dpal ldan/ rin chen bsod mchog man 'dra'o// //rdo rje'i
rigs kyi khro bo rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa'i gzungs la brten nas slob dpon sa wA ri pas bkral ba'i rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa khro nag lha bco lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang
bskur ba 'brug pa pad dkar gyi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa/ ganggA dha ra/ ma Ni ka badzra/ dza ya warma/ dharma shrI/
sa wA ri pa/ bal po de wa pU rNa ma ti/ lo tsA ba chos bzang / rin chen dngos grub/ skyi ston/ kre ston/ dam pa grub shes/ ye ston padma can/ jo btsun pa mdo sde 'bum/
go lung mdo sde dpal/ grub chen o rgyan pa/ rje chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ gar thig pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ thel mkhan po shes rab rdo rje/ chos dpal shes rab/ grags pa
rdo rje/ grags pa don grub/ rngog rin chen byang chub dpal/ rngog byang chub dpal grub/ dge slong rin chen rnam rgyal/ rje 'jam dbyangs grags pa/ rnam 'joms rjes bzung ye
shes mthu stobs/ kun mkhyen ngag dbang nor bu/ lha rtse ba ngag dbang bzang po/ kun mkhyen dpag bsam dbang po/ yongs 'dzin kun dga' lhun grub/ mi phab chos kyi dbang phyug
rje thugs kyi rdo rje/ chos rgyal rgya mtsho/ yongs 'dzin 'jam dpal dpa' bo/ kun gzigs chos kyi snang ba/ yongs 'dzin ye shes dbang po/ 'brug pa thams cad mkhyen pa mi
'gyur 'jigs med grub pa/ lha btsun don grub rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //

slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba dang kha chen dznyA na shrI nas brgyud de grub chen las kyi rdo rje sogs kyis dar rgyas su mdzad pa'i snor lugs rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa mthing
nag rdo rje pho nya mo drug cu rtsa bzhi dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba lho brag grub chen gyi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / byams
pa/ ganggA dha ra/ sangs rgyas gsang ba/ sa manta bhadra/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ shu gnyan stong legs/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ gnyal nyi ma shes rab/ snur chen po nyi ma
'od zer/ snur rdo rje seng ge snur byang chub 'od/ snur nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ snur ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ri zangs rdog po ye shes mdzes/ seng ge bzang po/ rgyal sras bzang
po/ grub chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rje tsong kha pa/ gnyal gong snang chos rjes mdzes pa dpal ldan bzang po/ blo gros mchog ldan mdzes pa/ seng ge dpal ldan mdzes pa/
nam mkha' mdzes pa/ nam mkha' chos bzang / nam mkha' 'od mdzes/ lhun grub dpal mdzes/ nam mkha' mdzes pa dpal/ bsod nams 'od mdzes/ don yod mdzes pa/ shes rab 'od mdzes/
nyi zla 'od mdzes/ mgon po mdzes pa'i rdo rje/ mdzes pa'i dbang phyug grub dbang 'phags pa bstan dar/ bsod nams lung rigs/ chu bar sprul sku dge 'dun bkra shis/ rje klong
rdol bla ma/ rje dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po/ rje dkon mchog bstan pa'i sgron me/ rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ brag dgon pa dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas/ 'jam pa'i
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //rdo rje'i rigs kyi bdag po khro bo rdo rje sa 'og gi rgyud

la brten nas slob dpon 'gro bzang snying pos bkral ba'i dpal phyag na rdo rje gos sngon can gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi sgrub dkyil/
shAkya dpal gyi lhan thabs bcas pa'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang phyag na rdo rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ dpal kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro
bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ bram ze sadzdza na/ jo bo te dza de wa/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab/ g.yor bo jo ston/ pu ra ba bsod nams rin chen/
'chad phub padma bkra shis/ lha rje ltag par jo bzang / byams pa lo tsA ba dpal ldan tshul khrims shes rab/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug khro phu ba rin chen bsod nams
seng ge yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ chos rje nam mkha' mchog grub/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/ mkhyen rab
chos rje/ des sgo lung pa bkra shis dpal 'byor dang / 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan gnyis/ gnyis kas byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug dbang phyug rab brtan/ bsod nams mchog grub/ bsod nams dpal ldan/ byams pa mkhas btsun/ grags chen 'jam dpal rab brtan/ rab rgyas slob dpon rin chen don grub/
lce btsun bstan 'dzin phrin las/ rje rin chen lhun grub/ rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong / kun gzigs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na blo gsal
bstan skyong nas/ byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ rje kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ des so/ /yang na/ kha che rin chen rdo rje nas/ kha che

dgon pa ba/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ zhu ston/ sa chen/ grags pa rgyal mtshan/ jo btsun grags pa seng ge rgya ston sgrub pa po/ rgya ston sgrub mchog rdo rje dpal/ bsod nams seng
ge rin chen seng ge/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na/ rdo rje dpal nas/ gzhon nu seng ge/ yab grags ston/ bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na/ bkra shis rgyal
mtshan nas/ dpal ldan chos bzang / rin chen rgya mtsho/ bsod nams mchog grub man 'dra'o// ! //gnyis pa spyod pa'i rgyud kyi mtshan nyid ni/ 'dzum zhing dgod pa'i bde ba
lam du byas te yid mtshan rtog las skyob par byed pa'i thabs 'khor dang bcas pa'o/ /sgra don ni/ u bha ya tantra zhes pa'i ra las drangs nas/ gnyis ka'i rgyud dam/ spyod
pa'i rgyud ces bya ste/ phyi lus ngag gi bya ba dang nang ting nge 'dzin cha mnyam du skyod pas na gnyis ka gzhi mthun pa'i phyir de skad do/ /de la dbye na/ sku'i rgyud
de bzhenabazhin gshegs pa'i rigs dang / gsung gi rgyud padma'i rigs dang / thugs kyi rgyud rdo rje'i rigs kyi rgyud dang gsum las/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi rgyud rnam
par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud la brten nas slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang bas bkral zhing / lo chen rin chen bzang pos bsgyur bshad kyis gtan la phab pa'i
bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad snying rje chen po'i snying po can gyi sku'i bkod pa mi zad pa'i rang bzhin gyi dkyil 'khor chen po la nang gi rnam par snang mdzad
kyi dkyil 'khor la lha brgya dang sum cu rtsa lnga mtshan ma gnyis dang bcas pa/ de'i phyi rol shAka thub kyi dkyil 'khor la drang srong drug dang lha dbang gi 'khor ma gtogs
pa'i lha/

bzhi cu rtsa gcig gam bzhi cu rtsa dgu/ de'i phyi rol dam pa sbyin pa'i dkyil 'khor lha sum cu rtsa bdun gyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bskur ba kun mkhyen bu ston gyi dkyil
chog ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi lhan thabs/ blo gsal bstan skyong gi dbang chog bcas pa'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ston pa thub dbang rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun
'jam dpal dbyangs/ /dzai tA ri dgra las rnam rgyal/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ 'bring po rol ba'i rdo rje/ chung ba don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin
chen grags/ /mchims brtson 'grus seng ge/ mchims don yod rgyal ba/ mchims chos kyi seng ge mchims blo gros brtan pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ slob dpon dar ma rgyal mtshan/
byang chen pa bsod nams 'phel/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen
grags pa gzhon nu/ 'jam dbyangs grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dbur stod pa gu Na shrI/ rong po blo bzang grags pa/ rje mkhyen rab chos rje/ slob dpon sangga shrI/ chos rje tshul
khrims 'od zer/ dgon stod pa bsod nams dpal 'byor/ byang gling ba bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon rdo rje bzang po/ /lha tho ba rin chen rgya mtsho/ /rin chen bsod
nams mchog grub/ chen po rin chen bzang po/ mkhan chen byams pa mkhas btsatsunabatsun/ rin chen 'jam dpal don grub/ chos rje ye shes grags pa/ dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang
po/ 'jam dbyangs thub bstan nyi ma/ zag sgom zhabs drung dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas/ zhwa lu blo gsal bstan skyong / gnyis kas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ mkhan
chen dpal

ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis kas bdag 'jam dbyangs blo gter dbang po la'o/ /yang na/ bu ston nas/ khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ des kun mkhyen shes rab dpal
bzang dang / rje bla bzang grags pa gnyis/ gnyis kas sher 'byung blo gros/ 'dul 'dzin dpal ldan bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs dge 'dun 'phel/ rgyud chen bkra shis 'phags/ rgyud
chen bsam 'grub rgya mtsho/ /rgyud chen brtson 'grus 'phags/ rgyud chen rdo rje bzang po/ rgyud chen sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rje
dge 'dun don grub/ skyi shod ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phrin las/ ngag dbang blo bzang mkhas btsun/ ngag dbang chos kyi grags pa/ chos rje yon tan dar rgyas/ bkur ba blo bzang
tshul khrims/ zhabs drung blo bzang rgyal mtshan/ lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje/ rgyal sras skal bzang thub bstan 'jigs med rgya mtsho/ yongs 'dzin blo bzang bstan 'dzin/
shar rtse blo bzang yon tan/ zhwa lu blo gsal bstan skyong man 'dra'o// //de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi bdag por gtogs pa 'jam dpal dpa' bo gcig grub kyi rgyud la brten
nas slob dpon shrA ddhA ka ra warmas bkral ba'i 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsa na lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba ngag dbang legs grub kyi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun 'jam dpal dbyangs/ phyag rdor zhes pa'ang 'dug rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ slob dpon rab 'byor
bskyangs/ grub chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon shes rab bskyangs/ zhi ba'i snying po/ dge mtshan bshes

gnyen/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddhA ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo blo gros grags pa/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon
bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje 'jam dbyangs sa paN/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ skyi ston grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ dol po shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin
dkon mchog 'phel pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ lha mchog seng ge gnyis kas sangs rgyas seng ge/ des thar paN nam mkha' dpal bzang dang / mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang
gnyis/ gnyis kas ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ denas mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ de'i dbon byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ mkhas grub kun dga' chos 'phel/ mtshungs
med bsod nams dpal ldan/ byams pa nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ kun dga' mkhas grub dbang po/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ dpon slob ngag dbang legs
grub/ gnyis kas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ kun dga' 'jam dpal grags pa/ de gnyis kas bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ lo chen nas/ dbus pa dge ser ba/ gnam khu'
chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ sa skya gong ma rnam lnga/ dga' ldan slob dpon mi pham pa/ rgan lhas pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ bla ma nam mkha' dpal/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog legs
blo gros/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag gi

dbang po/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge man 'dra'o// ! //gsum pa rnal 'byor rgyud kyi mtshan nyid ni/ lag bcang gi bde ba lam du byas te yid mtshan rtog las skyob par byed
pa'i thabs 'khor dang bcas pa'o/ /sgra don ni/ yo ga tantra zhes pa'i sgra les drangs nas/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud de/ gtso bor ting nge 'dzin la sbyor ba'i rgyud yin pas na
de skad do/ /dbye na thabs gtso bor ston pa dang / shes rab gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud gnyis kyi dang po la/ rtsa ba'i rgyud dpal de nyid bsdus pa/ bshad pa'i rgyud rdo rje
rtse mo/ cha mthun gyi rgyud dpal mchog dang po 'phros pa'i rgyud/ ngan song sbyong rgyud sogs mang du bzhugs pa las/ rtsa rgyud de nyid bsdus pa'i dum bu dang po 'dod
chags can gyis 'dod chags 'dul bar bstan pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs dpal rdo rje dbyings kyi dbang bkal la/ dkyil chog rdo rje 'byung ba'i lugs kyi dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus

rab/ de gnyis kas rgyang ro ba rkyang po chos blo/ lo chung dang rkyang po gnyis kas sum ston ye 'bar dang / lce zhar ba gnyis/ gnyis kas stag tshal dong sngon gyi sbu ston
'bar thob/ de nas rong smad lha steng gi gtsang yang dag rdo rje/ gtsang ston smra seng / lce ston mdo sde seng ge kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya

pra dznyA pA li ta/ rab 'byor

bskyangs/ pra dznyA bo dhi/ mu kti ko Sha/ dharma pA la/ rin chen bzang po/ gur shing brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ rtsa skya ston

cha

mthun gyi rgyud la dbang bka' gsum yod pa'i/ dang po shes rab gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud la de nyid bsdus pa'i cha mthun gyi rgyud dpal mchog dang po rtogs pa'i rgyal po la brten
