dbus mar rdo rje sems dpa' lha so gsum/ 'jig rten pa zhi bzhi/ 2) shar du rdo rje hU mdzad lha dgu/ 'jig rten pa zhe gnyis/ mtshan ma bzhi/ 3) lhor nam mkha'i snying po
lha dgu/ mtshan ma brgyad/ 4) nub tu 'jig rten dbang phyug lha bcu gsum/ mtshan ma bzhi/ 5) byang du rdo rje khu tshur lha bcu bdun/ mtshan ma bzhi/ 6) shar lhor rdo rje
'jam dpal lha dgu/ mtshan ma brgyad/ 7) lho nub tu nam mkha' mdzod lha bcu gsum/ mtshan ma bzhi/ 8) nub byang du rdo rje 'khor lo lha bcu gsum/ de'i grwa bzhir zhi ba mdung
sogs bzhi/ 9) byang shar du rdo rje gnod sbyin lha dgu/ mtshan ma bcu gnyis/ 10) gzhi dkyil phyi ma'i grwa bzhi'i shar lhor zhi ba mdung gi dkyil 'khor du dbang phyug
chen po lha sum cu/ yi ge dang bcas pa/ 11) lho nub tu ma mo'i dkyil 'khor la nag po chen po lha bcu gsum/ 12) nub byang du ming po gsum gyi dkyil 'khor la rgyal bar byed
pa gtso 'khor bcu gcig 13) byang shar du sring mo bzhi'i dkyil 'khor la sring mo bzhi/ mtshan ma bzhi dang bcas pa ste/ 14) yongs dril lha sum brgya dang sum cu rtsa dgu
mtshan ma zhe brgyad bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor du bu ston gyi dkyil chog don yod pa'i dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor 'byung ba la/ ye shes

rgya mtsho'i ngag 'don dang / dbang bskur gyi lhan thabs sogs sbyar ba'i steng nas/ nyin dang por sa chog dang sta gon gyi chos sngon du 'gro bas/ nyin gnyis par sgrub cing
mchod pa/ nyin gsum par gzhi dkyil dang dbus dkyil kyi bdag 'jug dang slob ma gzhug cing dbang bskur ba mtha' brten dang bcas pa/ nyin bzhi par rdo rje hU mdzad sogs phyogs
bzhi'i dkyil 'khor bzhi/ nyin lnga par rdo rje 'jam dpal sogs mtshams bzhi'i dkyil 'khor bzhi/ nyin drug par zhi mdung sogs gzhi dkyil gyi phyi'i grwa bzhi'i dkyil 'khor
bzhi ste/ 'jig rten las 'das pa dang 'jig rten pa'i dkyil 'khor bcu bzhi'i dbang bskur ba mtha' brten dang bcas pa bla ma brgyud pa'i phyag gzhes ltar thob pa'i brgyud
pa la/ thog mar yo ga stod lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ kun dga' snying po/ pradznyA bA li ta/ pradznyA
bo dhi/ dharma pA la/ 'jig rten mig gcig lo chen rin chen bzang po/ rgya ye shes tshul khrims/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ rtsa skya dkon mchog
grags/ mnyam khad pa shAkya 'bum/ mnyam khad pa rgya gar 'phan/ bla ma chos grags dpal/ rtsa skya khri brtan chen po/ sras mchog bsod nams dpal bzang / gsal ba blo gros
dpal/ grags chen dpal/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub/ chos rje rin chen dpal grub/
rdor 'chang mkhyen rab chos rje/ 'gro mgon rgyal ba dpal ldan/ gnas brtan bstan pa bzang po/ byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan/

des 'brog khang pa rin chen sangs rgyas tshe dpal dang / chos 'khor thar gling log pa bsod nams dpal 'byor gnyis/ gnyis kas lha bo pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ denas mkhan chen
rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ chos 'khor slob dpon dpal mchog chen po bsod nams rgya mtsho/ byams pa chos rgyal/ ye shes bkra shis/ zhwa lu ri phug bla ma rin chen lhun
grub/ lha btsun don grub bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ sog po 'jam dbyangs phrin las/ thar rtse mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs rin chen rdo rje/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ rtsa
skya dkon grags nas/ rgya gar 'phan/ chos kyi grags pa/ khri chen mo/ bsod nams bzang po/ blo gros dpal/ bla ma grags chen/ 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na/ rtsa skya dkon
grags nas/ shAkya 'bum/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od man 'dra'o/ /smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bundha bai ro tsa na/ shrI badzra pA Ni/ ma hA sidha
ra bi shrI/ A tsARYa badzra warma/ sidhA tsARYA nanda garbha/ manydzu shrI bi ma la kirti/ su bhU ti pA li ta/ shraddhA ka ra warma/ ratna bha dra/ sA dhU pradznyA/ rkyang
po chos blo/ sum ston ye 'bar/ lce zhar ba/ spru ston 'bar thog gtsang yang dag rdo rje/ gtsang smra ba'i seng ge lce jo mdo/ chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon rgyam/
bu ston rin grub man 'dra'o/ /dpal mchog rdor sems rigs bsdus kyi dbus dkyil zur du phyung zhing / brgyud pa'ang rigs bsdus smad lugs dang gcig pas 'dir logs su ma bkod
do// //gnyis pa la gsum gyi/ dang po dpal ngan song sbyong ba'i rgyud nas gsungs pa'i dkyil 'khor bcu

gnyis te/ de'ang don dam bden pa gtso bor ston pa'i dkyil 'khor drug kun rdzob bden pa gtso bor ston pa'i dkyil 'khor drug ste bcu gnyis las/ dang po kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil
'khor/ shAkya thub pa sku'i dkyil 'khor/ tshe dpag med pa gsung gi dkyil 'khor/ phyag na rdo rje thugs kyi dkyil 'khor/ me ltar 'bar ba yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor/ 'khor los
sgyur ba phrin las kyi dkyil 'khor te 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dkyil 'khor drug gnyis pa phyag na rdo rje la rgyal chen bzhis bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor/ phyag na rdo rje la
phyogs skyong bcus bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor/ phyag na rdo rje la gza' brgyad rgyu skar nyer brgyad dang bcas pas bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor/ phyag na rdo rje la klu chen brgyad
gyis bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor/ phyag na rdo rje la 'jigs byed dgus bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor/ phyag na rdo rje la lha chen brgyad gyis bskor ba'i dkyil 'khor te 'jig rten pa'i
dkyil 'khor drug bcas/ mdor na sbyong rgyud kyi dkyil 'khor chen po bcu gnyis su dbang bskur ba thar rtse paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang gi yig steng nas thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla ba/ dzi na mi tra/ swa sti pha la/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ pradznyA pA li te/ kha che ye shes rdo rje/ pa ra
hi ta/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ kha che dharma pA la/ dznyA na shrI/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/
gshen ston rdo rje seng ge bla ma rgya gsar ba/ 'brom dzi ti pa/ snye mdo bsod nams dpal/ gnyal pa chos kyi grags pa/ bya ston rin chen 'od/

'dzin pa blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub
dpal ldan rdo rje/ bla ma mgon po dbang phyug gnyan lo grags pa blo gros/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra
shis/ de'i dbon shar ba shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhas grub shAkya kun dga'/ 'jam mgon lhun grub dpal ldan/ rje bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ thar rtse nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ sa chen
kun dga' blo gros/ nam mkha' 'chi med/ 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma/ 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen/ rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong / byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/
ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ngor khang gsar mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ nam mkha' dpal bzang yan gong ltar la/
de nas ngag dbang mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ dbon mkhyen brtse rab brtan/ kun mkhyen chos kyi nyi ma/ drung gnas
sbyin pa bstan 'dzin/ gling smad slob dpon bde ba rab bzang / rje kun dga' chos skyong / skyo mda' ba kun dga' bsod nams/ nam mkha' 'chi med man 'dra'o/ /'chi bdag 'joms
pa sbyong dkyil gyi nang nas zur du phyung pa'i sbyong rgyud thugs dkyil dang lha sngags gcig pas dbang zur du mi dgos shing / brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ rab
gsal zla ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ kun dga' snying po/ pradznyA pA li ta/ pradznyA bo dhi/ mukti ko Sha/ dharma phA la/ jo bo rje dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na/ go mI

sgom chen/ skyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ sras pradznyA singha/ snur byang chub 'od/ snur nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ snur ye rgyal/ chos 'phags
rgyal mtshan/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ rgyal mtshan grags pa/ bkra shis rin chen/ ngor chen man sbyong rgyud dang 'dra/ yang na/ shar chen kun bkras nas/ nam mkha' sangs rgyas/
dam chos bsam 'grub/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bsod nams dpal ldan/ sangs rgyas bstan pa/ nam mkha' bsam 'grub man 'dra'o// //gnyis pa sbyong rgyud brtag pa dang pos dngos
bstan kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor lha so bdun mgron thabs dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba ngor chen dkyil chog dang / dkon lhun mtshams sbyor gnyis kyi
steng nas thob pa'i dang po smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ ston mchog thub dbang shAkya'i tog gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/ za hor gyi rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ paNDi ta rab
'byor bskyangs/ grub chen kun dga' snying po/ paNDi ta shes rab bskyangs/ slob dpon zhi ba'i snying po/ slob dpon dge mtshan bshes gnyen/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/
slob dpon dad byed go cha/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo blo gros grags pa/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ des gnyan phul byung ba
gtsug tor rgyal po dang / slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo gnyis/ gnyis kas rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ de nas sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal
'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' bag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar
chen ye

shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ des mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ des kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge de gsum gas mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/
de nas mtshungs med dkon mchog lhun grub/ thugs sras shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / de'i dbon nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ hor se chen gan nam mkha'
dpal bzang / rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ de gnyis kas mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ de nas byams pa tshul khrims dpal bzang / byams pa bsod nams bzang po/ mkhan chen
nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ thar rtse nam mkha' 'chi med/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang 'jam dbyangs
rin chen rdo rje/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang na/ nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ ngag dbang kun dga' bsod
nams/ ngag dbang bsod nams dbang phyug ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ ngag dbang bsod nams rin chen/ ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros man 'dra/ yang na/ sa paN nas/ kun dga'
dpal ba/ bsod nams brtan pa/ ti shrI kun dga' blo gros/ de gnyis kas bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na/ sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ sangs rgyas seng
ge nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra/ yang na/ nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhas btsun kun dga' legs pa/ sangs rgyas
phun tshogs

man 'dra/ yang na/ ngor chen nas/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge sangs rgyas seng ge man 'dra'o/ /kha che lugs
kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ dpe med srung ba/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/ 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ kha che rnam bshad lha/ kha che paN chen
shAkya shrI/ rab 'byor zla ba/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba bsod nams seng ge zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ blo gros brtan pa/ dpal ldan tshul khrims man 'dra'o/ /chags
lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das kun rig rnam par snang mdzad/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ kun dga' snying po/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ shAnti pa/
rdo rje gdan pa/ a bhA ya ka ra/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ niShka langga de ba/ rdo rje gdan pa chung ba don yod rdo rje/ slob dpon rA wendra/ chag lo chos rje dpal/ g.yag
sde bsod nams seng ge paNDi ta rdo rje shes rab/ zhar dkon mchog dpal man gong smad lugs dang 'dra/ yang na/ g.yag sde bsod seng nas/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bag ston gzhon
nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan tshul khrims man 'dra'o/ /stod lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rnam par snang mdzad/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla
ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ kun dga' snying po/ pradznyA pA li ta/ pradznyA bo dhi/ mukti ko Sha/ dharma pA la/ dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na/ go mi sgom chen/ skyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal
pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ de'i sras snur badzra singha/ snur byang chub 'od/ snur nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rin chen shes rab/ yang rtse ba rin chen
seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/

bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po man gong smad lugs dang 'dra/ yang na/ snur nyi 'od nas/ rtsa skya ston grags/ slob dpon ston 'bum/ dbus pa sangs rgyas
'bum/ dge lding pa chos sku 'od zer/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na/ snur nyi 'od nas/ gnyen rdo rje seng ge glan chos kyi 'byung gnas/ gtum ston shAkya
'bum/ 'dzim pa rin chen shes rab/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge man 'dra/ yang na/ pradznyA pA li ta nas/ go mI dge bsnyen/ shAkya dznyA na/ jo bo rje man 'dra/ yang
na/ pradznyA pA li ta na/ dharma pA la/ rab 'byor bskyangs/ jo bo rje man 'dra/ yang na/ rab gsal zla ba nas/ ye shes rdo rje/ kun dga' snying po man 'dra/ yang na/ rnam
snang / dzai tA ri/ kun snying / rab 'byor bskyangs/ nA ya ka pa/ mai tri pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ niShka langka de ba/ re wendra/ chag lo/ g.yag sde lo tsA/ lo tsA ba mchog
ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston man 'dra'o/ /smad lugs kyi brgyud pa yang na/ kun dga' snying po yan snga ma ltar la/ de nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rdo rje/ dad byed
go cha/ lo chen rin bzang / lo chung legs sher/ sum ston ye 'bar/ gnyan ston tshul 'bar/ thod pa dben tsha grags/ thod pa 'od zer/ ri lung phug pa chos mgon/ bla ma blo
ldan seng ge 'phags 'od yon rgyam/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na/ ri phug chos mgon nas/ dmar chos kyi rgyal po/ bla chen 'phags pa/ paNDi ta rdo rje shes rab/ bla ma 'phags
rgyal/ bla ma rin chen dpal bzang / chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal tshul man 'dra'o// //gsum pa ngan song sbyong ba'i brtag pa phyogs gcig pa nas gsungs

pa'i shAkya seng ge gtsug tor dgu pa'i dkyil 'khor du bu ston gyi dkyil chog la byang gling pa bkra shis rgyan mtshan gyi lhan thabs sbyar ba'i steng nas dbang bskur ba thob
pa'i dang po stod lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ ston pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ chos rgyal rab gsal zla ba/ slob dpon ye shes rdo rje/ grub chen kun dga' snying
po/ pradznyA pA li ta/ go mI dge bsnyen/ shAkya dznyA na/ jo bo rje a ti sha/ go mI sgom chen/ skyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ snur nyi ma 'od zer/ zlum
ston yon nyan grags pa/ rtsa skya mnyam khad pa/ rtsa skya khri ston/ de sras bsod nams bzang po/ de gnyis kas gsal ba blo gros dpal/ bla ma grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od yon
tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha' mchog grub/ dka' bzhi pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ rin chen
rgyal po/ sku zhang rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ rin chen dpal ldan chos bzang / lha bo pa rin chen rgya mtsho/ rin chen
bsod nams mchog grub/ rin chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rin chen 'jam dpal don grub/ 'jam mgon gsung rab rgya mtsho/ lce btsun bstan 'dzin phrin las/ ye shes dpal 'byor/ blo
gsal bstan skyong / blo bzang mkhyen rab/ thar rtse mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs rin chen rdo rje/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ snur nyi nas/ sbu ston 'bar thog yang dag
rdo rje/ 'byung gnas seng ge'am smra seng / lce mdo sde seng ge chos sku 'od zer/ blo ldan seng ge 'phags 'od man 'dra/ smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ thub dbang / phyag
nor/ rab gsal zla ba/ des pad dkar ye shes/ ye shes rdo rje/

sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po/ nyi ma'i snying po ste slob ma'i mchog bzhi la/ de bzhi kas kun dga' snying po la/ denas tha ga na pa/ ngag dbang grags pa/ bha len shAnti/ mi bskyod
rdo rje/ shraddhA ka ra/ lo chen rin bzang / lo chung legs sher/ shangs chab lha khang gi sum ston ye 'bar/ g.yag sde'i gnyan ston tshul khrims 'bar/ thod pa dben rtsa
grags/ dge bshes jo phur/ thod pa 'od zer/ rong pa chos mgon/ lce btsun blo ldan seng ge 'phags lod/ bu ston/ rin chen rnam rgyal man stod lugs ltar ro/ /kha che'i lugs
kyi brgyud pa ni/ thub dbang / phyag rdor/ dznyA na shrI mi tra/ ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa/ a bhyA ka ra/ rdo rje gdan pa/ bi khyA ta de ba/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/
dA na shri la/ g.yag sde lo tsA ba/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ dpal ldan seng ge bu ston man 'dra'o// //dbang bka' gsum pa 'jam dpal mtshan brjod yo ga
ltar bkral ba'i skor la/ 'grel pa che 'bring chung gsum yod pa las/ dang po slob padapon 'jam dpal grags pas bkral ba'i 'grel chen lugs chos dbyings gsung gi dbang phyug
rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor/ chos kyi dkyil 'khor/ gzungs kyi dkyil 'khor gsum la 'jig rten las 'das pa'i lha brgya dang nyi shu rtsa lnga/ rdo rje'i rigs kyi dkyil 'khor la 'jig
rten pa'i lha brgya dang bzhi ste yongs dril lha nyis brgya dang nyi shu rtsa dgu'i dkyil 'khor chen por bu ston gyi dkyil chog dang / ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi ngag 'don
bcas pa'i steng nas sta gon dang 'jug pa rdo rje slob ma'i dbang sngon du 'gro ba'i/ shar rdo rje'i rigs/ lho rin chen rigs/ nub padma'i rigs/ byang

las kyi rigs/ dbus rigs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs te rnam pa lnga'i rdo rje slob dpon gyi dbang so sor rgyas par bskur ba dang / thun mong du lung bstan
pa sogs nas dkyil 'khor mchod pa dang / gsang bar gdams pa'i bar mthar chags su thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa 'i sangs rgyas/ rje btsun 'jam dpal dbyangs/
kha che ye shes rdo rje/ slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pa/ mkhas pa dpal sbas bzang po/ bram ze ye shes rdo rje/ shes rab 'byung gnas sbas pa/ bram ze bzhad pa'i rdo rje/
padma ka ra warma/ shra ddhA ka ra warma/ de gnyis kas lo chen rin chen bzang po/ de nas lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ rngog dge ser ba/ rkyang po dar ma grags/ khri ston
kun dga' 'od zer/ mkhan po chos kyi rdo rje/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'jam dbyangs
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ shar chen ye shes rgya mtsho/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ des mkhas grub rig pa'i glog phreng dang / 'khrul zhig blo gros thogs med
gnyis/ gnyis kas nor bu gling pa nor bu rdo rje/ de nas 'jam dbyangs dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ don grub gling pa paN chen bsod nams mchog ldan/ dam chos gling pa kun dga'
dbang po/ rngog ston nam mkha' mdzod pa/ rje mang thos rgya mtsho/ sgyi chu mkhan chen blo gros dbang phyug sems bskyed gling pa kun dga' chos 'phel/ khang ltag dge bshes
bsod nams don ldan/ gser 'bum chos rje phun tshogs rnam rgyal/ rong pa chos rje dkon mchog sbyin pa/ des byang 'dren chen mo phun tshogs chos 'phel dang / 'bras bu gling

pa slob dpon dge 'dun rab rgyas gnyis/ gnyis kas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des chos rje bla ma kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ mang thos
rgya mtsho nas/ bla ma chos grags dar rgyas/ rnam grong chos dbang rgya mtsho/ mang thos bsod nams rgya mtsho/ khang ltag bsod nams don ldan man 'dra'o// //gnyis pa slob
dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes bkral ba'i 'grel pa 'bring po'i lugs 'jam dpal gsang ldan lha lnga bcu rtsa ginyasaganyis pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba khyung lhas pa dang
yongs grags rgya bo'i dkyil chog la/ dge 'dun dpal bzang gi lhan thabs sbyar ba'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal/ 'jam dpal bshes
gnyen/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ nyi ma'i snying po/ sURYa siddhiM/ chos kyi rdo rje/ mu tra siddhi/ des de wa shwa ra dang / smr-i ti dznyA na gnyis/ gnyis kas rngog sangs
rgyas yon tan/ phyi ma gnyis kas tshangs sde ngag gi dbang phyug des khams pa shes rab rdo rje dang / bye ma lung pa gnyis/ gnyis kas rngog chos kyi rdo rje/ de nas rngog
mdo sde/ rtsag dar ma rgyal po/ tshur dum bu khams pa/ dge bshes bzang po pa/ rngog rin chen bzang po/ rngog chos kyi rgyal po/ rngog don grub dpal/ rngog byang chub dpal/
rngor 'dzin karma phrin las/ rngog byang chub grags pa/ gnyis kas rngog bsod nams lhun grub/ de nas rngog bsod nams bstan 'dzin/ zhabs drung 'jam dbyangs 'od zer/ thar
gling pa bsod nams dpal 'byor/ kun dga' mang thos rgya mtsho/ gong dkar phun tshogs rgya mtsho/ byams pa chos rgyal/ rje

ye shes bkra shis/ ye shes dpal 'byor/ zhwa lu ri phug sprul sku blo gsal bstan skyong / lha btsun don grub rgyal mtshan/ rje 'jam dbyangs phrin las/ mkhan chen 'jam dbyangs
rin chen rdo rje/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ zhabs drung 'jam dbyangs 'od zer nas/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ mtshungs med rin chen rgya mtsho/ kun dga' mang
thos rgya mtsho man 'dra/ yang na/ ye shes bkra shis nas/ lce btsun mkhyen rab dbang po/ ye shes dpal 'byor man 'dra'o// ! //bzhi pa rnal 'byor chen po bla na med pa'i rgyud
kyi ngo bo'am mtshan nyid ni/ dbang po gnyis sbyor gyi bde ba lam du byas te yid mtshan rtog las skyob par byed pa'i thabs 'khor dang bcas pa'o/ /sgra don ni/ mahA yo
ga zhes pa'i sgra las drangs na/ rnal 'byor chen po ste/ thabs dang shes rab zung du 'jug pa'i nang gi rnal 'byor gyi khyad par gong na med pa gtso bor ston pa'i phyir na
de skad do/ /dbye na/ rgyud sde'i skor dang / gdams ngag gi skor gnyis/ dang po la thabs gtso bor ston pa pha'i rgyud dang / shes rab gtso bor ston pa ma'i rgyud/ de gnyis
ka'i khyab byed du gyur pa zung 'jug gtso bor ston pa gnyis su med pa'i rgyud dang gsum las/ dang po la'ang gdul bya 'dod chags can gtso bor rjes su gzung ba'i don du
gsungs pa dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i skor dang / gdul bya zhe sdang can gtso bor rjes su gzung ba'i don du gsungs pa dpal gshin rje'i gshed kyi skor dang / gdul bya gti mug
can gtso bor rjes su gzung ba'i don du gsungs pa rnam snang sgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i skor dang gsum/ dang po la/ sangs rgyas gnyis pa 'phags mchog klu sgrub zhabs kyis

legs par bkral ba'i dpal gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod rdo rje lha so gnyis pa'i dkyil 'khor du rje ngag dbang legs grub kyi sgrub dkyil nag 'gros dang / sngags chen kun dga'
rin chen gyi mtshams sbyor gnyis kyi steng nas sta gon dang 'jug pa sngon du 'gro ba'i dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa la/ thog mar klu byang gi dkyil chog nyi
shu pa'i rjes su 'brang ba sa lugs kyi dbang bka' rnying ma'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang / dpal phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po indra bhU ti/ klu las gyur pa'i rnal
'byor ma/ rgyal po pi su kalpa/ bram ze sa ra ha pa/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ des ARYa de wa/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ klu'i byang chub/ ma taM gi pa/ zla ba grags pa ste lnga/ lnga
kas slob pa'i rdo rje/ de nas nag po spyod pa/ sa 'dres pa chen po/ des paNDi ta chen po bI dya bha dra/ de wa a ka ra tsandra/ dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na gsum/ gsum
gas 'gos khug pa lhas btsas/ de nas dbus pa dge ser/ gnam kha'u pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ dar ma rgyal mtshan/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ kha'u pa rdo rje bdud 'joms/ rje
btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ de gnyis kas bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ de nas buddha shrI/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/
go rams pa bsod nams seng ge yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo 'jam dbyangs kun dga'

bsod nams/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen/ spyan snga dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ des mus chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan dang / sngags 'chang grags
pa blo gros gnyis/ gnyis kas a mes zhabs kun dga' bsod nams/ sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ rje dkon mchog rgyal po/ yab rje bsod nams rin chen/ sa chen
ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros/ byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag gam/ yang na/ kun dga' bstan 'dzin
nas/ dpon slob ngag dbang legs grub/ grub mchog bsod nams bzang po/ sprul sku shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter la'o/
/yang na/ go rams pa bsod nams seng ge nas/ paN chen dbang phyug grub pa/ 'jam dbyangs ngag gi dbang phyug sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen man 'dra/ yang na/ rje btsun sangs
rgyas rin chen nas/ rje dkon mchog rin chen/ dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ bsod nams lhun grub/ ngag dbang chos grags/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis
man 'dra/ yang na/ yab rje bsod rin nas/ rje seng ge rgyal mtshan/ sa chen kun blo man 'dra'o/ /bka' babs bdun ldan du bzhugs pa ltar na/ dang po 'gos lugs kyi brgyud
pa ni/ 'gos khug pa lhas btsas yan sngar bzhin la/ gzhan yang rje 'gos kyis paNDi ta bla ma bdun cu/ mkha' 'gro'i bla ma gnyis dang bcas pa las gsan/ de nas mdar ba seng
ge rgyal mtshan/ rngog

ye shes seng ge rngog nyi ma seng ge glan rtsad tsha nyi ma lcam/ de gnyis kas rngog ARYa de wa/ de nas zhar chos pa skyi mkhar 'jug stag pa rin chen grags/ thur lhas pa tshul
khrims skyabs/ thang spe ba 'phags pa skyabs/ gser lding pa gzhon nu 'od/ kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston rin chen grub/ khyung lhas
pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun bzang man snga ma ltar ro/ /gnyis pa mar lugs grub thob rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / indra
bhU ti/ DA ki bde ba'i zhabs/ Dombi he ru ka rdo rje dril bu pa/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ kampa ma la/ nag po spyod pa/ te lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar lo chos kyi blo gros/
mtshur ston dbang gi rdo rje/ 'khon gad pa kIrti/ 'khon bsod nams rin chen/ thur lhas pa tshul khrims skyabs man snga ma ltar ro/ /gsum pa mar lugs mkhas pa paNDi ta'i
brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa klu sgrub yan gong sa lugs kyi dbang bka' rnying ma'i brgyud pa ltar la/ de nas slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen/ grub chen klu'i byang chub/ slob dpon
'phags pa lha/ ma taM gi pa ste thugs sras bzhi dang / sangs rgyas bskyangs/ legs ldan 'byed/ zla ba grags pa/ slob dpon dpa' bo ste nye ba'i thugs sras bzhi/ de nas tai
lo pa'am/ yang na/ klu sgrub/ ma taM gi pa/ te lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa lo tsA ba'am/ yang na/ ma taM gi pa nas/ zla grags/ rig pa'i khu byug a wa dhU ti pa/ spyod pa'i
rdo rje/ nag po'i zhabs/ dri med blo gros/ dpal ye shes snying po/ mar pa lo tsA ba/ mtshur dbang gi rdo rje/ 'khon gad pa kIrti/ 'khon

bsod nams rin chen/ mi nyag thur lhas pa tshul khrims skyabs/ dbus 1.mgar 2.dge 3.gsum/ gsum gas rin chen gling pa tshul khrims mdzes pa/ bla ma rgya 'pho ba lung pa/ dge slong
chos grags dpal bzang / bla ma shAkya gzhon nu/ bla ma blo ldan pa/ 'phags 'od yon rgyam man 'dra'o/ /bzhi pa jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / indra bhU
ti/ slob dpon nA ga jo ki/ grub chen sa ra ha pa/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ ARYa de wa/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ zla ba grags pa/ ku sA li che chung gnyis/ jo bo rje/ ngor pa mgar
dge/ lha rje stod pa tshul khrims dpal/ de sras che ba shes rab rgyal mtshan/ chung ba shes rab gtsug tor/ lha rje dharma tsakra/ thang stod chos kyi 'od zer/ bla chen klog
skya grags pa bzang po/ bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan grags pa/ 'phags 'od man snga ma dang 'dra'o/ /lnga pa chag lugs kyi brgyud pa
ni/ klu sgrub yan sngar ltar la/ de nas ARYa de wa/ klu'i byang chub/ slob dpon dpa' bo/ zla ba grags pa/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ dzA landhA
ri pa'am drwa ba 'dzin/ dpe med dpal/ gambhi ra ma ti'am blo zab pa/ niShka langka de wa'am rnyog med lha/ nyi dbang srung / chag lo chos rje dpal/ 'u yug ku ngar ba bla
ma dpal/ bla ma grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od man 'dra'o/ /drug pa slob dpon sgra gcan 'dzin bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i dbang chog zung 'jug gsal ba'i rjes su 'brang ba sa
lugs kyi dbang bka' gsar ma'i brgyud pa ni/ rdor 'chang / phyag rdor/ klu sgrub/ ARYa de wa/ klu'i byang chub/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ zla ba grags pa/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ bha
bya kIrti'am skal ldan grags pa/

'od zer 'byung gnas grags pa/ 'od mdzad lha/ chos 'byung zhi ba/ bi khyA ta de wa/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI bha dra/ sa skya paNDi ta/ 'od zer shAkya kha'u pa dar ma shes
rab/ se mo da pa rin chen dpal/ bla ma ra gnyis pa rgyal mtshan rin chen/ spro lung pa kun dga' smon lam/ bla ma grags chen pa/ 'phags 'od man 'dra'o/ /bdun pa dpyal lugs
kyi brgyud pa ni/ kha che paN chen yan gong ltar la/ de nas dpyal chos kyi bzang po/ rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ bla ma dpal gyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma don mo ri pa/ grags
chen pa man 'dra/ yang na/ rngor 'chang / phyag rdor/ indra bhU ti/ klu sgrub/ ARYa de wa/ ma taM ga pa/ sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bshes gnyen/ bi khyA de wa man 'dra'o/ /yang
dge ldan phyagosaphyogs su brgyud pa ltar na/ 'phags 'od yan gong mar lugs paNDi ta'i brgyud pa dang 'dra zhing / de nas bu ston rin chen grub/ sgra bsgyur nam mkha'
bzang po/ re mda' ba gzhon nu blo gros/ rje blo bzang grags pa/ gnas brtan bzang skyong ba/ rje shes rab seng ge 'dul nag dpal ldan bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs dge 'dun yar 'phel/
rgyud chen bkra shis 'phags/ paN chen bsam 'grub rgya mtsho/ rgyud chen brtson 'grus 'phags/ rgyud chen rdo rje bzang po/ rgyud chen sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ rgyud chen
dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ rgyud chen dkon mchog yar 'phel/ 'jam dbyangs bzhad pa'i rdo rje/ 'jam dbyangs bde ba'i rdo rje/ mkhan chen dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ dkon mchog 'jigs
med dbang po/ dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des so// //

yang slob dpon klu sgrub zhabs kyis bkral ba'i gsang ba 'dus pa mi bskyod pa mar lugs lha so gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du 'jam mgon blo gros mtha' yas kyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi
rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ indra bhU ti/ klu las gyur pa'i rnal 'byor ma/ bi su kalpa/ sa ra ha pa/ klu sgrub/ ARYa de wa/
shAkya mi tra/ nA ga bo dhi/ ma taM gi pa/ zla ba grags pa/ slob pa'i rdo rje/ nag po dam tshig rdo rje/ dri med blo gros/ ye shes snying po'am/ yang na/ zla grags nas/ rig
pa'i khu byug a wa dhU ti pa/ spyod pa'i rdo rje/ nag po spyod pa/ dri med blo gros/ ye shes snying po/ gang ltar yang de nas mar lo chos kyi blo gros/ mtshur ston dbang
gi rdo rje/ 'khon ston gad pa kIrti/ bla ma bsod nams rin chen/ mi nyag thur lhas pa tshul khrims skyabs/ dbus mgar dge gsum/ bzhi gas gangs bar gser kha'i rin chen gling
pa tshul khrims mdzes pa/ rgya pho ba lung pa/ gnyos a seng / ye shes dpal/ karma pa rang byung rdo rje/ rtogs ldan mgon po rgyal mtshan/ chos rje rol pa'i rdo rje/ rin
chen rgyal po/ mkhan chen mgo blon pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mtshur phu 'jam dbyangs chen po don grub 'od zer/ slob dpon bla ma rgyal mtshan/ spyan snga chos kyi grags
pa/ rab 'byams pa tshul khrims dbang phyug dpa' bo gtsug lag phreng ba/ dkon mchog 'bangs/ dbang phyug rdo rje/ chos kyi dbang phyug 'bri gung chos grags/ dkon mchog lhun
grub/ dkon mchog phrin las bzang po/ don grub chos rgyal/ lho sprul dkon mchog chos kyi rgya mtsho/ brab shi karma rnam rol/ tshe dbang kun khyab/ karma ratna/ 'od gsal
'gyur med/ rje ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo

gter la'o/ /yang na/ thur lhas tshul skyabs nas/ thang spe 'phags skyabs/ gser lding gzhon 'od/ dge lding chos 'od/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ byang chub rgyal
mtshan/ sku zhar rin chen bkra shis/ rwa sgreng dka' bzhi pa/ sku zhang sangs rgyas dpal 'byor/ dus zhabs pa shAkya dbang phyug 'jam dbyangs chos kyi grags pa/ des kun
spangs shes rab rgya mtsho dang / sngags 'chang tshe bdag bkra shis gnyis/ gnyis kas 'thug pa padma dkar po/ de nas lha rtsi pa ngag dbang bzang po/ 'brug pa dpag bsam dbang
po/ rje btsun yar 'phel dbang po/ ngag dbang kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ chos rgyal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo/ tshe dbang kun khyab man 'dra/ yang na/ rin chen rnam rgyal
nas/ dpal mchog don grub/ zla ba dpal/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab mchog grub/ dkon mchog dpal bzang / bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan chos bzang / tA ra
nA tha/ rin chen rgya mtsho/ ye shes rgya mtsho/ snying po mtha' yas/ kun bzang dbang po/ kun dga' rnam rgyal/ tshe dbang kun khyab man 'dra/ yang na/ bu ston nas/ bla ma
dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos rje/ bsod nams bzang po/ kun dga' rnam rgyal/ byang chub dbang po/ shAkya kun dga'/ ye shes dbang po/ tA ra nA tha man 'dra'o/
/yang na/ bu ston nas/ khyung lhas pa/ shar chen/ ngor chen/ shAkya mchog ldan/ rab gsal zla ba mgon po/ kun dga' grol mchog byams pa lhun grub/ tA ra nA tha man 'dra'o//
//grub pa'i slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis legs par bkral

pa'i dpal gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du rje ngag dbang legs grub kyi sgrub dkyil dang / kun blo'i mtshams sbyor gyiigyi steng nas sta gon

slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes/ dpal mar me mdzad bzang po/ kun dga' snying po/ tha ga na/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/ dad byed go cha/ padmA ka ra warma/ de gnyis kas

pa sa phug pa shAkya rdo rje/ rong pa chos mgon/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ khyung po lhas pa gzhon
nu bsod nams/ shar chen ye rgyal/ ngor chen kun bzang / rgyal tshab kun dbang / go rams pa bsod seng / rje btsun sangs rin/ sa lo kun bsod dam 'jam dpal rdo rje/ dkon

grub/ bkra shis lhun grub/ sangs rgyas ye shes/ kun dga' blo gros/ des nam mkha' 'chi med dang / kun dga' mkhas grub dbang po gnyis/ gnyis kas byams pa kun dga' bstan
'dzin/ des 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po dang / dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan gnyis/

phyug 'jam mgon kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen/ zhwa lu blo gsal bstan skyong / mkhyen brtse'i dbang po man 'dra'o/ /gnyis pa sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / 'jam dpal rdo rje/ sangs rgyas ye shes/ mar me mdzad/ dpal bde ba/ dri med sbas pa/ rin chen rdo rje/ rin chen grags pa/ ri sul gyi rnal 'byor ma/ bla
ma sendha ba/ gnyan lo dar ma grags/ gnam kha'u pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ sa skya'i gong ma rnam lnga/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ kun dga' bsod
nams/ khams pa rdo rje dpal/ spang khang grags pa dpal/ kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa/ sa bzang paN chen ma ti dhwa dza/ de dbon sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen
man 'dra'o/ gsum pa kha che lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'jam dbyangs/ sangs rgyas ye shes/ mar me mdzad/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ kha che ganggA dha ra/
paNDi ta bi na shrI/ khams pa rdo rje dpal man 'dra'o/ /bzhi pa gnyos lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ dri med sbas pa yin gong sa lugs ltar la/ de nas seng ge'i rnal 'byor ratna
shrI/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ ba linta A tsARYa/ gnyos lo tsA ba yon tan grags/ gnyos rdo rje bla ma/ gnyos dpal le/ gnyos grags pa dpal/ gnyos rgyal ba lha nang pa gzi
brjid dpal/ ston mo lung pa ye shes dpal/ kun mkhyen chos 'od/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston man lo chen lugs dang 'dra'o/ /

lnga pa jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'jam dbyangs/ sangs rgyas ye shes/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ kun dga' snying po/ tha ga na/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/
jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha/ rgya lcags ri gong kha ba/ rji bu kha pa/ spen phug pa/ zhang ye shes rdo rje/ gze pa don grub mgon po/ bar thang pa yab sras/ bla ma dar ma
shAkya/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug lo tsA ba mchog legs blo gros/ dpal ldan seng ge bu ston man 'dra'o/ /drug pa rwa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'jam dbyangs/

kIrti/ puNye shrI/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rdo rje sra brtan man gong lo chen lugs dang 'dra'o// //jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti shas bkral ba'i dpal gsang ba 'dus pa
spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug lha bcu dgu'i dkyil 'khor du zhu chen gyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / spyan ras
gzigs/ slob dpon sangs rgyas ye shes/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ tha ga na pa/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/ mnyam med jo bo chen po mar me mdzad
dam/ yang na/ rdo rje 'chang / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha lha btsun byang chub 'od/ khum pa byang chub rdo rje/ rgya lcags ri gong kha pa/ rdzi
bu kha pa shAkya grags/ spen phug pa dar ma grags/ zhang ye shes rdo rje/ gze pa don grub mgon

po/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ de'i sras chos kyi grags pa/ bla ma dar ma shAkya/ bsod nams dbang po/ lo tsA ba mchog legs blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen
grub/ khyung lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab kun dga' dbang phyug kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge mus chen sangs
rgyas rin chen/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge thar paN nam mkha' dpal bzang / de'i dbon nam mkha' rin chen/
hor nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhan chen shes rab rgya mtsho/ mkhas btsun kun dga' chos 'phel/ chos rje dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med bkra shis bzang po/ 'jam mgon
sangs rgyas ye shes/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ des byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med dang / mi nyag ri khug sprul sku kun dga' mkhas grub dbang po gnyis/ gnyis kas byams pa
kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ de gsum gas rje dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ des bdag gam/ yang na/ rje mkhyen
brtses bdag blo gter la'o// //slob dpon dza wa ri pas bkral ba'i pha rgyud mi bskyod pa'i rigs su gtogs par dpal phyag na rdo rje 'khor lo chen po lha bco brgyad kyi dkyil
'khor du 'dul 'dzin grags pa'i sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ mkha' 'gro ma seng ge gdong pa
can/ grub chen sha ba ri pa/ paN chen dza ba

ri pa/ paNDi ta de ba pUrNa ma ti/ lo tsA ba mgar chos kyi bzang po/ bshes gnyen rin chen dngos grub/ dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ dmar shes rab rdo rje/ dmar thub pa shes rab/
dmar brtson 'grus rdo rje/ dmar chos rgyal shes rab/ dmar shAkya grub pa/ yang / rtse ba rin chen seng ge kun mkhyen bu ston rin chen grub/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs dkar po/
chos rje rin chen legs pa/ sku zhang mkhyen rab chos rje/ 'bul 'dzin grags pa rgyal mtshan/ zhwa lu pa legs pa rgyal mtshan/ rgyud smad pa shes rab bzang po/ mkhas grub
nyi ma bkra shis/ mkhas pa bde legs nyi ma/ sgom sde shar pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ byang ma khang gsar ba dpal 'byor bsod nams lhun grub/ zhang ston phrin las lhun grub/
'khon ston dpal 'byor lhun grub/ zur dpal 'byor phrin las rab rgyas/ lnga pa chen po ngag dbang blo bzang rgya mtsho/ skyid shod sprul sku ngag dbang bstan 'dzin phrin
las/ khri chen blo gros rgya mtsho/ khri chen blo bzang mkhas btsun/ khri chen ngag dbang chos grags/ rje yon tan dar rgyas/ rje bzod pa bzang po/ khri chen ngag dbang
mchog ldan/ bder 'byor ngag dbang don grub/ lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje/ dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po/ sde khri 'jam dbyangs nyi ma/ grag dgon dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas/
rdo rje 'chang 'jam dbang mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ thub bstan legs bshad bzang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ dmar shAkya
grub pa nas/ bla ma grags pa dpal/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal/ shangs kun mkhyen shes rab/ mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang / rje bzang po rgyal

mtshan/ rje ngag dbang blo gros/ dmar tshul khrims rin chen/ dge 'dun bkra shis/ lha btsun bsod nams dpal bzang / sgom sde shar pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan man 'dra'o// //'jigs
bral rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan biRWa pas bla ma sa chen la dngos su stsal ba'i pha rgyud rdo rje'i rigs rdo rje rnam par 'joms pa bla med ltar bkral ba lha
bdun cu rtsa lnga'i dkyil 'khor du bsod nams rtse mo'i dbang chu dang / nam mkha' dpal bzang gi byin rlabs gnyis kyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ biRWa pa/ sa skya'i gong ma rnam lnga/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen
shes rab rdo rje/ chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ rnam rgyal rin chen/ shAkya kun dga'/ ye shes dbang
po/ dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ bsod nams mchog ldan/ gong dkar phrin las rnam rgyal/ byams pa bstan pa rgya 'tsho/ khri zur bkra shis don grub/ rje phun tshogs rnam rgyal/
bla ma dkon mchog sbyin pa/ gong dkar mkhan chen bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //mi g.yo bla med kyi rgyud
la brten nas slob dpon klu sgrub zhabs kyis bkral ba'i khro rgyal mi g.yo ba lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du jo nang sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / khro bo mi g.yo ba/ slob dpon nA gardzu na/ grub chen sha ba ri

dbang phyug slob dpon blu'i byang chub/ shAkya srung ba/ chos kyi grags pa/ rin chen bzang po/ rin chen 'byung gnas/ grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ ye shes rgya mtsho/
nyi ma seng ge sangs rgyas srung ba/ shAkya seng ge rgyal mtshan/ paNDi ta nags kyi rin chen/ kun mkhyen rong ston shAkya rgyal mtshan/ rje blo gros chos skyong / paN

rgyal/ de'i dbon ngag dbang phrin las/ grub dbang kun mkhyen dbang po/ rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bu/ si tu chos kyi 'byung gnas/ lo chen tshe dbang kun khyab/ karma nges
don bstan 'dzin/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med/ karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //slob dpon wa la tsandras
bkral zhing ras chung rdo rje grags kyis bod du spyan drangs pa dpal phyag na rdo rje gtum po lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du karma pa dbang phyug rdo rje'i yig steng nas dbang

pakshi/ gnyan ras sogs kar lugs don brgyud ltar la/ karma pa dbang phyug rdo rje man gong ltar byas kyang chog par gsungs so// //gnyis pa gdul bya zhe sdang can gtso bor
rjes su gzung ba'i don du gsungs pa rnam snang gi rigs su gtogs pa dpal gshin rje'i gshed kyi skor la dmar nag gnyis las/ dang po la gshin rje'i gshed dmar po'i rgyud le'u

/ 'jam dpal gshin rje'i gshed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen biRWa pa/ Dombi he ru ka pI rA Ti pa/ ma taM garbha/ gombI ra ma ti/ rdo rje gdan pa mya ngan med

pa/ padma badzra/ dI paM ka ra/ rwa rdo rje grags man gong ltar ro// //gnyis pa gdong drug gi rgyud sdom pa gsum pa la brten nas grub chen nag po pa sogs kyis bkral ba'i

badzra/ bal po me dza gling pa'am thugs rje chen po/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rong pa rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/
de'i sras rong pa shes rab seng ge bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang nam mkha'i mtshan can/ chos rje rin chen dpal
grub/ rin chen mkhyen rab mchog grub/ rje rig 'dzin rgyal po/ rje chos rig rgyal mtshan/ dgon stod pa bsod nams dpal 'byor/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/
chos rje rdo rje bzang

po/ lha bo pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ chen po chos dbang rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byams pa mkhas btsun/ byang gling bla chen rin chen brtson 'grus/
mtshungs med 'jam dpal chos dar/ byang gling bla chen smon lam bsam gtan/ byang gling grub dbang ye shes dpal 'byor/ zhwa lu mchog sprul blo gsal bstan skyong / 'jam
dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /jo nang gshin rams ltar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra
shis rgyal mtshan yan gong ltar la/ de nas/ nam mkha' dpal bzang / nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ nyi gling pa tshul khrims bkra shis/ bka' 'gyur ba
rin chen rgya mtsho/ gong dkar ba kun dga' bsam 'grub/ kun dga' dar rgyas/ kun dga' chos 'phel/ be lo karma tshe dbang kun khyab/ sprul sku karma rin chen/ bla ma 'od gsal
'gyur med/ rje karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o// //gsum pa ni/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud rtogs bdun la gtso bor brten nas grub chen la li ta badzra
dang / don yod rdo rjes bkral zhing / gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir rwa skyo zhang gsum gyi bka' srol las/ dang po rwa lugs 'jigs byed lha dgu ma'i dkyil 'khor du rje ngag
dbang legs grub kyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje 'jigs byed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen la li ta badzra/
paNDi ta a mo gha badzra/ dznyA na ka ra gupta/ grub chen padma badzra/ dI paM ka ra rakShi ta/ rwa lo rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes

seng ge rwa 'bum seng / klog skya pa dbang phyug grags/ ldong ston shes rab dpal/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/
chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen byang chub dpal bzang / shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge paN chen grags pa rgyal mtshan/ glo
bo mkhan chen bsod nams kyi lhun grub/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge buddha singha/ brang ti paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / dpal ldan don grub/ de gnyis kas shar chen kun
dga' bkra shis/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ rje bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ thar rtse nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ ngor mkhan 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog
grags pa/ de'i dbon phun tshogs don grub/ grub dbang sprul sku kun dga' bsod nams/ thar rtse mkhan chen nam mkha' 'chi med/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ rje 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag gam/ yang na/ kun dga' bstan 'dzin nas/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ khu na 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo
gter la'o/ /yang na/ glo bo mkhan chen nas/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ shes rab 'byung gnas/
dam chos bsam 'grub/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bstan 'dzin lhun grub man 'dra/ yang na/ sa lo nas/ gnyen chen grags pa blo gros/ chos rje shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar paN
nam dpal man 'dra/ yang na/ nam mkha'

dpal bzang las/ shar chen dang nam mkha' sangs rgyas gnyis/ gnyis ka las rje dam chos pas so/ /yang na/ snga ma gnyis las gzar chen pas/ de las dam chos pas so/ /yang na/ rwa
'bum seng nas/ rong pa rgwa lo/ rong pa sher seng / rong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bu ston/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ ngor chen man 'dra/ yang
na/ rong pa sher seng nas/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal/ bla ma dge ba rgyal mtshan/ bla ma shes rab zla dbang
/ sngags 'chang rin chen rnam rgyal/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ lha mchog seng ge man 'dra/ yang na/ nam mkha' dpal bzang nas/ brang ti nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ hor
nam mkha' dpal bzang / sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ dpal ldan chos skyong / de'i dbon rin chen mchog grub/ dpal ldan rin chen chos mdzod/ thar rtse nam
mkha' bsam 'grub man 'dra/ yang jo nang gshin rab ltar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rwa 'bum seng yan gong ltar la/ de nas rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ gru gu mkhar sngon pa
rin chen rgyal mtshan/ rwa chos dbyings/ brtson 'grus seng ge chos kyi bkra shis/ shes rab seng ge rwa kun dga' seng ge rwa chos kyi seng ge rwa 'jam dbyangs blo gros/ rwa
blo gros rgya mtsho/ rwa tshul khrims rnam rgyal/ rwa don grub legs pa/ rwa jo nang rje btsun kun dga' snying po/ des snying po mtha' yas/ ye shes rgya mtsho/ rin chen
rgya mtsho gsum/ gsum gas kun bzang dbang po/ de nas rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bu/ si tu chos kyi 'byung gnas sam bstan pa'i nyin

byed/ tshe dbang kun khyab/ karma rin chen/ 'od gsal 'gyur med/ yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na/ rwa 'bum seng nas/ ldong ston shes rab dpal/ bla ma chos kyi rgyal
po/ gzhi thog pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ snar thang pa bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ snar thang pa tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs ral gri/ blo brtan bzhi pa/
shAkya mchog ldan/ byams gling pa dpal ldan tshul khrims/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog /rdo ring dbon kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen lung rig rgya mtsho/ rje btsun
tA ra nA tha/ rin chen rgya mtsho/ kun bzang dbang po man gong ltar ro// //grub chen la li tas bkral ba'i dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lugs lha bcu gsum ma'i dkyil 'khor du
kun blo'i sgrub dkyil dang / zhu chen mtshams sbyor sogs kyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'jigs byed/ rdo rje ro langs ma/ grub chen
la li ta badzra/ grub chen rdo rje gdan pa a mo gha badzra/ paN grub ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ grub chen padma badzra/ bal po bha ro phyag sdum/ rwa chen lo tsA ba rdo

pa kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma/ rdo rje 'chang tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug

ldan bkra shis/ kun

rdo rje 'chang dbang phyug rab brtan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ sngags 'chang dbang drag rdo rje/ dus 'khor ba 'jam dpal bzang po/ bla chen byams pa smon lam
bsam gtan/ byang gling pa ye shes dpal 'byor/ dge slong bkra shis dpal 'byor/ brag sgom zhabs drung dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas/ zhwa lu blo gsal bstan skyong ngam dpal
ldan tshul khrims/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ rje btsun rgwa lo nas/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ dga'
ldan pa kun dga' bsod nams/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge man gong ltar ro// //rje rin po che blo bzang grags pa dpal gyi nye brgyud/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa bdud
las rnam rgyal gyi dkyil 'khor du rje rin po che'i sgrub thabs dang / skal bzang rgya mtsho'i dkyil chog gi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal
rdo rje 'jigs byed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ grub chen la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ grub chen padma badzra/ mar me mdzod srung ba/
rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rong pa rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ rong pa shes rab seng ge

lam 'bras pa ye shes dpal ba/ rje bsod nams lhun grub/ chos rje don grub rin chen/ rje tsong kha pa blo bzang grags pa/ mkhas grub dge legs dpal bzang / zhwa lu pa legs pa
rgyal mtshan/ gnyis kas rje shes rab seng ge 'dul 'dzin dpal ldan bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs dge 'dun 'phel/ rgyud chen bkra shis 'phags/ paN chen bsam 'grub rgya mtsho/ rgyud
chen brtson 'grus 'phags/ rgyud chen rdo rje bzang po/ rgyud chen sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ sangs rgyas bkra shis/ ngag dbang blo
bzang / khri chen blo gros rgya mtsho/ 'jam bzhad ngag dbang brtson 'grus/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas rdo rje/ dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po/ skal bzang dngos grub/ rtse thang
mkhan zur thu med ngag dbang shes rab/ lha btsun ye shes don grub rgyal mtshan/ rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /nye brgyud
ni/ dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed/ 'jam dbyangs brtan pa'i 'khor lo/ rgyal ba 'jam dpal snying po'am/ yang na/ rje btsun 'jam dpal dbyangs dang / rdo rje 'jigs byed so so nas/
dbu ma pa dpa' bo rdo rje/ gsum gas chos kyi rgyal po blo bzang grags pa/ de nas ba so chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ grub chen chos kyi rdo rje/ rgyal ba blo bzang don grub/
mkhas grub sangs rgyas ye shes/ paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan man 'dra'o// //gsum pa gdul bya gti mug can gtso bor rjes su gzung ba'i don du gsungs pa dpal rnam snang sgyu
'phrul drwa ba'i skor la/ slob dpon sgeg pa'i rdo rjes 'jam dpal mtshan

brjod bla med ltar bkral ba'i 'jam dpal gsang ldan rigs bsdus pa lha lnga bcu rtsa gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du rje ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho'i sgrub dkyil dang / mtshams sbyor
gyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal ye shes sems dpa'/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ sgeg pa'i
rdo rje/ nyi ma seng ge las kyi rdo rje/ mu drar shAkya siddhi/ lha'i dbang phyug gam lha'i dngos grub/ shAntiM garbha/ paNDi ta smr-i ti dznyA na kIrti/ de gnyis kas
nyi ma'i dngos grub/ lo tsA ba ye shes bla ma/ ngag gi dbang phyug /pu hrang pa shes rab rdo rje/ gnyis kas rngog chos sku rdo rje/ rngog zhe sdang rdo rje/ rngog kun dga'
rdo rje/ rngog gzi brjid grags pa/ des dar ma rgyal po/ dum bu kha pa/ bzang po pa gsum/ gsum gas rngog rin chen bzang po/ de nas rngog chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rngog don
grub dpal bzang / rngog byang chub bzang po/ khrus khang lo tsA ba bsod nams rgya mtsho/ zhwa dmar bzhi pa spyan snga chos kyi grags pa/ mkhan chen shes rab dpal/ 'bri
gung rin chen phun tshogs/ drung rin chen dpal/ chos rgyal phun tshogs/ bkra shis phun tshogs/ chos kyi grags pa/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog phrin las bzang po/ don
grub chos rgyal/ si tu chos 'byung / tshe dbang kun khyab/ dbon sprul karma rin chen/ 'od gsal 'gyur med/ rdo rje 'chang karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo
gter la'am/ yang na/ thub dbang / 'jam dbyangs/ sha ba ri pa/ mai tri pa/ mar pa lo tsA ba/ rngog chos sku rdo rje man gong ltar ro/ /gnas mdo'i

brgyud pa ltar na/ bkra shis phun tshogs yan gong ltar la/ de nas rje dkon mchog rin chen/ lho dkon mchog phrin las rnam rgyal/ grub thob karma chags med/ padma kun dga'/ phrin
las dbang 'byung / shes rab grags pa/ thub bstan rab 'phel/ pad dbang sprul sku bstan 'dzin don grub/ karma theg mchog nges don bstan 'phel/ zla bzang karma nges don
bstan pa rab rgyas/ karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ /jo nang brgyud pa ltar na/ rngog zhe sdang rdo rje yan gong ltar la/ de nas rtsang ston chos kyi
rgyal mtshan/ des dar ma rgyal po/ dum bu kha pa/ bzang po pa gsum/ gsum gas rngog rin chen bzang po/ rngog sangs rgyas yon tan/ rngog byang chub dpal ba/ rngog byang chub
dpal grub/ rngog blo gros dpal bzang / rje ye shes rdo rje/ chos sku lha dbang grags pa/ rje btsun tA ra nA tha/ rin chen rgya mtsho/ ye shes rgya mtsho/ tshe dbang nor
bu/ bka' brgyud phrin las shing rta/ nges don bstan 'dzin/ tshe dbang kun khyab/ karma rin chen/ 'od gsal 'gyur med/ rdo rje 'chang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des so/ /yang na/
tA ra nA tha yan gong ltar la/ de man chad dgra nag jo lugs ltar ro// //gnyis pa shes rab gtso bor ston pa ma'i rgyud kyi skor la ma rgyud spyi dang bye brag gnyis las/
dang po sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor gyi rgyud la brten nas slob dpon dri med grags pa dang / grub chen ku ku rA dza sogs kyis ma rgyud spyi dang mthun par bkral ba'i dpal sangs
rgyas thams cad mnyam par sbyor ba he ru ka gtso bor bzhugs pa'i/ rnam snang rgyal ba rtag pa/ rin 'byung rdo rje nyi ma/

'od dpag med padma gar dbang / don yod grub pa rdo rje rta mchog /rdo rje 'chang ngam rdo rje sems dpa' ste rigs drug phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa lha brgya dang nyi shu rtsa bdun
ma'i dkyil 'khor chen por rje kun blo'i sgrub dkyil dang / nam mkha' 'od zer dang / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i zin bris sbyar ba'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba chen po kun bzang rdo rje 'chang / rgyal ba rigs lnga/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/ yangs pa can gyi li tsa bi dri ma med par
grags pa/ rgyal po dzaH'am rab gsal zla ba'am indra bhU ti che ba/ de'i sras rgyal po u pa rA dza'am rgyal bu sgra gcan 'dzin/ grub chen ku ku rA dza/ mukti ta nyi zla
rdo rje/ ba hu ta mukti/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra'am/ ku ku rA dza nas/ mukti ko Sha/ M ga so ma badzra/ ba hu ta/ mu sto ba hu ra/ gu sko
ta/ bi ma mi tra zhes kyang snang / gang ltar yang de nas rma A tsaRYa rin chen mchog des gye re mchog skyong dang / gtsug ru rin chen gzhon nu gnyis/ gnyis kas 'og go bo'ang
'dug 'om tshul khrims byang chub/ des cog ro rgyal ba'i yon tan dang / la sum gzhon nu mchog dang / stag rtse rdo rje 'jam dpal gsum/ gsum gas khu byang chub 'od/ de
nas bla ma blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rong paN rin chen tshul khrims/ rong ston ma hA paNDi ta chos kyi bzang po/ yam shud blo chen bzang po/ 'gos zla ba 'bar/ 'gos zla ba
'bum grags/ 'gos dngos grub rgyal mtshan/ 'gos dge slong chos kyi rdo rje/ 'gos dngos grub mgon/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ dge sding pa chos sku 'od zer/ yu mo mi bskyod
rdo rje/ byang chen bsod nams 'phel/ bag

ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ lam 'bras pa bla chen bsod nams dpal/ grub chen 'jam dbyangs kun dga' blo gros/ chos rje nam mkha' tshul khrims/
rong po blo bzang ba/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ chos 'khor thar pa gling gi bla chen slob dpon sanggA shrI/ slob dpon tshul khrims 'od dpal bzang yang snang / zer/ slob dpon
bsod nams dpal 'byor/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ grub dbang shAkya seng ge rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ bla chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen
byams pa mkhas btsun/ rin chen 'jam dpal chos mchog mkhas dbang rin chen don grub/ chos rje rin chen blo gsal lam ye shes bkra shis/ chos rje ye shes dpal 'byor/ zhwa lu
blo gsal bstan skyong / 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ bi ma mi tra nas/ rma A tsaRYa rin chen mchog
/des gnyags dznyA na ku mA ra/ de gnyis kas khyung po dbyig 'od/ cog ro rgyal 'bum/ dam pa khu gro dpal gzhon/ de gsum gas cog ro rgyal ba'i yon tan/ de bzhi gas yon
tan bzang po/ de nas cog ro byang chub 'byung gnas/ za rigs 'phags pa/ rmugs byang chub snying po/ dmar sgom yon tan tshul khrims/ lce bsod nams bzang po/ de gnyis kas mgar
ston tshul khrims bzang po/ de nas yam shud blo chen bzang po man gong ltar ro// //dpal sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam par sbyor ba'i rgyud la brten nas grub chen ku ku ri
pas bkral ba'i dpal mnyam sbyor rdo rje sems dpa' bde ba chen po

gtso bor bzhugs pa'i gzhi'i dkyil 'khor gcig gi nang du dkyil 'khor chen po dgu bzhugs pa'i lha nyis brgya bco brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor chen por jo nang gi steng nas dbang bzhi
rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan yan mnyam sbyor gong ma ltar la/ de nas ngag gi dbang phyug byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon
blo/ ngor chen kun bzang / dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ byams gling paN chen bsod nams rnam rgyal/ rdor gdan kun dga' rnam rgyal/ thugs sras kun dga' rgyal po/ sngags
'chang tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug rje dbang phyug rab brtan/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ 'bras bu
gling pa ngag dbang o rgyan/ gter chen rig 'dzin 'gyur med rdo rje/ rgyal sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ 'gyur med padma bstan 'dzin/ o rgyan bstan 'dzin rdo rje/ 'gyur med
phrin las rnam rgyal/ 'gyur med padma dbang rgyal/ rdzogs sprul bzhi pa mi 'gyur nam mkha'i rdo rje'am 'jigs med mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug thub bstan legs bshad bzang po/
des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan yan mnyam sbyor snga ma ltar la/ de nas tshar chen man 'di'i gong ltar ro/ /yang gsar brgyud
ltar na/ rdor 'chang / phyag rdor/ dznyA na DA ki nI/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ 'gro bzang snying po/ kha che rin chen rdo rje/ te dza de wa/ zangs dkar lo tsA
ba 'phags pa shes rab/ gnyan tshul khrims 'bar/ 'gos rin chen bzang po/ gzhon nu seng ge dbang phyug rin chen/ shAkya rdo rje/ chos kyi grags pa/ dbus pa sangs 'bum/ lo tsA
mchog ldan/

bag ston gzhon tshul/ bla ma tshul rgyam/ ngag gi dbang phyug man gong ltar ro// //gnyis pa bye brag gi rigs la/ he ru ka rnam snang / rdo rje nyi ma/ padma gar dbang / rta
mchog rdo rje sems dpa' ste drug las/ dang po he ru ka'i rigs gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud la/ bde mchog sangs rgyas thod pa/ mu hA mA yA/ a ralli ste bzhi las/ dang po ni/
rgyud gzhan gyi lugs la sprul pa'i sku rnams da lta mi yul na dngos su mi bzhugs shing / bde mchog gi lugs la sprul pa'i sku rnams da lta yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi na dngos su
bzhugs pas byin rlabs gzhan las myur ba'i phyir/ byin rlabs gzhan las khyad par du 'phags pa'i bde mchog rtsa ba'i rgyud le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa dang / bshad rgyud/
sdom 'byung / rdo rje mkha' 'gro/ kun spyod/ kha sbyor/ nges brjod bla ma rnams la brten nas grub chen so sos bkral ba'i 'khor lo bde mchog gi bka' srol sum cu rtsa gnyis
tsam yod par grags shing / bod 'dir yang ci rigs pa dar pa las gtso bor lU nag dril gsum ste/ de la dang po grub pa'i slob dpon chen po lU hi pas rtsa rgyud dang rnal 'byor
ma kun spyod kyi rgyud dag la brten nas sbyang gzhi sgong skyes sbyong byed du bkral ba dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lha drug cu rtsa gnyis pa'i dkyil 'khor chen por rje ngag
dbang legs grub kyi sgrub dkyil dang / shar chen kun dga' bkra shis kyi mtshams sbyor steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa la bka' babs dgu las/dang po
sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang chen he ru ka dpal phyag na rdo rje/ bram ze sa ra ha pa/ 'phags pa klu sgrub/ grub chen sha ba ri pa dbang phyug

slob dpon lU hi pa/ slob dpon dA ri ka pa/ des rdo rje dril bu pa dang / rnam rgyal zhabs gnyis/ gnyis kas rus sbal zhabs/ de nas shrI dzA landha ri ba/ grub chen nag po pa
spyod pa'i rdo rje/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ bal po pham mthing pa gcen 'jigs med grags pa/ gcung ngag gi dbang phyug klog skya shes rab brtsegs/
mal lo blo gros grags pa/ sa chen/ rje btsun sku mched/ chos rje khu dbon/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bla ma dam pa/ ri khrod pa blo gros brtan pa/ de
gnyis kas bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ de nas shar chen ye rgyal/ ngor chen kun bzang / mus chen dkon rgyam/ des kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge dang / grub chen dkon mchog
blo gros gnyis/ de gsum gas mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ des 'jam dbyangs sa lo/ de gnyis kas ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ des shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/
thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang / des sgrub khang dpal ldan don grub/ de gnyis kas nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ des shes rab 'byung gnas/ phyi ma gnyis kas dam chos bsam 'grub/
de nas mkhan chen sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bkra shis lhun grub/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas ye shes/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ zhal dkar ba ngag
dbang shes rab/ chos rje rin chen grags pa/ rje dpal ldan grags pa/ mus chen bsod nams dbang phyug sa skya pa 'jam mgon kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'am/ yang na/ kun dga' bstan 'dzin nas/ smra ba'i dbang phyug shes rab

rgya mtsho/ mkhan rin po che dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ des so/ /yang na/ chos rgyal 'phags pa yan gong ltar la/ de nas 'u yug pa bsod nams seng ge dbus pa sangs rgyas
'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ des bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang / khyung lhas pa gzhon nu bsod
nams gnyis/ gnyis kas shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ yang na/ sa paN nas/ dmar chos kyi rgyal po/ mi nyag chos kyi rgyal po/ mi nyag rdo rje grags pa/ lce mdo
sde seng ge bla ma ston shAka lce btsun blo ldan/ kun mkhyen 'phags pa 'od zer/ bu ston man 'dra/ yang na/ sa paN nas/ bo dong rin chen rtse mo/ khro phu bsod nams seng
ge bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston man 'dra/ yang na/ sa paN nas/ bo dong rin chen rtse mo/ nyan chen bsod nams brtan pa/ bla ma dam pa man 'dra/ yang na/ dkon mchog lhun
grub nas/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ de'i dbon shes rab 'byung gnas man 'dra/ yang na/ sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ sangs rgyas seng ge thar paN/
nam mkha' sangs rgyas man 'dra'o/ /gnyis pa mar do lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ lU hi pa/ DheM gi pa/ paN grub dbang po lwa ba pa/
rgyal po indra bhU ti/ ka tsa Ta pa/ grub chen dril bu pa/ dzA landha ri pa/ nag po spyod pa/ ku sha la nwa tha/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ man ka shrI dznyA na/ bal po bha danta/
lo tsA ba mar pa do pa chos kyi dbang phyug gze pa blo ldan seng ge gze pa jo bde/ slob dpon khu pa/ khams pa lho tshad kun dga' rin chen/ lo tsA ba

mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ khyung lhas pa/ shar chen/ ngor chen/ mus chen/ sangs rgyas rin chen/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ sangs rgyas seng ge
des thar rtse pa dang mus pa nam mkha' dpal bzang gnyis/ gnyis kas sgrub khang pa dpal don man gong sa lugs ltar ro/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/
grub chen lwa ba pa/ la ki mi pa/ 'bar ba'i gtso bo/ dge ba'i gtso bo/ ku sha la nA tha man gong dang 'dra/ yang na/ khyung lhas pa nas/ chos rje bkra shis rin chen/ ngor
chen man 'dra/ yang na/ gze pa blo ldan nas/ gze pa don grub ye shes/ sa phug pa shAkya rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan man 'dra'o/ /gsum pa jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ lU hi pa/ dA ri ka pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ ratna a ka ra shAnti/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha rong pa mgar dge lha rje stod pa tshul khrims
dpal/ steng pa thugs rje zla gsal/ shod nyi ma mkha' 'gro/ gcen shes rab rgyal po/ gcung shes rab gtsug tor/ lha rje chen po dharma tsakra/ thar ston pa chos kyi 'od
zer/ zhang grags pa dpal/ bla ma sgom pa ye shes/ bla ma grags chen/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston man mar do lugs dang 'dra'o/ /bzhi pa kha che paN chen lugs kyi
brgyud pa ni/ tsakra samba ra/ badzra wA rA hI/ lU hi pa/ sha ba ri pa/ kanta pa/ 'dren mdzad zhabs/ bi khyA ta de wa/ kha che paN chen shAkya shrI/ bi bhU ti tsandra/
g.yag sde lo tsA ba puNye bha dra/ mnga' ris ze dmar ba buddha dznyA na/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor
chen man gong mar do

lugs dang 'dra/ yang na/ kha che paN chen nas/ spyi bo lhas pa seng ge dpal/ zhang phya ru pa/ 'bro lung pa/ khro phu lo tsA ba/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston man 'dra/
yang na/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ dril bu pa/ dA ri ka pa/ dga' ba'i rdo rje/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ a bhA ya de wa pUrNa/ kha che paN chen man 'dra/ yang
na nye brgyud ni/ 'khor lo sdom pa nas/ paN chen shAkya shrI man 'dra'o/ /lnga pa pu rong lo chung lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ lU hi pa/ DheM
gi pa/ dA ri ka pa/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ dzA landha ri pa/ nag po spyod pa/ dge ba'i mgon po/ rus sbal zhabs/ gu hya pa/ bhu ba ri pa'ang snang / rnam rgyal zhabs/ tilli
pa'ang 'dug tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ ma na ka shrI/ pradznyA rakShi ta/ pham mthing ba gsum/ bha danta/ pu rong lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ mnga'
ris stod pa dkon mchog 'bar/ thur la ba tshul khrims skyabs/ thang spe ba 'phags pa skyabs/ gser lding pa gzhon nu 'od/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya
mtsho/ bu ston rin po che/ khyung lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po man mar do lugs bzhin no/ /yang na/ dmar chos
kyi rgyal mtshan nas/ mi nyag chos rgyal/ mi nyag rdor grags/ lce mdo seng / bla ma ston shAka blo ldan seng ge 'phags 'od man 'dra/ yang na/ ma na ka shrI dang pradznyA
rakShi ta gnyis las ka na ka shrI/ de dang pham mthing pa gnyis kas bha danta/ de nas pu rong lo chung man 'dra'o/ /drug pa dmar lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ pham

mthing pa yan gong sa lugs ltar la/ de nas bal po bha danta/ lo chung grags 'byor shes rab/ dmar chen po chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ dbon po shes rab rdo rje/ dmar thub pa shes
rab/ dmar brtson 'grus rdo rje/ dmar chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma shAkya gzhon nu/ lce blo ldan seng ge kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston man pu rong lugs dang 'dra'o/ /bdun
pa dpyal lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ lU hi pa/ rgyal po dA ri ka pa/ mnga' bdag mai tri pa/ nya ka pa/ karNa pa/ ghandha pa/ bi khyA ta de
wa/ paN chen shAkya shrI/ rdo rje gdan pa/ paNDi ta kShi ti garbha/ dpyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po/ rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ de sras rong pa shes rab seng ge grum chos
skyong dpal/ khyung po lhas pa/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po man pu rong lugs dang 'dra'o/ /brgyad pa sba spang sna ba'i lugs kyi brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ slob dpon chen po tsandri ka pa/ bram ze chen po me ko pa/ lU hi pa/ dA ri ka pa/ bram ze sdom pa bzang po/ jo bo rje a ti sha
des lo chen rin chen bzang po dang / nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba gnyis/ gnyis kas 'phan yul 'am pa ston mgon dang / 'am pa jo btsun gnyis/ de gnyis kas sgom
pa mang sgom dang / sba spang sna pa sku mched gnyis/ de nas me rag pa dar ma byang chub/ de'i dbon rin chen rgyal po/ bla ma don ri pa grags pa dpal/ bla ma 'phags 'od man
gong lo chung lugs ltar ro/ /dgu pa gnyos lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ kahNa pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ de wa rakShi
ta/ nag po lha la dad pa/ pham mthing pa

sku mched/ de gsum gas bal po bha danta/ su ma ti kIrti/ de gnyis kas gnyos lo tsA ba/ de nas gnyos bla ma/ gnyos dpal le/ phug ka ba jo bo 'bum/ gtsang pa lha steng pa/ lce
mdo sde seng ge bla ma ston pa shAkya/ bla ma blo ldan/ bla ma 'phags 'od man gong lo chung lugs ltar ro/ /yang bde mchog rab 'byams ltar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen
kun dga' bzang po yan gong sa lugs brgyud pa ltar la/ de nas rin chen bkra shis/ shAkya mchog ldan/ brag dkar sems dpa'/ bkra shis rnam rgyal/ kun dga' grol mchog rdo
ring pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun tA ra nA thas/ rin chen rdo rje ma/ rin chen rgya mtsho gnyis/ gnyis kas ye shes rgya mtsho/ snying po mtha' yas/ de nas kun bzang
dbang po/ dge legs bkra shis/ dpa' bo gtsug lag dga' ba'i dbang po/ lo chen tshe dbang kun khyab/ karma ratna/ 'od gsal 'gyur med/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang yon tan rgya
mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //grub chen nag po spyod pas rtsa rgyud kyi zab don sbyang gzhi mngal skyes sbyong byed du bkral ba'i bde mchog lha drug cu rtsa gnyis
kyi dkyil 'khor du ngag dbang legs grub kyi sgrub dkyil dang / sangs phun gyi mtshams sbyor steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin
chen yan gong lU hi pa'i sa lugs brgyud pa ltar la/ de nas rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge rje sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / de'i dbon nam mkha' sangs
rgyas/ mtshungs med dam chos bsam 'grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ sngags 'chang kun dga'

bkra shis/ yab rje bsod nams rin chen/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des
bdag blo gter la'am/ yang na/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin nas/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ dpal ldan blo gros rgya mtshan/ des so/ /yang na/ sangs rgyas rin chen
nas/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra'o/ /yang na/ dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ kun dga'
bkra shis/ shes rab 'byung gnas/ dam chos bsam 'grub man 'dra/ yang na/ chos rje khu dbon nas/ stag ston shes rab gzhon nu/ bla ma brag dkar ba/ mkhas grub gzhon nu bsod
nams/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ des kha char ba bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang / gzhon nu seng ge gnyis/ gnyis kas sangs rgyas dpal grub/
de nas lha mchog seng ge man 'dra/ yang na/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen nas/ dge legs bshes gnyen/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ thar rtse nam mkha' dpal bzang
/ dpal ldan don grub/ nam mkha' sangs rgyas man 'dra'o/ /yang jo nang bde rams ltar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ he ru ka dpal/ yo gi nI/ spyod pa ba/ gu hya pa/ santa ra pa/
tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa sku mched/ mal lo/ sa skya pa brtse chen/ bsod nams rtse mo/ grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa paN/ yon tan dpal/ la ru pa/ gangs khrod pa/
theg chen chos rgyal/ gang dgon pa/ shAka mchog man gong lU hi pa'i bde rams ltar ro/ /yang na/ sa paN

nas/ chos 'phags/ mang mkhar lo tsA ba/ dpal ldan seng ge/ bu ston/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ byang chub seng ge/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun
dga' bzang po/ rin chen bkra shis/ shAkya mchog ldan man 'dra'o// //grub pa'i slob dpon chen po rdo rje dril bu pas bkral ba'i dpal 'khor lo bde mchog la phyi nang gnyis
las/ dang po phyi dkyil lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du kun blo'i sgrub dkyil dang / zhu chen gyi mtshams sbyor sogs kyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa la/
dang po sa lugs ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ 'bar ba 'dzin pa/ karNa pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ nA
ro pa/ pham mthing pa gcen 'jigs med grags pa/ gcung ngag gi dbang phyug/ klog skya shes rab brtsegs/ mal lo blo gros grags pa/ brtse chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon
bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa paN kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ des chos 'phags blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bo dong pa brtson 'grus rdo rje/ tshogs sgom pa
kun dga' dpal gsum/ gsum gas khro phu pa bsod nams seng ge yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ kun dga' rin chen/ rin chen
rgyal mtshan/ bsod nams bzang po/ gong dkar kun dga' rnam rgyal/ yon tan rgya mtsho/ shAkya kun dga'/ dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ tshul khrims bkra shis/ rin chen rgya mtsho/
gong dkar phrin las rnam rgyal/ blo gros dbang phyug theg chen gling pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ mus pa

bsod nams blo gros/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ mus chen bsod nams dpal bzang / mus chen chos nyid ye shes/ rje btsun ma 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma/ ngag dbang rdo rje rin chen/
rdo rje 'chang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'am/ yang na/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ kun mkhyen shes rab dpal bzang / mkhas grub smra ba'i nyi
ma dge legs dpal bzang / zhwa lu pa legs pa rgyal mtshan/ rgyal ba rin chen rgyal mtshan/ nyan po shAkya rgyal mtshan/ yon tan bshes gnyen/ chen po blo gros rnam rgyal/
shar pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ sgom sde pa shar chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ paN chen blo bzang chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ sngags chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ lcang skya sku
gong ma ngag dbang blo bzang chos ldan/ mkhas grub shes rab dar rgyas/ lcang skya 'og ma rol pa'i rdo rje/ dkon mchog 'jigs med dbang po/ des khri gung thang rin po che
dkon mchog bstan pa'i sgron me dang / dpal mang mkhan chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gnyis/ gnyis kas brag dgon dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang
po/ des so/ /mar do lugs ltar na/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ dril bu pa/ lwa ba pa/ dzA landha ra/ nag po spyod pa/ dge ba'i mgon po/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ ma
na ka shrI/ bal po pham mthing pa sku mched/ bal po bha danta/ mar pa do pa chos kyi dbang phyug gze pa blo ldan seng ge gze ba bde mchog rdo rje/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/
rong pa chos mgon/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ shes rab dpal bzang / dge legs dpal bzang man gong ltar ro/ /

pu rong lo chung lugs ltar na/ pham mthing pa sku mched nas/ pu rong lo tsA ba grags 'byor shes rab/ sa skya gong ma rnam lnga man 'dra'o/ /jo nang bde rams ltar na/ mar do
chos kyi dbang phyug yan gong mar do lugs ltar la/ de nas gze pa bde mchog rdo rje/ gze pa blo ldan seng ge lho tshad dbang phyug brtson 'grus/ chos rgyal 'phags pa blo
gros rgyal mtshan/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ grags chen pa grags pa seng ge 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ khyung lhas pa/ nor bzang / dka' bzhi pa/ rin chen rgyal mtshan/
mkhyen rab chos rje/ lha bo pa/ kun dga' don grub/ bsod nams dpal 'byor/ byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis/ rdo ring dbon kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ tA ra nA tha man lU
hi pa'i bde rams brgyud pa ltar ro// //gnyis pa grub pa'i slob dpon dril bu zhabs de nyid kyis dpal 'khor lo sdom pa rnal 'byor gsang mtha' ltar bkral ba'i nang zab mo
lus kyi dkyil 'khor du rje ngag dbang legs grub kyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa la bka' babs dang po sa lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ chos rgyal 'phags
pa yan dril bu phyi dkyil ltar la/ de nas zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ des bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang / blo gros brtan pa gnyis/
gnyis kas dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ sangs rgyas
seng ge brang ti paN chen/ lce btsun mchog legs rdo rje/ mkhyen rab bstan 'dzin bzang po/ byams pa ngag dbang

lhun grub/ 'jam mgon sangs rgyas phun tshogs sngags 'chang kun dga' bkra shis/ rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mus chen bsod nams dpal bzang / mus chen chos nyid ye shes/ zhi
dgon pa bsod nams dbang phyug sa skya pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag la'am/ yang na/ mus chen dkon mchog
rgyal mtshan yan gong ltar la/ de nas zhwa lu pa sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mnga' ris pa dpal ldan rgyal po/ chos rje bzang po dpal ba/ nam mkha' dbang phyug rje btsun
chos kyi dbang phyug mus pa sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ zhi dgon slob dpon bkra shis lhun grub/ byams pa sangs rgyas dpal bzang /
mus dga' ldan rtse'i byang 'dren pa bsod nams mchog ldan/ zhi dgon pa shes rab chos bzang / rje byams pa rab brtan/ mkhan sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mus bsod nams dpal bzang
/ mus chos nyid ye shes/ mus bsod nams dbang phyug sa skya pa ngag dbang kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen/ de gnyis kas khams ston ngag dbang bzang po/
'dren mchog ngag dbang legs grub/ des mthu chen 'jam dpal bstan 'dzina'adzin dang / rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po gnyis/ gnyis kas bdag blo gter

bzang po/ byams pa rab brtan bzang po/ bla ma sangs rgyas dpal bzang /

mtshungs med 'jam mgon chos mchog rdor 'dzin rin chen don grub/ chos rje rin chen skal bzang / ye shes dpal 'byor/ rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong / rje mkhyen brtse'i dbang
po/ des so/ /yang na/ sa paN nas/ bo dong brtson 'grus rdo rje/ khro phu bsod nams seng ge yang rtse rin chen seng ge bu ston rin chen grub/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal
mtshan/ rje blo bzang grags pa/ shar pa gnas brtan rin chen rgyal mtshan/ 'brom btsun sher 'byung blo gros sbas pa/ thon pa mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho/ rje btsun blo
bzang e wa~M/ rgyal khang rtse pa dpal 'byor rgya mtsho/ sgom sde shar chen nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ paN chen blo bzang chos rgyan/ sngags chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/
lcang skya blo bzang chos ldan/ des grub dbang blo bzang chos 'dzin dang / mkhas grub shes rab dar rgyas gnyis/ gnyis kas lcang skya rol pa'i rdo rje/ des dkon mchog 'jigs

brtse'i dbang po/ des so/ /kha che paN chen lugs ltar na/ badzra bha ra/ badzra wA rA hi/ badzra ghaNDa pa/ A dga' ba'i rdo rje/ nanda badzra/ a yan lag med pa'i rdo

lugs ltar na/

pham mthing pa sku mched nas/ pu rong lo chung / dmar chen po/ skyi ston dkon mchog 'bar/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ dpal ldan seng ge mkhan chen shes rab
rdo rje/ 'dzam gling paN chen/ don yod rdo rje/ grags pa rin chen/ nam mkha' tshul khrims/ chos kyi seng ge kun dga' gzhon nu/ 'jam dbyangs blo gros/ don grub legs pa/
tA ra nA tha man gong bde mchog lU hi pa'i jo lugs brgyud pa ltar ro/ /yang jo nang bde rams brgyud pa ltar na/ ngor chen nas/ mus chen/ shAkya mchog ldan/ brag dmar ba/
rab gsal zla ba mgon po/ grol mchog lha dbang grags pa/ tA ra nA tha man gong bde rams ltar ro/ /yang na nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje dril bu pa/ de wa purNa/
gsum gas kha che paN chen man 'dra'o// //grub chen mai tri pas rtsa brgyud kyi dgongs pa ltar bkral ba'i 'khor lo bde mchog lha bcu gsum ma'i dkyil 'khor du 'brug pa pad
dkar dang / rgyal dbang chos rje'i yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang / blo gros rin chen/ ri khrod pa dbang phyug /mnga'
bdag mai tri gupta/ ti phu gsang sngags sdong po'am dri med bshes gnyen/ ba reg lo tsA ba/ ras chung rdo rje grags pa/ rgyal ba lo ras/ sum pa ras pa/ gling ras padma rdo
rje/ gtsang pa rgya ras ye shes rdo rje/ dga' ldan bsod nams dar/ 'ging phu ba nges 'byung dar/ 'od zer rgya mtsho/ sangs rgyas ras pa/ skyes mchog smon lam dpal/ lung
mang po yon tan bzang po/ kun dga' dpal 'byor/ ngag dbang chos rgyal/ rnam rgyal bkra shis/ kun dga' grol mchog /brag stod lha dbang grags pa/ kun dga' snying po/

ye shes rgya mtsho/ blo gros rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang phrin las/ kun bzang dbang po/ tshe dbang nor bu/ bka' brgyud phrin las shing rta'am chos kyi snang ba/ rgya ye rdor sprul
sku nges don bstan 'dzin/ tshe dbang kun khyab/ karma rin chen/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med/ karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i

mtsho las thob pa tsam ma gtogs gong dang 'dra'o// //yang / 'brug lugs bde mchog lha bcu gsum ma gong mai tri lugs dang lha sngags gcig pas dbang bskur zur du ma dgos

dbang po/ kun dga' lhun grub/ mi pham chos kyi dbang phyug dge legs bzhad pa/ 'jam

mgon dgyes pa/ 'jam dpal dpa' bo/ 'brug pa gtsug lag chos kyi snang ba'i lha/ khyab bdag theg mchog rdo rje/ rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag
blo gter la'o// //grub dbang nA ro pas bde mchog rtsa ba'i rgyud la brten nas bkral ba'i dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du rgyal dbang mi bskyod rdo rje'i
sgrub dkyil dang / si tu'i mtshams sbyor gyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob ba'i brgyud pa ni/rdo rje 'chang / grub chen tai lo pa/ grub chen nA ro pa/ mar pa chos
kyi blo gros/ mi la bzhad pa'i rdo rje/ dwags po zla 'od gzhon nu/ karma zhwa nag sku phreng dang po rje dus gsum mkhyen pa chos kyi grags pa/ ras chen sangs rgyas grags
pa/ spom brag pa bsod nams rdo rje/ rje gnyis pa karma pakshi chos kyi bla ma/ gnyan ras pa dge 'dun 'bum/ rje gsum pa rang byung rdo rje/ g.yung ston rdo rje dpal/ rje
bzhi pa rol pa'i rdo rje/ zhwa dmar mkha' spyod dbang po/ rje lnga pa de bzhin gshegs pa/ ratna bha dra/ rje drug pa mthong ba don ldan/ ban sgar 'jam dpal bzang po/ rje
