dbang phyug rdo rje/ si tu chos kyi dbang phyug/ rje bcu pa chos dbyings rdo rje/ zhwa dmar ye shes snying po/ rje bcu gcig pa ye shes rdo rje/ zhwa dmar brgyad pa chos kyi
don grub/ rje bcu gnyis pa byang chub rdo rje/ si tu chos kyi 'byung gnas/ rje bcu gsum pa bdud 'dul rdo rje/ si tu padma nyin byed dbang po/ rje karma bcu bzhi pa theg
mchog rdo rje/ de gnyis kas

dbon sprul karma theg mchog gsum gas ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //rje nA ro ta pa'i man ngag yum bka' rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma lha lnga'i
dkyil 'khor du mthong ba don ldan gyi sgrub dkyil dang / si tu nyin byed dbang po'i dbang chog gi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang
/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa/ mi la/ dwags po bsod nams rin chen/ rje dus gsum mkhyen pa/ ras chen/ spom brag pa/ karma pakshi/ mkhas grub o rgyan pa rin chen dpal/ rang
byung rdo rje/ rgyal ba g.yung ston pa/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ rtogs ldan mkha' spyod dbang po'i bar chig brgyud dang / de nas de bzhin gshegs pa/ sog dbon rig pa'i ral gri
dang / sprul sku chos dpal ye shes gnyis/ gnyis kas mthong ba don ldan/ go shrI dpal 'byor don grub/ chos grags rgya mtsho/ bkra shis dpal 'byor/ mi bskyod rdo rje/ dkon
mchog yan lag dbang phyug rdo rje/ chos kyi dbang phyug/ chos dbyings rdo rje/ ye shes snying po/ ye shes rdo rje/ chos kyi don grub/ si tu bstan pa'i nyin byed/ rgyal dbang
bdud 'dul rdo rje/ padma nyin byed dbang po/ theg mchog nges don bstan 'phel/ 'jam mgon ngag gi dbang phyug yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //grub pa'i dbang
phyug chen po dpal ldan biRWa pas bde mchog rtsa ba'i rgyud la brten nas bkral ba'i rdo rje rnal 'byor ma lha so bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du jo nang sgrub thabs dang /
nag po'i dkyil chog gi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa la babs so gsum las/ dang po gong dkar lugs ni/ rje btsun ma/ a bhA ya/ legs pa'i bu/ sa manta
shrI/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye seng / rwa 'bum seng /

mkhan shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ brag thog pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ yon tan rgyal mtshan/ o rgyan rgyal po/ bsod nams rgyal po/ nyi ma gling pa tshul

rin chen blo gsal bstan skyong / rje bla ma mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des so// //byang chub sems dpa' phyag na rdo rjes bde mchog nyung ngu'i rgyud kyi stod nas shlau ka
bcu gcig la brten nas dus kyi 'khor lo dang mthun par bkral ba'i dpal 'khor lo sdom pa stod 'grel lugs lha drug cu rtsa gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du jo nang gi sgrub thabs dang
/ si tu'i dkyil chog gi steng nas dbang bdun gong ma gong chen bcas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ he ru ka dpal 'khor lo bde mchog rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ dpal phyag na rdo rje/

//'phags yul grub pa'i slob dpon rnams kyis bshad rgyud mngon brjod bla ma'i stod smad khog bsdebs nas bkral ba'i bde mchog khro bo rdo rje sems dpa' lha lnga bcu rtsa

phyag 'bum ltar la/ ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //grub chen sha ba rI dbang phyug dang / paNDi ta dza ya se nA sogs kyis rtsa brgyud dang mkha'
'gro rgya mtsho'i rtsa bshad sbyar nas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo dang mthun par bkral ba'i bde mchog mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho lha stong dang lnga brgya dang bzhi pa'i dkyil 'khor
chen por ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi sgrub thabs/ dkyil chog sngags phreng / mchod phreng / sangs phun gyi zur 'debs bcas pa'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ chos sku rdo rje 'chang / rgyal yum rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ byang sems blo gros rin chen/ grub chen sha ba rI dbang phyug mnga'
bdag mai tri gupta/ rgya gar phyag na rdo rje/ slob dpon ka ma la badzra/ paNDi ta dza ya se nA/ sum pa lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa paN
kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ bla ma skyob pa dpal bzang po/ rgyal tsha lung mang po chos kyi dbang phyug mang mkhar lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs blo/ snar thang pa bag ston

gzhon nu tshul khrims/ snar thang pa tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag dbang grags pa/ bla ma byang chub seng ge sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje
'chang kun dga' bzang po/ gung ru shes rab bzang po/ de gnyis kas kun mkhyen rab 'byams pa bsod nams seng ge byas 'gyur ba bsod nams seng ge mkhan chen dkon mchog tshul
khrims/ sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug byang gling pa rin chen bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / rin
chen dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam dbyangs dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ khams ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rdor 'chang bkra shis rgya mtsho/
mkhan chen sangs rgyas ye shes/ zhal dkar ba ngag dbang shes rab/ bla ma kun dga' phun tshogs/ dbu mdzad dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bzhi sde chos rje rin chen chos 'phel/
rong po bla ma ngag dbang bzang po/ sde dge grwa sgang bla ma wA gindra bha dra/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po dpon slob ngag dbang legs grub/ rje bla ma 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen
brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang chen/ phyag na rdo rje/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ dA byang chub sems dpa'/ slob dpon a
bha yA ka ra/ ratna rakShi ta/ dza ya se nA man gong ltar ram/ yang na/ badzra dha ra/ badzra pA Ni/ grub thob padma badzra che chung gnyis/ indra bhU ti/ lcam lakShmI ka
ra/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ badzra a sA nA/ a bha yA ka ra/ ratna shrI/ dza ya se nA man gong ltar ro/ /yang bde mchog rab 'byams ltar na/ sum pa lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan

nas/ bla ma mkhas pa rgya mtsho/ seng ge rgyal mtshan/ rgya kun mkhyen pa/ rdo rje dpal/ bla ma tshul khrims rin chen/ karma pa rang byung rdo rje/ 'brang bu bsod nams mgon
po/ yor pa ye shes dpal/ mtshur bu 'jam dbyangs chen mo/ slob dpon bla ma rgyal mtshan/ zhwa dmar chos kyi grags pa/ rje karma phrin las pa/ rje mi bskyod rdo rje/ zhwa
dmar dkon mchog 'bangs/ rgyal tshab grags pa don grub/ stag lung rnam rgyal bkra shis/ stag lung ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ stag lung bkra shis dpal grub/ mkhan chen karma nyi
ma/ yongs 'dzin karma skyes mchog zhwa dmar dpal chen chos kyi don grub/ si tu chos kyi 'byung gnas/ 'brug pa bka' brgyud phrin las shing rta/ sprul sku nges don bstan
'dzin/ karma tshe dbang kun khyab/ sprul sku karma rin chen/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med/ ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des so/ /yang na/ sa bzang gzhon nu blo gros nas/ seng
ge dpal/ paN chen byams gling pa bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog rje byams pa
lhun grub/ rje btsun tA ra nA tha/ stag lung bkra shis dpal grub man gong ltar ro// //bshad rgyud mngon brjod bla ma'i le'u sum cu rtsa drug pa las bstan pa'i yum bka'
rdo rje phag mo lha bcu bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du jo nang sgrub thabs dang / lU hi pa'i dkyil chog la bshad rgyud kyi 'dor len byas pa'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ bi rU pa/ go lennA tha/ sha ri pu tra/ grub chen kun blo/ dge ba rgyal mtshan/ blo gros dpal 'byor/ zal mo brag pa/
kun dga' grol mchog brag stod pa lha dbang grags pa/ tA ra nA tha man

gong lU hi pa'i bde rams brgyud pa ltar ro// //bshad rgyud mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho las bstan pa'i rdo rje rnal 'byor ma phag gdong chen mo lha so bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du jo
nang sgrub thabs dang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i dbang chog kha bsgyur ba'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gong gi bde mchog drag po phyag 'bum ltar
ro// //slob dpon zhi ba sbas pas phag mo'i rtogs pa dang rtsa bshad khog bsdebs nas bkral ba'i rdo rje phag mo 'byung ba lha nyer gcig ma'i dkyil 'khor du jo nang sgrub
thabs dang / nag po'i dkyil chog kha bsgyur ba'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen ye shes bshes
gnyen/ zhi ba sbas pa'am bde ba chen po'i rdo rje/ go bi pa/ nirpA Ni shrI tA ra nA tha man gong lU hi'i bde rams brgyud pa ltar ro// //grub pa'i slob dpon chen po padmA
ka ras khrag 'thung gal po che'i rgyud la brten nas bkral te 'khon klu dbang srung ba la stsal ba'i dpal sa skya pa'i yab chos yang dag he ru ka zla gam dgu pa'i dkyil 'khor

dpa'/ sprul sku dga' rab rdo rje/ slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ slob dpon ro langs bde ba/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba/ slob dpon chen po hU~M kar/ slob dpon padma
thod phreng rtsal/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra/ bal po shI la manydzu/ sna nams rdo rje bdud 'joms/ gnyags chen dznyA na ku mA ra/ 'khon klu dbang srung

pa/ 'khon ston rdo rje rin chen/ 'khon shes rab yon tan/ 'khon yon tan 'byung gnas/ 'khon tshul khrims rgyal po/ 'khon gtsug tor shes rab/ 'khon dge skyabs/ 'khon dge mthong
/ 'khon bal po/ 'khon shAkya blo gros/ 'khon shes rab tshul khrims/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ dpal sa skya pa brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon rin po che
bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/

ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ chos sgo ba shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ yar klung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ klu pa bsod nams dar/ dmar ston rgyal
mtshan 'od zer/ mkhas btsun nam mkha' blo gros/ chag lo gsum pa rin chen chos rgyal/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug /mkhan chen dbang phyug rab brtan/ a mes zhabs kun dga' bsod nams/ 'jam dpal rdo rje bsod nams dbang phyug zhwa lu rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ gong dkar phrin
las rnam rgyal/ sgyi chu mkhan po blo gros dbang phyug rnam grong pa chos dbang rgya mtsho/ grub rgyal gling pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rnam grong pa mkhan chen ye shes
rnam rgyal/ po ta la gong dkar mkhan chen bstan 'dzin tshul khrims/ khyab bdag he ru ka mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //gnyis pa grub chen sa ra ha pas

gar dbang gi rigs la/ slob dpon padma badzras padma zab pa'i rgyud la brten nas bkral ba'i 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug rgyal ba rgya mtsho lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor

mtsho/ sangs rgyan gnyan pa bkra shis dpal 'byor/ karma pa brgyad

rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ thub bstan legs bshad bzang po/ de gsum gas bdag blo gter la'o// //ma gcig grub

pa'i rgyal mo'i bka' srol ma rgyud padma'i rigs su gtogs pa tshe dpag med zhi ba lha mang zhes lha bcu gsum ma'i dkyil 'khor du 'brug pa padma dkar po'i yig steng nas dbang

rje/ 'gro mgon dwags po lha rje/ phag gru rdo rje rgyal po/ 'bri gung pa rin chen dpal/ spyan snga chos grags 'byung gnas/ yang dgon pa thugs kyi rdo rje/ spyan snga rin

kas rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga'

dbang phyug mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ kun mkhyen rab 'byams pa bsod nams seng ge gsum/ gsum gas yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ de nas rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/
rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar paN nam mkha' dpal bzang ngam/ yang na/ lha mchog seng ge nas/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge
thar paN nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen lhun 'grub dpal ldan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ byams pa
bsod nams bzang po/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang / sangs rgyas grags pa/ ngag dbang dam chos/ dpal ldan chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ des 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dang / rje
'jam dpal bstan 'dzin gnyis/ gnyis kas bdag la'am/ yang na/ sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan nas/ bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan/ rdo ring kun
spangs pa kun bzang chos kyi nyi ma'am kun dga' rgyal mtshan nam yang na blo ldan shes rab/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug /mkhan
chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ khyab bdag dbang phyug rab brtan/ mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan/ rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhyen rab byams pa ngag dbang lhun grub/ rmor
chen kun dga' lhun grub/ gnas gsar ba ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ sa skya pa chen po ngag dbang kun dga' blo gros/ thar rtse byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med/
byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ des byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ 'jam

dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ zhabs drung 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ de gsum gas bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ kun dga' bstan 'dzin nas/ khang gsar mkhan chen
'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ des so// //lam dus kyi dbang gi chu bo ma nub pa dkon mchog lhun grub dang / shar chen byams pa kun dga' bkra shis kyi yig steng nas thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni gong song ma thag pa'i rgyu dbang ji lta ba bzhin no// //bka' babs gnyis pa o rgyan gyi slob dpon padma badzras bkral ba'i dpal kye rdo rje mtsho skyes
lugs sam nas gling mar grags pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du mkhan chen byams pa tshul khrims dpal bzang gi sgrub dkyil dbang chog nag 'gros ma'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs
par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / bi lA sya badzra/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ slob dpon mtsho skyes rdo rje/ rgyal po indra bhU ti/ lcam lakShmi ka
ra/ slob dpon nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ paN chen ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ se ston kun rig zhang ston chos 'bar/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po/ stag
so ba rin chen don grub/ de dbon chos kyi shes rab/ la kha ba rgyal mtshan grags pa/ dpal chu bo ri pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ ri khrod pa blo
gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen/
rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang /

byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bla ma bkra shis dbang phyug nub bla ma bkra
shis bzang po/ mkhan chen sangs rgyas ye shes/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma/ 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ kun dga'
bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang / dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan gnyis/ gnyis kas bdag blo gter la'o// //bka' babs gsum pa grub pa'i slob
dpon chen po nag po dam tshig rdo rjes bkral ba'i dpal kye rdo rje sku/ gsung / thugs/ snying po skye rdo rje dang bzhi la lha dgu dgu ste so so'i dkyil 'khor du mkhan
chen byams pa tshul khrims dpal bzang gi sgrub dkyil dbang chog nag 'gros ma'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba rdo rje 'chang chen/ rgyal
yum rdo rje bdag med ma/ slob dpon nag po dam tshig rdo rje/ bram ze nag po shAnti bha dra/ 'gos khug pa lhas btsas/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu pa
dgra lha 'bar/ brtse chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dkar ston shAkya grags/ bde lung pa kun bzang dpal/ bla ma gung
pa dar ma ye shes/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan don grub/ sa bzang 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen rdo rje
'chang / mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge rje lha mchog seng ge buddha singha/ brang ti nam mkha' dpal bzang / khri chen bsod nams lhun grub/
mkhan

chen ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ bdag chen bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen bsod nams chos 'phel/ grub dbang sangs rgyas brtan pa/ rje nam mkha'
bsam 'grub/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ rje manydzu shrIHrje kun dga' dpal bzang / rje kun dga' 'jam dpal/ yongs 'dzin blo gros rgya mtsho/ 'jam mgon rdo rje rin chen man
chad dam/ yang na/ bsod nams dbang phyug nas lhun grub dpal ldan man gong bka' babs gnyis pa dang 'dra'o// //bka' babs bzhi pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug biRWa pa dang /
ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro mas dngos su byin gyis brlabs pa'i grub pa'i slob dpon chen po Dombi he ru kas bkral ba'i dpal kye rdo rje 'grel pa lugs sam/ Dombi lugs su grags pa
lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du mkhan chen byams pa tshul khrims dpal bzang gi sgrub dkyil dbang chog nag 'gros ma'i yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ biRWa pa/ slob dpon Dombi he ru ka a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ dza ya shrI dznyA na/ slob dpon mi thub zla ba/ dge slong
dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ sa paN kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ rong pa rgwa lo rnam rgyal rdo rje/ de'i sras rong pa shes rab seng ge zhang grags 'byor zhabs/ bla ma bsod nams lhun
grub/ bla ma ngag dbang grags pa/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ mkhas grub dpal ldan rdo rje/ rwa ston yon tan dpal bzang /

glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/ sa lo kun dga' bsod nams/ gnyan chen grags pa blo gros/ shar khang pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub
dpal ldan don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan man gong mtsho skyes lugs bzhin no// //rtsa rgyud brtags pa gnyis pa las bstan cing
/ 'jigs bral rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po dpal ldan biRWa pas rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma las dngos su gsan pa'i yum bka' bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dkyil 'khor du
dkon mchog lhun grub kyi tho yig dang / 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kun dga' bsod nams kyi sgrub dkyil dbang chog bcas kyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo rje bdag med ma/ grub chen biRWa pa/ nag po pa/ DA ma ru pa/ a wa dhU ti pa/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi/ se mkhar chu ba/ zhang dgon pa ba/
sa chen/ ne tso sbal ston/ slob dpon gnam bye ma lung pa/ bla ma shes rab grags pa/ gnam shes rab 'phags pa/ gnam mngon par byang chub brtson 'grus/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal
'phags pa/ paNDi ta shes rab rdo rje/ de gnyis kas zhang dkon mchog dpal/ chos rje brag phug pa/ des bla ma dam pa dang / ri khrod pa gnyis/ gnyis kas dpal ldan tshul khrims/
des shar chen ye rgyal dang / grub chen buddha shrI gnyis/ gnyis kas ngor chen/ de nas mus chen/ bdag chen/ rdo ring pa/ tshar chen/ klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ ngag dbang
chos grags/ a mes zhabs/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang phyug sngags

'chang kun dga' bkra shis/ yab rje bsod nams rin chen/ rje seng ge rgyal mtshan/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ byams pa nam mkha' 'chi med/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ byams
pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //rtsa rgyud brtags pa gnyis pa la brten nas slob dpon mtsho skyes zhabs dang / nA ro/ mai tra'i man ngag
mnga' bdag mar ston chen por bka' babs pa dgyes mdzad rdo rje lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho'i sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob
pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ byang sems rdo rje snying po/ ARYa nA ga rdzu na/ ARYa de ba/ tsandra kirti/ ma tanggi pa/ tai lo pradznyA
bha dra/ nA ro dznyA na siddhi/ mar pa lo tsA ba chos kyi blo gros/ rngog chos sku rdo rje/ rngog zhe sdang rdo rje/ rngog seng ge sgra/ rngog kun dga' rdo rje nas ngag
dbang yon tan rgya mtshos bdag blo gter la stsal ba'i bar gong bde mchog ma hA mA yA dang 'dra'o// //mar ston chen po'i bka' srol bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dkyil 'khor
du rje blo gros mtha' yas kyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ dpal sa ra ha/ slob dpon klu sgrub/ DA ki ma skal
ba bzang mo/ lwa ba pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar ston chos kyi blo gros/ rngog ston chos sku rdo rje/ rngog zhe sdang rdo rje/ rngog seng ge sgra/ rngog kun dga' rdo rje
nas yon tan rgya mtshos bdag pa stsal ba'i bar gong bde mchog ma hA mA yA bzhin nam/ yang na/ rngog kun dga' rdo rje yan gong ltar la/ de nas rgya sgom ye shes 'od zer/ karma
pa dus gsum

mkhyen pa/ gnyan ras dge 'dun 'bum/ tshul khrims rin chen/ rang byung rdo rje/ tshogs dpon yon tan rgyal/ rin chen rgyal mtshan/ mtshur ston chos kyi rin chen nam/ yang na/
rang byung rdo rje nas/ kar shod chos rgyal/ rgyal ba rdo rje/ mtshur ston chos kyi rin chen/ gang ltar yang / de nas/ chos dpal ye shes/ mthong ba don ldan/ go shrI dpal
'byor don grub/ zhwa dmar bzhi pa spyan snga chos grags man gong bde mchog ma hA mA yA dang 'dra'o// //kun mkhyen jo nang pa nas brgyud pa'i grub chen zhi ba sbas pa'i
lugs kyi dpal kye rdo rje lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du jo nang sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dgyes mdzad he ru ka /rdo rje bdag med
ma/ grub chen zhi ba sbas pa/ paN chen gang ba'i rdo rje/ jo nang tA ra nA tha/ phrin las dbang mo/ snying po mtha' yas/ kun bzang dbang po/ g.yu rtse 'bras spungs pa ma
ti bha dra/ dpa' bo bdun pa gtsug lag dga' ba'i dbang po/ 'be lo tshe dbang kun khyab/ dbon sprul karma rin chen/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med/ ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/
'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //dpal stag lung pa nas brgyud pa'i kye rdo rje dznyA na lugs sam nA ro lugs su grags pa lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor
du 'phags pa sangs rgyas kyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dgyes mdzad he ru ka rdo rje bdag med ma/ gsang bdag rdo rje 'dzin/ padma badzra/
indra bhU ti/ nA ga DA ki Dombi he ru ka bi na badzra/ kamba la/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ Dombi ba phyi ma/ ka na ka shrI/ badzra A ka ra/ biRYA tsandra/

ko ki lI pa/ su ma ti badzra/ buddha kIrti/ gu Na siddhi/ a pa garbha/ bai ro tsA na rakShi ta/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dznyA na badzra ta pa/ stag lung sangs rgyas dbon
grags dpal 'od zer/ sku zhang lha btsun kun dga' dpal/ lha btsun dbang phyug dpal/ bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rgyal ba bzang po/ drung blo gros rin chen/ drung don grub rin
chen/ chos dpal bzang po/ mkhar drung bsod nams bkra shis/ rje drung mtsho skyes rdo rje/ rje kun dga' bkra shis/ stag lung pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ bkra shis dpal grub/
grags pa legs grub/ bkra shis 'jam dpal rgya mtsho/ bkra shis dbang rgyal/ grags pa mthong thos/ ngag dbang phrin las bstan 'dzin/ grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dge legs dpal
'byor/ 'phags mchog chos dbyings lhun grub/ stag lung pa ngag dbang bstan pa'i nyi ma/ lha btsun don grub rgyal mtshan/ gnyis kas 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des
blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ kun dga' dpal nas/ chos rje o rgyan mgon po/ rje rgyal ba'i mtshan can/ rje ratnA ka ra/ rje grags pa'i mtshan can/ rje drung mi g.yo mgon po/
mgon po ye shes/ 'jig rten dbang phyug /padma rgyal po/ mtsho skyes rdo rje man gong ltar ro// //gnyis pa dpal kye rdo rje'i bshad rgyud thun mong ma yin pa mkha' 'gro ma
rdo rje gur gyi rgyud la brten nas 'phags yul grub pa'i slob dpon mi thub zla bas bkral ba'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos bcom ldan 'das mkha' 'gro lnga rigs bsdus pa'i
dkyil 'khor chen por rje ngag dbang legs grub kyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje

'chang / bdag med ma/ biRWa pa/ Dombi he ru ka a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ dza ya shrI/ mi thub zla ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'gog mi lo tsA ba/ mnga' ris pa gsal
ba'i snying po/ 'khon sgyi chu ba/ sa chen/ ne tso sbal ston/ stag so pa rin chen don grub/ gan pa ston dar/ gan pa so ston/ gan pa chos rgyal/ gan pa dbang rin/ gan pa
rin rgyal/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims/ shar chen ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ rje sangs rgyas dpal grub/
'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ shar khang pa shes rab rgya mtsho/ thar paN nam mkha' dpal bzang / byams pa kun dga' bkra shis/ mkhas grub dpal ldan
don grub/ shar chen shes rab 'byung gnas/ rje dam chos bsam 'grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ byams pa dpal ldan chos skyong
/ de dbon rin chen mchog grub/ chos rje rin chen lhun grub/ ngag dbang blo gros bzang po/ bshes gnyen ngag dbang bstan pa/ 'jam mgon ngag dbang legs grub/ 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'am/ yang na/ ngag dbang legs grub nas/ sprul sku shes rab rgya mtsho/ dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ des so// //mnga' bdag
lho brag pa chen po nas brgyud pa'i gur rigs bsdus lha bzhi bcu rtsa dgu'i dkyil 'khor du ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho'i sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / bram ze sa ra ha/ dpal mgon klu sgrub/ DA ki ma skal ba bzang mo/ grub chen lwa ba pa/ rnal

'byor gyi dbang phyug tai lo pa/ paN chen nA ro pa/ rje btsun mar pa lo tsA/ rngog ston chos sku rdo rje/ rngog zhe sdang rdo rje/ ra ma rdo rje grags/ bka' lung gnyan sgom/
mnga' ris pa byang chub tshul khrims/ rgya pho ba lung pa yon tan grags/ bla ma rgyal po dga' ba/ rngog seng ge sgra/ rngog chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rngog don grub dpal/
rngog byang chub dpal/ lo chen bsod nams rgya mtsho/ spyan snga chos kyi grags pa/ mkhan chen shes rab dpal/ chos rgyal rin chen phun tshogs/ rje btsun rin chen dpal/ mtshungs
med chos rgyal phun tshogs/ chos rje bkra shis phun tshogs/ rig 'dzin chos kyi grags pa/ rdor 'dzin dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog phrin las bzang po/ don grub chos
kyi rgyal po/ kun mkhyen chos kyi 'byung gnas/ karma nges legs bstan 'dzin/ karma tshe dbang kun khyab/ nges don bstan 'dzin rab rgyas/ khra leb ye shes nyi ma/ rdo rje
'chang ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //'phags yul grub pa'i slob dpon rta mchog zhabs dang / sa ra ha pa/ klu sgrub/ nag po'i zhabs sogs kyis
bde dgyes sogs rgyud sde bdun cu rtsa gnyis kyi bshad rgyud thun mong ba dpal sambu Ta'i rgyud la brten nas bkral ba'i bde mchog zhi ba rdor sems rdo rje dbyings lha sum
cu rtsa bdun gyi dkyil 'khor chen por rje ngag dbang legs grub kyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ biRWa
pa/ Dombi he ru ka a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri/ dza ya shrIH mi thub zla ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog lo shAkya ye shes/ mkhas pa gsal ba'i snying po/

'khon dgra lha 'bar/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ paN chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ gnyags
snying po rgyal mtshan/ zhang bkra shis dpal/ spang khang pa grags pa dpal/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen/ sa bzang gzhon nu blo gros/ ngor chen kun dga' bzang po/ go rams
bsod nams seng ge mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen/ dge legs bshes gnyen/ shar khang shes rab rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' dpal bzang / dpal ldan don grub/ shes rab 'byung gnas/
lhun grub dpal ldan/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ des byams pa bsod nams bzang po/ tshul khrims lhun grub gnyis/ gnyis kas gu rum pa bstan pa rgyal mtshan/ de nas ngag dbang
bsod nams bstan 'dzin/ chos rje kun dga' ye shes/ bshes gnyen ngag dbang brtan pa/ khyab bdag ngag dbang legs grub/ byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ bka' drin
mnyam med dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan nas/ ngag dbang chos skyong bzang po/ rin chen lhun grub/ blo
gros bzang po/ dbon blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bshes gnyen ngag dbang bstan pa man 'dra'o// //mnga' bdag mar pa'i bka' srol zhi ba rdo rje sems dpa' rdo rje dbyings lha so
bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor du 'jam mgon ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho'i sgrub dkyil gyi steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / tai lo pa/ nA
ro pa/ pra dznyA rakShi ta/ me dza gling pa/ rwa lo tsA

ba rdo rje grags pa/ rngog mdo sde'am zhe sdang rdo rje/ rngog kun dga' rdo rje/ rngog gzi brjid grags pa/ rngog rin chen bzang po/ rngog chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ rngog don grub
dpal/ rngog byang chub dpal/ rgyal dbang kun dga' dpal 'byor/ ngag dbang chos rgyal/ gcung rin po che/ rje 'brug pa padma dkar po/ lha rtse pa ngag dbang bzang po/ des
mi pham dbang po/ sangs rgyas rdo rje/ dpag bsam dbang po gsum/ phyi mas yongs 'dzin kun dga' lhun grub/ de nas mthu chen chos kyi mgon po/ yongs 'dzin 'jam dpal dpa' bo/
karma thub bstan ngag dbang / tshe dbang kun khyab/ karma ratna/ sgrub bla ma nA tha'i mtshan can/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med/ ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo
gter la'o/ /yang sa lugs ltar na/ sa bzang ma ti paN chen yan gong ngor saM ltar la/ de nas theg chen chos rje/ brag thog chos rje/ kun dga' rnam rgyal/ yangs pa can pa/
lung rigs rgya mtsho/ tA ra nA tha man 'og ltar ro/ /ngor lugs ltar na/ ngor chen yan gong ngor saM ltar la/ de nas dpal ldan pa/ glo bo mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub/
kun dga' grol mchog lung rigs rgya mtsho/ tA ra nA tha man 'og nas 'byung ba ltar ro/ /yang na/ ngor chen nas/ rdor 'dzin yon tan dpal/ gnas nang bla ma rgyal mtshan/ spyan
snga chos kyi grags pa/ 'bri gung rin chen phun tshogs man gong bde mchog 'khor los sgyur drug ltar ro/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang chen/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ nag po spyod
pa/ gha ma pa/ langka li pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ a wa dhU ti pa/ sau rI pa/ 'jigs med 'byung gnas/

stobs bcu pa/ rdo rje dpal/ dge mtshan dpal/ mi dbang dpal bzang / rab zhi bshes gnyen/ ra ti gupta/ shAnti gupta/ bi pu la garbha/ gang ba'i rdo rje/ tA ra nA tha/ rin chen
rgya mtsho/ ye shes rgya mtsho/ snying po mtha' yas/ kun bzang dbang po/ tshe dbang nor bu/ si tu chos kyi 'byung gnas/ karma tshe dbang kun khyab/ nges don bstan 'dzin
rab rgyas sam karma rin chen/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //gangs can bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje btsun
sa skya pa chen po la chos srung dam can rgya mtsho'i gdams ngag mang du bzhugs pa las gtso bor gyur pa rdo rje gur gyi rgyud las bstan pa'i dpal rdo rje nag po chen po
gur gyi mgon po gri gug lha lnga snyan brgyud lugs dang rgya gzhung lugs gnyis/ lha brgyad ma/ lha bcu gnyis ma/ lha bcu bdun ma ste bka' babs bzhi'i dbang bka' zab mo rnam
par dag pa lnga skyo mda' ba 'phags pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan gyi yig steng nas thob pa la/ thog mar ga ya dha ra nas brgyud pa'i gri gug lha lnga snyan brgyud lugs kyi
sindhu ra'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ padma badzra/ indra
bhU ti/ phun tshogs bde ba/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ paN chen gha ya dha ra/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes/ se mkhar chu ba zhe sdang rdo rje/ zhang dgon
pa ba chos 'bar ram rol pa'i rdo rje/ sa chen kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ shar pa shes

rab 'byung gnas/ shar pa rdo rje 'od zer/ 'phags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mthu chen a gnyan dam pa/ rong mi ye shes/ tre bo rdo rje grags pa/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/
bla ma tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ bla ma ngag gi dbang po/ mkhan chen byang chub seng ge theg chen kun dga' bkra shis/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan nam 'jam dbyangs
grags pa/ nam mkha' lhun grub bzang po/ mnyam med dpal 'dzin bzang po/ mthu chen 'jigs med dpa' bo'am kun dga' rnam rgyal/ klu dbang gling pa kun dga' rgyal po/ 'bras spungs
pa tshe dbang bkra shis/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ bod mkhar ba byams pa don grub rgyal mtshon/ mi pham chos kyi rgya mtsho/ spyan snga kun dga' don grub/ ngag
dbang kun dga' bsod nams/ de sras bsod nams dbang phyug de sras ngag dbang kun dga' bkra shis/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ bkra shis dbang phyug bkra shis bzang
po/ bstan nor/ rin chen mchog grub/ chos 'phel bzang po/ byams pa dpal ldan bzang po/ mthu chen 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin/ des bdag blo gter la'o// //bka' babs gnyis pa mal
lo nas brgyud pa'i gri gug lha lnga/ lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis ma rnams rgya gzhung lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur/ slob dpon bram ze mchog
sred/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddhA ka ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul khrims/ mal lo blo gros grags pa/ sa chen kun dga'
snying po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun

grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos rgyal 'phags pa/ bkra shis lung pa nam mkha' bsod nams/ dge sding pa chen po/ sangs rgyas dpal ba/
rin chen gling pa/ dkar shod pa rin chen rdo rje/ theg chen kun dga' bkra shis/ rdzong chung ba kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' lhun grub bzang po/ brag thog dpal 'dzin
bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal/ des klu dbang gling pa kun dga' rgyal po dang / lcang lo can pa bsod nams mchog ldan gnyis/ gnyis kas 'bras spungs pa tshe
dbang bkra shis/ des tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug gnyis/ gnyis kas bod mkhar ba byams pa don grub rgyal mtshan man bka' babs snga
ma ltar ro// //bka' babs gsum pa mi 'dra ba'i khyad par ni/ thog mar gri gug lha lnga/ lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis ma rnams kyi brgyud pa sangs rgyas phun tshogs yan bka'
babs snga ma ltar la/ de nas bsod nams dpal ldan/ nam mkha' bsam 'grub/ sa chen kun blo/ yar klung nam mkha' legs pa/ ngag dbang chos 'byor/ ngag dbang bzang po/ ngag dbang
legs grub/ mthu chen 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin/ des bdag la'o/ /yang lha bcu gnyis ma jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ltar na/ shraddhA kA ra warma nas/ jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti
sha lo chen rin chen bzang po/ dge tshul bsod nams/ rgya lcags ri gong pa/ rdzing bu kha pa shAkya grags/ spen phug pa dar ma shAkya/ bla ma bsod nams dbang phyug gan pa
rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ta dben pa chen po/ lo tsA tshul khrims

brtan pa/ byams gling paN chen bsod nams rnam rgyal/ tshar chen blo gsal rgya mtsho man sngar ltar ro// //bka' babs bzhi pa gyi ljang lugs kyi mgon po gshin rje ltar sgrub
pa lha bcu bdun ma'i dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ bram ze mchog sred/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/
nag po ro 'dzin/ lo tsA ba gyi ljang dbu dkar/ khams pa tshar dgu ston pa/ grub thob bsod nams grags pa/ bla ma yon tan/ smon mig dmar ston pa/ bla chen ra lam pa/ bla ma
zhang chung ba/ lang gro byang chub dar/ des lce mdo sde/ dpal chen skye med/ jo gdan pa gsum/ gsum gas grub ston shAkya 'bum/ de nas dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ sa skya
pa dharma gzi brjid/ nyi thog sngags 'chang kun dga' zla ba/ 'dar chen blo gros rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha rgod chos kyi rje/ brag thog bsod nams bzang po/
gong dkar rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal nas/ mthu chen 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin gyis bdag blo gter dbang por gnang ba'i bar bka' babs snga ma ltar ro// //bstan srung
kun gyi gtso bo dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po khro bo bcu'i rjes su gnang ba zab mo rje ngag dbang chos grags kyi yig steng nas legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang chen/ slob dpon bram ze mchog sred/ paN chen bde ba'i rdo rje/ shraddha kA ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ brag steng pa yon tan tshul
khrims/ mal lo blo gros grags pa/ brtse chen kun dga' snying po/ slob

dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'gro mgon chos rgyal 'phags pa/ mthu chen a gnyan dam pa/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po/ chos
rje bla ma dam pa/ sngags 'chang gzungs kyi dpal ba/ bzang po rgyal mtshan/ dge ba rgyal mtshan/ sangs rgyas mchog pa/ skyes mchog rgyal mtshan/ bkra shis seng ge blo gsal
rgya mtsho/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ dbang phyug rab brtan/ bsod nams mchog ldan/ bsod nams mchog grub/ ngag dbang lhun grub/ kun dga' lhun
grub/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ kun dga' legs 'byung / kun dga' blo gros/ yar klung pa nam mkha' legs pa lhun grub/ bkra shis dbang phyug ngag dbang chos 'byor/ bstan 'dzin
chos dpal/ kun dga' bkra shis/ kun dga' bsam gtan/ rin chen chos skyong / ngag dbang bsam gtan/ mthu chen 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ kun blo
nas zhal ngo nang brgyud kyi padma bdud 'dul dbang phyug dang / yab chen kun dga' rin chen gnyis/ gnyis kas rdo rje 'chang mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag la'o// ! //gnyis
pa gdams ngag gi skor la/ grub chen dam pa rgya gar gyis bkral ba'i dam chos sdug bsngal zhi byed las thugs dam bde gshegs bcu gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor du yig rnying gi
steng nas dbang yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rnam par snang mdzad/ shAkya thub pa/ phyag na rdo rje/ mkha' 'gro dbyings kyi gtso mo/ dam
pa sangs rgyas/ rgyal sras byang sems kun dga'/ pa tshab dgon pa tshul

khrims 'bar/ grub pa'i rgyal ba te ne pa/ rog shes rab 'od zer dang / zhig po nyi ma seng ge snye mdo smra ba'i seng ge ste sku mched gsum/ rog thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams
dpal/ rog rgyal sras kun dga' bzang po dang / kun dga' dngos grub ste sku mched gnyis/ mtshan ldan ri khrod dbang phyug mkhan chen tshul khrims phan pa/ drin can sangs
rgyas dbon po'am/ yang na/ kun dga' sku mched nas/ rgya ston smon lam shes rab dang / sangs rgyas dbon po/ gnyis kas gcen byang chub bzang po/ gcung mi bskyod rdo rje ste
dam chos kun mkhyen sku mched/ rgya sgom rdo rje gdan pa/ byang sems rgya mtsho sbyin pa/ yang na/ kun mkhyen gcen byang chub bzang po nas/ chos rje blo gros rgya mtsho/
ras chen dpal ldan bsod nams/ thugs sras bsod nams 'od zer/ lung chen pa bsod nams dpal bzang dang / rgya mtsho sbyin pa gnyis nas/ sku gsum bde chen lhun grub/ mkhas grub
nam mkha' bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs dpal 'byor lhun grub/ khyab bdag dpal 'byor phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bkra shis bzang po/ ding ri ba 'chi med blo gros brtan pa/ ding
ri ba 'chi med gzhon nu blo gros/ gnas gsar pa ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas/ bsam yas mkhan po blo gsal rab rgyas/ 'phags pa dge legs rgyal mtshan/ smin gling
khri chen 'gyur med phrin las rnam rgyal/ rje btsun ma 'gyur med phrin las chos sgron/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ bai ro tsa na blo gros mtha' yas/ des
bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ byin rlabs mkha' 'gro'i bla ma sum cu rtsa drug grub thob lnga bcu rtsa lnga/

dam pa rgya gar ram dam pa sangs rgyas man gong ltar ro// //rje dam pa rgya gar nas brgyud pa'i dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lha bcu gsum ma'i dkyil 'khor du yig rnying gi steng
nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / 'khor lo sdom pa/ shA ba rI pa/ mai tri pa/ dam pa sangs rgyas man gong gi bde gshegs bcu gnyis dang 'dra'o//
//rje btsun dam pa sangs rgyas kyi bka' srol las byon pa'i yum bka' khros ma rigs lnga rgyal chen bzhi dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor du yig rnying gi steng nas dbang
bskur rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dam pa sangs rgyas/ grogs chung dkon seng / shang sa pha lu sdems/ de nas mkha' 'gro ma'i bla ma bzhi la brgyud de/ labs khye sgron
ma/ khyi rdzi ma/ gcer bu ma/ 'pher mo ro zan/ de nas rgyal ba te ne man gong gi bde gshegs bcu gnyis dang 'dra'o// //bcom ldan 'das kyis sdom pa 'byung ba'i rgyud las/
de nas yang dag bshad par bya/ /sku ni kye yi rdo rje la/ /gsung ni sgyu 'phrul rdo rje'o/ /thugs ni 'khor lo bde mchog che/ /phrin las rdo rje 'jigs byed nyid/ /bdag
nyid gsang ba 'dus par brjod/ /ma 'ongs sems can don du ni/ /thabs 'di dag ni bstan pa yin/ /thabs kyi rim pa 'di dag ni/ /kun gyi thun mong ma yin te/ /dkyil 'khor gcig
tu dbang bskur bas/ /gsang sngags spyod pa'i rnal 'byor pas/ /rgyud sde rnam lngar gang bstan pa/ /klo klo'i skad kyis 'di sbas pas/ /thub pa'i zhal shes gsang ba 'di/ /snying
po kun gyi don gyi rgyud/ /dka' thub spyod byed thun mong min/ /

zhes sogs gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang 'di nyid kyi rgyud rin po che'i rgyal po zhes 'phags yul du bzhugs pa rnams la brten nas bla ma rdo rje gdan pas bkral zhing / grub chen
khyung po rnal 'byor gyi gser chos rgya mtsho tsam zhig bzhugs pa'i nang nas gtso bor gyur pa shangs lugs rgyud sde lnga rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor chen por jo nang gi
sgrub dkyil dbang chog dang bcas pa'i steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa la/ dgyes pa rdo rje'i ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ Dombi he ru ka ngo mtshar
rdo rje/ gandha ri pa/ rgyal ba dpal/ mi thub zla ba/ shAnti pa/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ a bha yA ka ra gupta'am bod skad du 'jigs med 'byung gnas sbas pa'o/ /gsang
'dus mi bskyod rdo rje'i ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ klu'i rnal 'byor ma/ bi su kalpa/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ 'phags pa lha/ byang chub bkra shis ma/ ma tanggi/
tai lo/ nA ro/ ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ a bha ya'o/ /bde mchog gi ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rnal 'byor ma/ lU hi pa/ Dombi pa/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ ga pA la/ dzA lendha ra/ nag
po spyod pa/ dge ba'i mgon po/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ blo gros bzang po/ a bha ya'o/ /ma hA mA yA'i ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ku ku ri pa/ padma pa/ zhi ba bzang po/ shAnti pa/
rdo rje gdan pa/ a bha ya'o/ /'jigs byed kyi ni/ rdo rje 'chang / skal ba bzang mo/ la li ta/ indra bhU ti chung ba/ dpal 'dzin/ rnam snang srung ba/ ka ma la rakShi ta/
a bha ya'o/ /rgyud sde lnga ga'i man ngag gi nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / grub pa'i dpa' bo/ rin chen 'byung gnas/ a ta ya badzra/ rA hu

la gupta badzra ste/ de ltar bla ma rgya gar ba rnams kyi bka' babs kyi chu bo gcig tu 'dus shing / rgyal bas nyan thos rdzu 'phrul chen por lung bstan pa/ sa gsum na 'gran
pa'i zla thams cad dang bral ba'i mkhas grub chen po khyung po rnal 'byor tshul khrims mgon po/ mnyam med rin chen brtson 'grus/ skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge gnyan ston
brtson 'grus seng ge chos rje ston pa chos kyi brtson 'grus/ shangs ston rin chen 'bum/ khyung po gsum pa tshul khrims mgon po/ ras chen sangs rgyas seng ge shangs dkar
ba/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang / nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya sgom legs pa rgyal mtshan/ rje kun dga' grol mchog /brag stod pa lha dbang grags pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa tA ra
nA tha'am/ yang na/ chos kyi brtson 'grus nas/ mkhas btsun rgyal mtshan 'bum/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal/ 'jag chung blo gros dpal bzang / 'jag chung kun dga' dpal bzang /
chos dpal bzang po/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab mchog grub/ kun bzang chos dbyings/ tA ra nA tha'o/ /gang ltar yang / de nas rgyal tshab ye shes rgya mtsho/ blo
gros rnam rgyal/ rin chen mnyam gzhag ye shes rgyal mtshan/ bla ma sbyin pa/ rnam rgyal don grub/ 'be lo tshe dbang kun khyab/ mchog sprul karma ratna/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur
med/ ngag gi dbang phyug yon tan rgya mtsho dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ de gnyis kas bdag blo gter dbang por stsal to// //ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro
ni gu mas mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor la dngos su stsal ba'i gdams ngag la byin rlabs sgo 'byed kyi bka' gnyis las/ 'dir

dpal 'khor lo bde mchog lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du jo nang sgrub dkyil gyi yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi
mkha' 'gro ma ni gupta ste nges par sbas mar grags pa/ mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor/ rmog lcog pa rin chen brtson grus/ dbon ston skyer sgang pa chos kyi seng ge gnyan
ston sbas pa'i rnal 'byor brtson 'grus seng ge 'gro mgon sangs rgyas ston pa chos kyi brtson 'grus/ mkhas grub gtsang pa shangs ston rin chen 'bum/ khyung po tshul khrims
mgon po/ bya bral ri khrod ras chen sangs rgyas seng ge mkhyen ldan shangs pa dkar po rin chen rgyal mtshan/ lkug lung pa mnyam med sangs rgyas dpal bzang / grub chen
nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ rgya 'di yan la brgyud pa rin chen sna bdun snga phyi gnyis zer/ sgom legs pa rgyal mtshan/ rje grol mchog chos sku lha dbang grags pa/ rdo ring
dbon kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ gsang bdag tA ra nA tha/ rgyal tshab ye shes rgya mtsho/ byams pa yon tan mgon po/ 'ja' lus mgon po dpal 'byor/ rje mgon po grags pa/ grub dbang
mgon po rnal 'byor/ rig 'dzin tshe dbang nor bu/ 'brug chen thams cad mkhyen pa bka' brgyud phrin las shing rta/ rmog lcog pa kun dga' dge legs dpal 'bar/ kun dga' lhun
grub rgya mtsho/ sapatsha blo gros su grags pa grub chen bka' brgyud bstan 'dzin/ grub brnyes karma lhag mthong / grub dbang karma nor bu/ thams cad mkhyen pa karma ngag
dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhabs/ de gnyis kas bdag blo gter la'o/ /

ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ni gu mas mkhas grub khyung po rnal 'byor la dngos su gnang ba'i zab chos dbang bka' kun gyi snying por gyur pa sgyu lus dbang mo che zhes bla ma rdo
rje 'chang / yi dam rgyud sde lnga/ mkha' 'gro rnal 'byor ma lnga/ chos skyong phyag drug pa rnams phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor du blo gsal zhabs kyi yig steng
nas dbang yongs rdzogs legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhas grub gtsang pa shangs ston yan gong ni bde ltar la/ de nas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / bla ma rdo rje gzhon nu/
nam mkha'i rnal 'byor/ byang sems sbyin pa bzang po/ grub chen thang stong rgyal po/ brgyud 'dzin blo gros rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan dar po/ kun dga' grol mchog lo chen 'gyur
med bde chen/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ rgyal mkhar rtse pa ngag dbang bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ ka spe ba ngag dbang bstan pa rab rgyas/ mang thos bsod nams chos
'phel/ 'dren mchog sangs rgyas bstan pa/ khyab bdag sangs rgyas dpal bzang / mus chen bsod nams dpal bzang / skal ldan chos nyid ye shes/ mtshungs med ye shes rgyal mchog
yongs 'dzin blo gros rgya mtsho/ 'jam dpal gzhon nu rdo rje rin chen/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ rje blo gros mtha' yas/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang
na/ tA ra nA tha yan gong gi ni bde ltar la/ de nas/ thu btsun kun dga' bsod nams/ rmog lcog pa byams pa lhun grub/ byams pa yon tan mgon po/ ngag dbang kun dga' lhun grub/
ngag dbang blo gros/ ngag dbang 'jam dbyangs/ ngag dbang chos 'phel/ blo bzang mthu stobs/ zhwa lu blo gsal bstan skyong /

'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ ngag gi dbang po yon tan rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o// //paN chen nA ro tA pa'i man ngag rje mar par bka' babs pa'i snyan brgyud nor
bu skor gsum zhes grags pa rgyas pa ras chung snyan brgyud/ 'bring po dwags po snyan brgyud/ bsdus pa ngam rdzong snyan brgyud dang gsum las/ dang po ras chung snyan brgyud
du grags pa'i dpal 'khor lo bde mchog yab bka' lhan cig skyes pa'i dkyil 'khor du rje mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i yig steng nas dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ te lo pradznyA bha dra/ nA ro dznyA na siddhi/ mar pa chos kyi blo gros/ mi la bzhad pa'i rdo rje/ ras chung rdo
rje grags pa/ khyung tshang ye shes bla ma/ des mar ston tshul khrims 'byung gnas/ nye gnas shar pa star sgom/ thugs sras ma gcig ong jo ste sbas pa'i grub thob gsum/ gsum
gas zhang lo tsA ba byang chub 'od zer/ de nas 'gro mgon lha rje dhA ra shrI/ de'i sras byang sems bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ de'i sras mo ma gcig kun ldan ras ma/ gnyal
pa gzi brjid rgyal mtshan/ la shing gi mkhan po dbang phyug shes rab/ bya btang ri khrod pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ ras chen gdan gcig pa gzhon nu dpal ldan/ la phyi ba nam
mkha' rgyal mtshan/ gung thang ba 'dul 'dzin ngag gi dbang po/ shar sangs rgyas seng ge gtsang smyon chos gyi grags pa/ rgod tshang ras chen sna tshogs rang grol/ des gnas
pa rab 'byams pa byams pa phun tshogs/ rje btsun karma bkra shis/ sman sgom sangs rgyas 'od zer te rab 'byams pa gsum/ de gsum ga dang khyad par

gnas pa rab 'byams pas rgod tshang rnam 'phrul kun mkhyen grub mchog dbang po/ de nas rgod phrug ras pa'i rnam 'phrul phrin las rgya mtsho/ rje btsun ras chung gi rnam 'phrul
dang po bka' brgyud sgron me/ rgod phrug dbon sprul byang chub gling pa gong ma yon tan rgya mtsho gtsang smyon rnam 'phrul rgyal ba 'dzam gling rdo rje/ bka' brgyud sgron
me'i rnam 'phrul ras chung sprul sku gnyis pa rig 'dzin ngag gi dbang po/ yon tan rgya mtsho'i rnam 'phrul rgyal ba ye shes skal bzang / ngag gi dbang po'i rnam 'phrul
ras chung sprul sku gsum pa grub mchog dpal ldan rgya mtsho/ rje ras chung pa'i nye gnas rin chen grags pa'i rnam 'phrul gangs dge'u pa nges don bstan 'dzin chos kyi rgya
mtsho/ dpal ldan rgya mtsho'i rnam 'phrul ras chung sprul sku bzhi pa grub mchog mthu stobs rgya mtsho/ 'brom ston rnam 'phrul kha rag pa rin chen 'od zer/ dge'u pa'i
rnam 'phrul ras chung sprul sku lnga pa bka' brgyud phrin las dbang phyug 'jam pa'i dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ karma ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ de gnyis kas bdag
blo gter la'o// //ras chung snyan brgyud lugs kyi yum bka' lhan cig skyes ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i yig cha dang brgyud pa ni yab bka' dang 'dra'o//
