rol pa'i rdo rje/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ a mo gha badzra/ che chung gnyis/ don yod rdo rje/ skyo 'od 'byung zhabs/ de'i sras skyo 'jam me dang / skyo sad de gnyis/ 'jam
me'i sras skyo khams pa/ gnyan rin chen bstan pa/ gnyan 'od srung mgon po/ gnyan ston chos kyi rgyal po/ 'dzim pa rin chen shes rab/ sems dpa' thugs rje rin chen/ shar pa
'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ cha gan pa grags pa 'od zer/ klog skya grags chen/ kun mkhyen gad pa/ sa bzang paN chen/ sa bzang 'phags pa/ kun dga' bzang po/ gu ge
paN chen/ glo bo mkhan chen legs 'byung zhabs/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ dkon mchog dpal ldan/ shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ shes rab 'byung gnas/ dam chos bsam 'grub/ sangs
rgyas phun tshogs/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub/ chab mdo bsod nams dbang phyug mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen/ sangs rgyas lhun grub/
ngag dbang bzang po/ dpal ldan phrin las/ shar bla kun dga' dpal ldan/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ sangs rgyas phun tshogs nas/
kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang / sangs rgyas lhun grub/ shes rab chos bzang / dpal ldan phrin las/ rje btsun mdo khams pa/ ngag dbang legs grub/ bstan pa
rab rgyas/ bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ rje blo gros chos 'phel/ des so/ /yang na/ grol mchog gi yig

steng nas ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtshos stsal ba'i brgyud pa ni/ gu ge paN chen yan gong ltar la/ de man 'jam rdor ltar ro// //rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po rol pa'i
rdo rjes ye shes kyi DA ki ro langs ma las dngos su gsan pa'i snyan brgyud rdo rje'i tshig rkang gi man ngag zab mo/ 'phags yul paN grub rgya mtsho'i thugs dam gyi snying
por gyur pa/ bal yul ye rong dI paM ka ras rwa chen rdo rje grags pa la chig brgyud du stsal ba'i dpal rdo rje'i 'jigs byed rwa khrid mkha' 'gro'i snyan brgyud kyi nyams
khrid ngag dbang chos grags kyi rnam bshad/ mkhyen brtse'i khrid yig /kun dga' bsod nams kyi chos 'byung khog phub tu btad nas rnam bshad zin thun dang / khrid dngos la
sngon 'gro rnams dang / dngos gzhi'i bskyed rim la spyi bye brag la sems 'dzin pa phyi'i rnal 'byor/ nang du gnas lnga'i rdo rje 'jigs byed sogs la sems 'dzin pa nang gi
rnal 'byor/ lha sku gsal stong bde chen du bsgrub pa'i phyir rwa rtse'i rnal 'byor phyi nang gnyis dang sbyang gzhi sbyong byed/ rdzogs rim la gsang dbang / sher dbang /
bzhi pa'i lam gsum las/ dang po lus gnad 'khrul 'khor/ ngag gnad rdor bzlas/ yid gnad rlung lnga'i ting 'dzin/ lus rtsa grol ba'i thabs/ gtum mo ye shes kyis bdud rtsi 'bebs
thabs/ sher dbang la phyag rgya dngos dang ye shes gnyis/ dbang bzhi pa spros bral de kho na nyid/ rjes brtan zhing bogs dbyung ba/ spyod pa gsum dang lam gyi 'bras bu
mngon du gyur pa'i 'bras bu bcas legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje ro langs ma/ grub chen la li ta badzra/

a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ grub chen padma badzra/ bal po dI paM ka ra/ rwa lo rdo rje grags/ rwa lo tsA ba chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng /
rwa dharma seng ge /rwa dkon mchog seng ge /rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rgyas ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ dwang ma brtson 'grus byang
chub/ nyan po kun dga' rgya mtsho/ dbur stod pa rin chen/ yer pa ba brtson 'grus rgya mtsho/ mal gro ba chos skyong rgyal mtshan/ bla chen yon tan rgya mtsho/ tshar chen
blo gsal rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug mkhan chen bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ bsod nams chos 'phel gnyis/ gnyis kas dbang phyug rab brtan/ mgon po bsod
nams mchog ldan/ ngag dbang chos grags/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub/ kun dga' legs 'byung / mus chen bsod
nams dpal bzang / mus chen chos nyid ye shes/ 'chi med bstan pa'i nyi ma/ sngags 'chang kun dga' rin chen/ byams pa smon lam grags pa/ 'jam dbyangs blo gsal/ 'jam dbyangs
mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'am/ yang na/ kun dga' legs 'byung yan gong ltar la/ de nas/ kun dga' blo gros/ kun dga' mkhas grub dbang po/ byams pa kun
dga' bstan 'dzin/ shar bla kun dga' dpal ldan/ kun dga' bstan pa'i blo gros/ ngor mkhan chen dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ des so// //grub chen lU hi pa'i zhal snga
nas legs par bkral ba'i dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i bskyed rim dang rdzogs rim bsdu ba

gsum pa'i nyams khrid rdo rje 'chang mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i zhabs kyi bskyed rdzogs shin tu bsdus pa bde chen 'dod 'jo dang / grol mchog khrid brgya/ mnyam med shar tsong
kha pa chen po'i rdzogs rim rnal 'byor chen po'i steng nas nyal/ ldang / khrus/ tshad med/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bdag bskyed/ mchod pa/ bzlas pa ste brgyad/ gnas pa'i rim
pa la spyi bye brag gi sems 'dzin/ ldang ba'i rim pa la/ spyod lam/ gtor ma/ kha zas kyi rnal 'byor sogs dang / rdzogs rim la rdo rje sems dpa'i bsdu ba/ yi ge bsdu ba/
thig le bsdu ba/ rjes spyod pa la brten nas 'bras bu 'grub tshul sogs legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen yan gong dbang gi skabs kyi sa lugs brgyud pa ltar la/ de
nas mus chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge dkon mchog 'phel ba/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong khyi chen kun dga' bsod
nams/ mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ 'jam mgon a mes zhabs kun dga' bsod nams/ mus bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub/
mkhas grub sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ gnas gsar kun dga' legs pa/ sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ kun dga' mkhas grub dbang po/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ kun gzigs mkhyen brtse'i
dbang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang dge phyogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha ba rI pa/ lU hi pa/ dA ri ka pa/ dril
bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ dzA landha ra/ nag po spyod pa/ gu hye pa/

rnam rgyal zhabs/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa sku mched/ klog skya shes rab brtsegs/ mal lo blo gros grags/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ grags rgyal/ sa paN/ bsod nams seng ge
/mkhas btsun sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge /bu ston rin chen grub/ khyung lhas pa gzhon nu bsod nams/ rje 'jam dpal snying po/ mkhas grub
smra ba'i nyi ma/ ba so chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ grub chen chos kyi rdo rje/ dben sa pa blo bzang don grub/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas ye shes/ blo bzang chos rgyan/ sngags
chen dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ lcang skya blo bzang chos ldan/ rje ngag dbang brtson 'grus/ 'jam dbyangs bde ba'i rdo rje/ rje btsun ngag dbyangs byams pa/ klong rdol ngag
dbang blo bzang / yongs 'dzin ngag dbang chos 'phel/ 'jam mgon byams pa phun tshogs/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po la brgyud pa gnyis 'dus su gyur/ des bdag la'o/
/yang na grol mchog gi yig steng nas rje ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho las thob pa'i brgyud pa ni khrid brgya ltar ro// //'phags yul grub brgya'i ded dpon slob dpon nag
po'i zhabs kyis legs par bkral ba'i dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi rdzogs rim rim pa bzhi pa'i nyams khrid rje 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i bskyed rdzogs mdor bsdus bde chen
snying po dang / grol mchog khrid brgya'i yig steng nas sngon 'gro skyabs sems/ rdor sems/ dga' ba gsum/ tshogs gsag rten dang brten pa'i bskyed rim dang / rdzogs rim la
sngon 'gro/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ dngos gzhi la shes brgyud kyi rim pa/ nyams len sngags kyi rim pa/ skye ba ye shes kyi rim pa/ 'bras bu gsang ba'i rim pa sogs legs par thob

pa'i brgyud pa ni/ ngor chen yan gong dbang gi skabs kyi brgyud pa ltar la/ de nas gu ge paNDi ta/ grol mchog man gong gi gsang 'dus 'jam rdor khrid brgyud bzhin no// //grub
pa'i slob dpon chen po rdo rje dril bu zhabs kyis legs par bkral ba'i dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi grol byed rim pa lnga'i nyams khrid rje ngag dbang legs grub kyi yig steng
nas lan gcig dang / thar rtse mkhan chen gyi rnam bshad/ khrid yig /'chad thabs bcas kyi steng nas lan gcig nos pa'i tshul la/ sa bon dang bcas pa dang / rnam pa sna
tshogs pa dang / sa bon med pa'i sna tshogs rdo rje'i rim pa dang / nor bu 'gengs pa'i rim pa la dam tshig gi phyag rgya/ lag brda'i phyag rgya/ chos kyi phyag rgya/ phyag
rgya chen po dang / dzA landha ra'i 'khor lo so sor spo ba'i rim pa dang / bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rim pa/ de kho na nyid la blo gzhag tshul sogs legs par thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ slob dpon dril bu pa/ gang ba'i lha/ kha che paNDi ta/ seng ge dpal/ zhang ston phyar bu ba/ byang sems 'bri lung pa/ khro
phu lo tsA ba/ rin chen seng ge /rin chen grub/ khyung lhas pa/ shar chen ye rgyam/ ngor chen rdo rje 'chang / gu ge paN chen/ glo bo mkhan chen legs 'byung / rje grol
mchog lung rig rgya mtsho/ tA ra nA tha/ rin chen rgya mtsho/ dznyA na sA ga ra/ si tu chos 'byung / karma 'gyur med/ zur mang bla ma nor bu/ bstan 'dzin phun tshogs/ ngag
dbang bzang po/ ngag dbang legs grub/ kun dga' dpal 'byor/ rdo rje 'chang mthu chen 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ khyung lhas pa yan gong ltar
la/ de nas nor bzang rin chen/ rin chen rgyal

mtshan/ mkhyen rab mchog grub/ rig 'dzin grub pa'i rgyal po/ bro lung pa/ byang gling rje/ dpal ldan chos bzang / rin chen rgya mtsho/ zhwa lu pa rin chen bsod nams mchog grub/
kun dga' bsod nams/ grub mchog sangs rgyas bstan pa/ byams pa bzang po/ byams pa rab brtan/ sangs rgyas dpal bzang / 'jam dpal chos mchog rin chen don grub/ rin chen
skal bzang / bla ma dpal 'byor zhabs/ blo gsal bstan skyong / thar rtse mkhan chen byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ rje dbon 'jam dpal rgya mtsho/ mchog sprul
snyan grags bstan pa'i dbang phyug des bdag la'o// //rje btsun sa skya pa chen po'i lcags ri'i khongs las mi 'da' ba'i gser chos bcu gsum gyi ya gyal rje btsun rdo rje rnal
'byor ma nA ro mkha' spyod kyi nyams khrid mkhyen brtse'i khrid yig la zhal shes rnams kyis brgyan pa dang / sa chen kun blo'i 'chad thabs bcas kyi yig steng nas rnal
'byor bcu gcig gis khog phub ste bskyed rim sems 'dzin dang bcas pa dang / rdzogs rim la'ang chos nyid dngos su brtan pa dang / chos nyid rgyud nas brtan pa gnyis kyi phyi
ma la'ang / gzhi chos can 'khor ba'i gnad/ lam ji ltar bsgom pa'i gnad/ 'bras bu mthar thug sangs rgyas kyi sa'i gnad kyi skor rnams dang / mthar bsam gyis mi khyab thun
mong ma yin pa sogs legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gong sngags 'chang sangs rgyas rin chen bzhugs pa'i byin rlabs kyi brgyud pa ji lta ba bzhin no// //bal po yi rong
paNDi ta skal ldan bzang po la rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor mas dngos su stsal ba'i dpal 'khor lo bde mchog bong bu'i zhal can gyi nyams khrid rdo rje 'chang

mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyi khrid yig bde chen thig le'i steng nas brten bskyed rim sems 'dzin dang bcas pa dang / brten pa rdzogs rim phra thig gi rnal 'byor legs par thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ kun dga' grol mchog yan gong dbang gi brgyud pa ltar la/ de nas 'jam rdor khrid brgya ltar ro// //ras chung mkha' 'gro'i snyan brgyud kyi khrid brgyud ni
gong dbang dang 'dra'o// //mdo rgyud bstan bcos thams cad kyi snying po/ 'jig rten dang 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dngos grub thams cad kyi 'byung gnas/ dus gsum bde gshegs
thams cad kyi bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug rnams kyi 'jug ngogs/ khams drug dang ldan pa'i rdo rje'i lus can gyi gang zag rnams tshe gcig la sangs rgyas
kyi 'bras bu la dus myur bar sbyor nus pa'i dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i zab khrid sbyor ba yan lag drug la rje btsun sgrol mgon zhabs kyi khrid yig mthong ba don ldan dang
/ 'jam mgon yon tan rgya mtsho'i khrid bsdus sngon 'gro sogs kyi steng nas sngon 'gro rnam bzhi/ rten bskyed rim sems 'dzin dang bcas pa dang / rdzogs rim nyer bsdogs dben
pa gsum dang / dngos gzhi sor sdud bsam gtan sku rdo rje'i rnal 'byor/ srog 'dzin gsung rdo rje'i rnal 'byor/ rjes dran thugs rdo rje'i rnal 'byor/ ting nge 'dzin ye shes
rdo rje'i rnal 'byor sogs legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ jo nang tA ra nA tha yan gong dbang gi brgyud pa ltar la/ de nas rin chen rgya mtsho/ blo gros rgyal mtshan/
ngag dbang phrin las/ ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ kun dga' chos 'phel/ ngag dbang dri med/ ngag dbang chos 'phel/ bdag cag gi dus zhabs pa blo gros mtha' yas/

dang po'i sangs rgyas mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ de gnyis kas bdag blo gter la'o// //dus gsum bde gshegs thams cad kyi bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam/ mdo rgyud man ngag thams cad kyi
snying po/ 'jigs bral rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug biRWa pa la rje btsun rdo rje bdag med nas dngos su stsal ba'i gdams ngag snyan brgyud tshad ma bzhi dang ldan pa'i gsung
ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i khrid mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags kyi yig cha rnams kyi steng nas khog phub zin thun dang / gzhung ji lta ba bzhin bkri
ba'i khrid kyi sngon 'gro snang ba gsum dang / dngos gzhi rgyud gsum gyi sgo nas bkri ba la kun gzhi rgyu'i rgyud la 'khor 'das dbyer med kyi lta ba bsgom pa'i khrid kyi
nang gses lhan cig skyes pa'i chos gsum gyis mdor bstan/ nyams su blang ba'i gnas gsum gyis rgyas par bshad/ rgyud gsum gyis shin tu rgyas par bshad pa la/ nges 'byung
bskyed pa ma dag snang ba'i khrid/ lhag bsam bskyed pa nyams kyi snang ba'i khrid/ spro ba bskyed pa dag pa'i snang ba'i khrid kyis rgyud sbyangs nas rig thog tu brdar sha
gcad/ de dag gi skabs su dam tshig rnam bshad gtad/ lus thabs rgyud la dbang bzhi dang rjes su 'brel ba'i lam bsgom pa la/ dang po bum dbang la rnam bshad zin thun dang
/ phyi nang gi bskyed rim sems 'dzin dang bcas pa/ zhar byung lta ba/ grub mtha'/ 'da' kha ma/ bar do/ 'bras bu/ gsang dbang gi lam bdag byin brlabs/ khams 'dus pa dang
po rlung sbyor bdun dang / gtum mo'i dmigs skor nyer dgu drod rtags/ zhar byung lta ba sogs lnga/ sher dbang gi lam khams 'dus pa bar ma dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo 'dod pa'i
lcags kyu/ dga' bzhi lugs

'byung dang lugs ldog tu nyams su blang ba/ zhar byung lta ba sogs lnga/ dbang bzhi pa'i lam khams 'dus pa tha ma rba rlabs gsum/ zhar byung lta ba sogs lnga/ mthar thug sku
lnga ye shes lngar lhun grub kyi khrid sogs legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gong kye rdor man ngag lugs kyi tshar lugs dbang brgyud ltar ro// //dpal mkha' 'gro ma rdo
rje gur gyi dag pa gsum gyi khrid 'gro mgon 'phags pa rin po che dang / rje grol mchog zhabs kyi yig steng nas sngon 'gro rnams dang / dngos gzhi de bzhin nyid kyi dag pa/
lha so so'i dag pa/ rang rig pa'i dag pa sogs legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ Dombi pa/ ngo mtshar rdo rje/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri/ bsod
snyoms pa/ mi thub zla ba/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi/ se mkhar chu ba/ zhang dgon pa ba/ sa chen/ bsod rtse/ grags rgyal/ sa paN/ chos 'phags/ dga' ldan pa/ brag phug pa/
blo gros brtan pa/ dpal tshul ba/ shar chen/ ngor chen/ gu ge paNDi ta man grol mchog khrid brgya spyi ltar la/ rje mkhyen brtse'i zhabs dang / 'jam mgon yon tan rgya
mtsho gnyis ka las bdag blo gter gyis nos so// //dpal yang dag par sbyor ba'i rang byin brlabs kyi dmigs pa nyi shu rtsa dgu'i zab khrid gsung ngag rin po che'i pod dmar
las byung ba'i yig cha dang / rje grol mchog gi khrid brgya'i yig steng nas legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sa paN yan gong dag pa gsum gyi khrid brgyud ltar la/ de nas
tshogs sgom pa/ gnyags snying po rgyal mtshan/ bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ buddha shrI/ ngor chen/

dpal rdor ba/ dpal ldan tshul khrims man grol mchog khrid brgya spyi ltar las/ rje mkhyen brtse'i zhabs dang / ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ de gnyis kas bdag blo gter la'o//
//mnyam med jo bo chen pos bkral ba'i dge bshes bka' gdams pa rnams kyi gsang chos thig le bcu drug gi gdams pa'i nyams khrid rje mkhyen brtse'i yig steng nas sngon 'gro
sbyor ba'i chos drug dang / skyes bu gsum gyi lam rim/ dngos gzhi la bla ma rjes dran/ 'gro kun pha ma rjes dran/ gnas lugs rtong pa rjes dran/ rang lus lha sku rjes
dran/ ngag sngags kyi rdzes dran/ rdor bzlas sogs legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ lnga pa rin po che yan chad dbang brgyud ltar la/ de nas sgrub khang pa dge legs rgya mtsho/
phur bu lcog ngag dbang byams pa/ yongs 'dzin paNDi ta ye shes rgyal mtshan/ gung thang 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ /dkon mchog bstan pa rab rgyas/ yongs kyi dge ba'i bshes
gnyen 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ rje ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ de gnyis kas bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang khrid brgya'i brgyud pa ltar na/ rje blo gros mtha'
yas/ des so// //gangs can bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rdze btsun sa skya pa'i bstan srung kun gyi gtso bo rdo rje gur la phyi nang gsang ba'i khrid tshul mang du bzhugs pa las/
phyi srung ba'i 'khor lo rdo rje brag rdzong ma'i nyams khrid mkhyen brtse'i khrid yig /rdo ring pa'i zhal shes/ zhwa lu mkhan chen gyi 'chad thabs bcas kyi steng nas/ thog
mar khro bcu'i rjes gnang gis snod rung du byas shing / khrid dngos la sngon 'gro thun mong dang thun min/ dngos gzhi srung ba/ bzlog pa/ gsad pa/ mnan pa bcas ma tshang
ba med pa legs

par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / bram ze mchog sred/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shrAddhA ka ra warma/ rin chen bzang po/ yon tan tshul khrims/ blo gros grags
pa/ brtse chen kun snying / slob dpon bsod rtse/ rje btsun grags rgyal/ chos rje sa paN/ 'gro mgon chos 'phags/ mthu chen a gnyan/ bdag nyid chen po/ nam mkha' legs pa/
bla ma dam pa/ kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ blo gros rgyal mtshan/ kun spangs chen po/ blo gsal rgya mtsho/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug bslab gsum rgyal
mtshan/ dbang phyug rab brtan/ bsod nams mchog ldan/ bsod nams mchog grub/ ngag dbang lhun grub/ kun dga' lhun grub/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho/ kun dga' legs 'byung / kun dga'
blo gros/ yar klung nam legs/ bkra shis dbang phyug ngag dbang chos 'byor/ bstan 'dzin chos dpal/ kun dga' bkra shis/ kun dga' bsam gtan/ rin chen chos skyong / ngag dbang
bsam gtan/ mthu chen 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ kun blo nas/ nam mkha' 'chi med/ kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ rje shes
rab rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o// //da ni tha mar dge ba'i tshe khrid rnam pa gsum las/ dang po dpal 'khor lo bde mchog dkar po'i tshe khrid zab pa bzhi ldan rje mkhyen brtse'i
zhabs kyi yig steng nas phyi'i tshe sgrub/ nang gi tshe sgrub/ gsang ba'i tshe sgrub/ zhar byung bogs 'don nam mkha'i bcud len bcas legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
'khor lo bde mchog rdo rje phag mo/ shAkya shrI/ sa paN/ g.yag sde ba/ mnga' ris pa sangs rgyas ye shes/

mkhan chen bsod nams grags pa/ grags pa tshul khrims/ byang sems bya sder ba/ sa bzang / ngor chen/ bsod nams dbang phyug drung btsun dpal rgyal rje/ sangs rgyas rin chen/
grol mchog man khrid brgya ltar la/ 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ rje blo gros mtha' yas/ de gnyis kas bdag blo gter la'o/ /7 skyabs rje mkhyen brtse rin po ches
bo dong lugs kyi khrid brgyud rang rkang pa yar 'brog rdo rje phag mo chos dbyings bde chen mtsho mo las gsan kyang de'i brgyud pa ni ma rnyed do// //gnyis pa ma gcig grub
pa'i rgyal mo'i man ngag /rje btsun 'ja' tshon sku can ras chung rdo rje grags pa nas 'ba' ra rgyal mtshan dpal bzang gi bar du snyan brgyud kho nar bzhugs shing / da lta'i
bar du lam 'di la brten nas dngos grub kyi mtshan ma brnyes pa bar ma chad par byon pa'i mgon po tshe dpag med kyi nyams khrid rje tshar chen rin po che'i yig cha pad
dkar bzhad pa'i steng nas yang gsang lha gcig bum gcig gi byin rlabs kyis rgyud smin par byas nas/ 'jam mgon mkhyen brtse'i yig cha gzhir gzung / ngag dbang yon tan rgya
mtsho'i khrid yig gis khog bkrol te/ sngon 'gro thun mong ba bzhi/ dngos gzhi la rten bskyed rim/ tshe bcud bsdu ba'i dmigs skor bdun/ rdzogs rim la sbyor ba lus gnad/
dmigs gnad/ stong ra bsgom pa/ dngos gzhi gnas pa rtsa yig g.yo ba rlung / bkod pa byang chub kyi sems/ rjes steng 'og gi sgo bsdam pa/ snying gar tshe phur gdab pa/ bar
chad kyi 'brang dgag pa/ zhar byung bcud len gyi rnal 'byor bcas ma tshang ba med pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgyal ba tshe dpag med mgon/ ma gcig

grub pa'i rgyal mo/ ti phu gsang sngags sdong po/ ras chung rdo rje grags pa/ rje mi la/ sgom po pa/ mtha' rtsa ba/ 'bri gung pa/ spyan snga rin po che/ yang dgon pa/ spyan
snga rin chen mgon po/ zur phug pa/ 'ba' ra rgyal mtshan dpal bzang / rin chen 'phel/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ mkhyen rab chos rje/ rdo ring pa/ tshar chen/ mkhyen brtse'i
dbang phyug bslab gsum rgyal mtshan/ dbang phyug rab brtan/ bsod nams mchog ldan/ bsod nams mchog grub/ ngag dbang lhun grub/ blo gros chos 'phel/ ngag dbang ye shes/
chos grags rgya mtsho/ chos kyi rgya mtsho/ chos dbyings rdo rje/ blo gsal bstan skyong / mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ rdo rje 'chang ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ de gnyis
kas bdag blo gter la thugs dgyes bzhin du bka' drin stsal ba'o// //gsum pa dpal ldan sa skya pa'i zab chos dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po dkar po'i tshe khrid
chig brgyud ma tshar chen rin po che'i yig steng nas tshe bcud bsdu bstim gyi gnad/ bzlas pa sngags kyi gnad/ g.yo ba rlung gi gdan rnams legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ sprul sku shes rab rgya mtshos bdag blo gter la stsal ba'i bar gong khro bcu'i brgyud pa ltar ro/ /yang na/ mthu chen 'jam dpal bstan 'dzin/ des bdag blo gter la'o//
! //rtsa ba'i sa bcad gsum pa sgra dang yi ge lhan cig byed rkyen la ltos pa'i slob ma rnams kyis chos la dbang za mi dgos par ji dgar spyad chog pa'i lung gi skor la/ rgya
zhung rnams ni phal cher dbang khrid kyi brgyud par 'dres shing / bstan 'gyur lung bzhugs pa'i sdebs su yod pa rnams

ni bstan 'gyur gyi lung rgyun spyi ltar rje thub bstan legs bshad bzang po las bdag gis nos so/ /rdo rje'i tshig rkang rnams ni pod so so nas nos so/ /gong ma lnga'i gsung
phran bu yod pa rnams ni bka' 'bum brgyud pa ltar ro/ /yig cha so so'i khungs yig rnying la/ bu ston gyis mdzad pa'i yig cha rnams las 'od zer dri med ni/ chos rje thams
cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ sku zhang lce btsun nam mkha' mchog grub/ bla ma don grub legs pa/ kun mkhyen tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/
sku zhang mkhyen rab mchog grub/ byang gling pa dbon po rin chen rgyal po/ 'brog khang pa don grub rgyal mtshan/ byang gling bkra shis rgyal mtshan/ chos rje dkon mchog
rgyal mtshan/ mkhan po bsod nams mchog grub/ mkhas dbang rin chen dge legs/ chos rje bsod nams rgya mtsho/ rin chen 'jam dpal mkhyen rab/ dge slong rin chen bstan dar/
lce btsun bstan 'dzin phrin las/ rje ye shes dpal 'byor/ rdo rje 'chang blo gsal bstan skyong / mkhan chen byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ ngag gi dbang phyug
'jam dbyangs rin chen rdo rje/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /don yod zhags pa ni/ bu ston/ slob dpon 'jam dpal grub bzang / bla ma gnyal pa dge legs dpal/ bla ma rnam rgyal dpal
bzang / lce btsun chos rgyal/ mkhas pa tsandra shrI/ kun mkhyen tshul khrims rgyal mtshan man 'dra/ rnam snang mngon byang ni/ bu ston/ mkhan po grags gzhon/ 'jam dbyangs
grags pa rgyal mtshan/ yon tan dpal/ blo gros bzang po/ mkhyen rab rje man 'dra/ rdor dbyings/ dpal mchog chos dbyings gsung dbang / gshed dmar lha bcu gsum ma/ 'jigs
byed/

thugs chen pad drwa/ dus 'khor bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bu ston/ thugs sras/ nam mkha' mchog grub/ tsandra shrI man 'dra/ khams gsum rnam rgyal/ rtse mo/ gtsug dgu gsum ni/
bu ston/ dpal mchog don grub/ tsandra shrI man 'dra/ ngor chen gyis mdzad pa'i yig cha rnams ni/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug
yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ rgyal ba lha mchog seng ge 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mus chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / kun mkhyen dpal
ldan don grub/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' sangs rgyas/ mtshungs med bsod nams rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen lhun grub dpal ldan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ 'dren mchog
bstan 'dzin lhun grub/ byams pa dpal ldan chos skyong / de'i dbon rin chen mchog grub/ mgon bla kun dga' bsod nams/ ye na bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ grub dbang dge 'dun rgya
mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ dpon slob ngag dbang legs grub/ dA'u bstan bdag sprul sku/ chos rje ngag dbang rgya mtsho/ kun mkhyen 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya
mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad ba'i yig cha rnams kyi ni/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / mkhas grub
dpal ldan don grub/ 'jam mgon dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ mkhas grub sangs rgyas phun tshogs/ mtshungs med bsod nams dpal ldan/ mkhan chen dpal ldan chos skyong / de'i dbon
rin chen mchog grub/ lhun grub steng gi bla ma kun dga' bsod nams/

ye na bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma dam pa dge 'dun rgyal mtshan/ byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/ sprul sku shes rab rgya mtsho/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ des bdag
blo gter la'o/ /thar paN bka' 'bum rnams kyang brgyud yig ma rnyed kyang lung thob bo/ /zhu chen tshul khrims rin chen gyi yig cha rnams kyi ni/ ldan lo tshul khrims rin
chen/ thugs sras kun dga' bsod nams/ mang thos bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ rdor 'dzin dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ bla ma phrin las rin chen/ lhun grub steng gi dbu mdzad bla ma 'jam
dbyangs blo gsal/ thams cad mkhyen pa 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan/ 'jam dbyangs shes rab rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter
la'o/ /jo nang sgrol mgon zhabs kyi yig cha rnams ni/ rje btsun tA ra nA tha/ blo gros rnam rgyal/ ngag dbang phrin las/ kun bzang dbang po/ tshe dbang nor bu/ si tu karma
bstan pa'i nyin byed/ zur mang tshe dbang kun khyab/ dbon sprul karma rin chen rnam rgyal rdo rje/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med/ ngag dbang yon tan rgya mtsho/ bla ma blo
gros bzang po/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /yang na/ karma 'od gsal 'gyur med nas/ lung rtogs klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ rje ngag dbang chos 'phel/ rdor 'chang ngag dbang nor bzang
/ 'dren mchog kun dga' rgya mtsho/ dzaM thang bla ma bstan 'dzin rgya mtsho/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /go bo rab 'byams pa kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge'i yig cha rnams
ni/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge dkon mchog 'phel/ dkon mchog lhun grub/ nam mkha' dpal bzang / rtse gdong khri chen kun dga' bsod nams/

mkhan chen ngag dbang chos grags/ a mes zhabs kun dga' bsod nams/ mus pa bkra shis lhun grub/ mkhan chen bzang po rgyal mtshan/ rmor chen kun dga' lhun grub/ mkhas grub sangs
rgyas rgya mtsho/ ngag dbang kun dga' legs 'byung / sa chen kun dga' blo gros/ ri phug sprul sku kun dga' mkhas grub dbang po/ thar rtse byams pa kun dga' bstan 'dzin/
rdo rje 'chang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang po/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /sa skya pa kun blo'i gsung rnams ni/ mdzad pa po kun
dga' blo gros/ gzims 'og bstan 'dzin phrin las/ byams pa phrin las yon tan/ byams pa bstan 'dzin snyan grags/ a mdo bla ma mkhyen rab don ldan/ hor rong pa tsha ba snyan
grags bstan pa'i dbang phyug des bdag blo gter la'o/ /dpon slob ngag dbang legs grub gsung rnams ni/ mdzad pa po/ kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /zhwa lu
mchog sprul blo gsal bstan skyong gi gsung rnams ni/ mdzad pa po/ rje mkhyen brtse'i zhabs/ grwa sgang dbon po/ dge 'phel mchog sprul/ des so/ /blo gros mtha' yas kyi gsung
rngog dkyil rnams ni/ mdzad pa po/ bla ma padma nor bu/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /de las gzhan pa'i blo gros mtha' yas kyi gsung rnams ni/ mdzad pa po/ bla ma karma gsal
byed/ des so/ /rdo rje 'chang mkhyen brtse'i dbang po'i bka' mdzod rnams ni/ mdzad pa po/ kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ des so/ /

thub bstan legs bshad bzang po'i gsung rnams ni/ mdzad pa po nor bu bstan 'dzin/ des bdag blo gter la'o/ /dmigs kyis ma bsal ba rnams ni dbang brgyud dang 'dra'o/ /dbang dpe
min pa'i dpe tshan ji yod kyang lung thob pa sha stag go/ //rtsa ba'i sa bcad bzhi pa gang las 'phro ba'i gzhi'am 'byung gnas rdo rje 'chang chen po'i gsung rdo rje 'chang
gi rgyud sde rnams la khungs gtugs te nges shes mi 'phrogs par ster zhing / rnam gzhag thams cad khong du chud pa'i slad du rgyab brten rgyud kyi bshad bka' la brgyad
las/ dang po rnal 'byor bla med pa rgyud mtha' dag gi gtso bo zab pa dang rgya che ba'i rgyud thams cad kyi rgyal po dpal gsang ba 'dus pa dang / gnyis pa rnal 'byor bla
med ma rgyud thams cad kyi mthar thug pa dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi rgyud/ gsum pa rdo rje phur pa rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi dum bu chos rje sa skya paNDi tas bsgyur ba rje bla
ma mkhyen brtse'i zhabs la nye brgyud kyi bshad bka' bzhugs pa/ de dang 'brel ba'i dpal yang dag he ru ka'i gsang thig bzhi pa 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi mtshan yang dag par
brjod pa'i rgya cher bshad pa rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyi de kho na nyid gsal ba'i nyi ma chen po/ lnga pa rgya che ba gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal dus kyi 'khor
lo'i rgyud 'grel pa dang bcas pa/ drug pa dpal yang dag par sbyor ba'i rgyud 'grel pa dang bcas pa/ bdun pa dpal mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur gyi rgyud 'grel pa dang bcas
pa rnams ni 'og kha skong du 'chad par 'gyur la/ brgyad pa 'dir zab pa gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po dpal kye rdo rje'i rgyud kyi bshad bka' la/ de'i bshad lung
gi rgyun da lta'i bar du bzhugs pa dang / nye brgyud kyi dbang du byas na/ rje

btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi ye shes sgyu ma'i rnam rol rje bla ma mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyis mang mkhar mu gu lung lo tsA phug tu 'od gsal phyag rgya chen po'i
ngang nas mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho las rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi bshad bka' cha lag dang bcas pa gsan pa dang / slar yang dpal brtse ba chen po las kyang gsan pa'i lo rgyus
ngo mtshar can bzhugs pa'ang gtan tshigs kyi srog tu bzung ste nos pa'i tshul la/ nyin dang por/ bla slob thun mong du gnas khang byin rlabs dang / lam dus srung 'khor
yan grub mtshams/ slob dpon gyis mngon rtogs 'bring po'i mthar dbyung nas/ gtor chog mdzes rgyan bzhin thams cad kyis gtor ma dbul/ de nas brgyud 'debs kun khyab ma dang
/ maNDal sngon du 'gro bas/ tshul dang po rgyud sde spyi'i rnam gzhag nas dbu brtsams te tshul gnyis pa rgyud kyi mtshan don bstan pa yan chad gsung bshad rgyas par mdzad
mthar/ bla slob kun gyis kolla i re TaThi nas/ de yis sangs rgyas myur thob shog /gi bar gtor chog gzhug ltar bsngo smon rnam par dag pas grol/ nyin gnyis par/ sngon
'gro rnams kha sang ltar la/ tshul gsum pa rgyud kyi 'chad thabs nas brtsams te zin thun du bcad de/ tshul dang po gsum slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo zhes rgya gar
gyi chu bo ganggA tshun chad du 'gran zla spangs pa'i mkhas pa/ sku lus ma spangs par 'og min chen por mngon sum du gshegs pa de nyid kyis mdzad pa'i rgyud sde spyi rnam
dang / tshul dang po rgyud kyi mngon par rtogs pa gangs ri'i khrod tsam na mngon par mtho ba rdo rje 'dzin dbang bye ba'i gtsug rgyan rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi
gsung rab rin po che'i ljon shing la/ ngor chen dkon mchog lhun

grub kyis mdzad pa'i gong ma'i dgongs rgyan gyis kha 'gengs bcas gzhir bzhag ste/ de gnyis kyi sa bcad rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pas mdor bstan/ gzhung so so la 'bru gnyer
ba'i sgo nas rgyas par bshad/ ngor chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gsung rab tshul gsum mdzes rgyan dang / ljon shing mdzes rgyan gnyis sa gzhung sbrags
ma zhib bshad dang bcas pas don bsdu ba'i tshul gyis gtan la phab pa sngon du 'gro bas/ rgyud bshad dngos gzhi la/ 'jam mgon sa skya paNDi tas mdzad pa'i gsung rab ltar
sa bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan/ rje btsun rin po che'i rnam 'grel dag ldan gyi 'bru bsnan pas rgyas par bshad/ rgyud rang gi tshig don mdor bsdus pa'i tshul gyis bshad pas
ngag 'don snying por dril ba'i bshad lung sbrags ma nyin bco lnga'i bar legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa la gnyis/ 'grel pa lugs gtso bor bton pa'i brgyud pa dang / man ngag
lugs kyi bshad pa'i brgyud pa'o//dang po ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug biRWa pa/ Dombi he ru ka a la la badzra/ dpal ldan nags khrod pa/
garbha ri pa/ bsod snyoms pa dza ya shrI/ slob dpon sbyang dka' zla ba/ de la slob ma'i mchog dpa' bo rdo rje/ seng ge rdo rje/ sgra gcan 'dzin dang gsum las/ 'dir dge slong
dpa' bo rdo rje/ des lo tsA ba chen po shAkya ye shes la gnang / de la 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ mnga' ris pa gsal ba'i snying po/ se mkhar chu ba kun rig 'khyin lo
tsA ba 'od kyi snang ba dang bzhi las/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ rje sa chen/ yang na/ bla ma mnga' ris pa/ 'khon sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar/ rje sa chen/ yang na/ se mkhar
chu ba/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/

rje sa chen/ yang na/ 'khyin lo tsA ba/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ rje sa skya pa chen po'o/ /de ltar brgyud pa'i bka' babs chen po bzhi dang ldan pa'i bla ma sa skya pa chen
pos/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ tshul khrims grags pa/ gtsug tor rgyal po gsum la gnang / de gsum gas rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ des chos
rje sa skya paNDi ta chen po/ des 'phags pa rin po che la/ de nas dga' ldan pa bkra shis dpal/ chos rje brag phug pa bsod nams dpal/ bla ma blo gros brtan pa/ bla ma dpal
ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ de gnyis ka la rgyal tshab dam pa
kun dga' dbang phyug dang / kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge gnyis/ de gnyis ka la yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ de nas thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub/ thar rtse
paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ 'di yan bshad pa rgya cher gnang ba'i rgyun dang / man gtso bor lung gi brgyud pa'o/ /mchan/ thar rtse nam
mkha' sangs rgyas/ sgrub khang pa dpal mchog rgyal mtshan/ rje don grub rgyal mtshan/ khams ston nam mkha' dpal bzang / 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas ye shes/ 'jam mgon sa skya
pa chen po kun dga' blo gros/ mkhan chen chos bkra shis/ mkhan chen kun dga' rab rgyas/ rab 'byams smra ba chos dpal 'byor/ mkhan chen ngag dbang grags pa/ 'dar mkhan
chen kun dga' dpal bzang / slob dpon kun dga' 'jam dbyangs/ 'jam mgon ngag dbang legs grub/ rje bla ma rdo rje 'chang 'jam dbyangs mkhyen brtse'i dbang

po/ mkhan chen rdo rje 'chang dpal ldan blo gros rgyal mtshan/ des bdag blo gter dbang po la dgyes pa chen pos bka' drin du stsal ba'o/ /yang rgyud rkyang gi bshad lung ni
rje bla ma nyid kyi zhal nas kyang thob/ yang 'jam mgon blo gros mtha' yas kyi yig steng nas brtag gnyis kyi rgyud bshad thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje mkhyen brtse'i zhabs
nas/ 'jam mgon blo gros mtha' yas/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na/ dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ rab 'byams pa kun dga' mchog ldan/ mang thos klu sgrub rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen ngag dbang
chos grags/ 'di yan bshad pa rgya cher gnang ba'i rgyun/ mchan/ byams pa ngag dbang rnam rgyal/ byams pa bkra shis lhun grub/ 'phags chen chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ mang
thos bsod nams dbang phyug rje chos kyi nyi ma/ bla ma bkra shis chos bzang / sprul sku ngag dbang bsod nams/ rdo rje 'dzin pa dge 'dun rgya mtsho/ bla ma ngag dbang bzang
po/ 'jam mgon ngag dbang legs grub man 'dra/ yang na/ dkon mchog lhun grub nas/ de'i dbon sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang man 'dra'o/ /gnyis pa man ngag
lugs kyi bshad srol gyi ring brgyud ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ biRWa pa/ nag po pa/ DA ma ru pa/ a ba dhU ti pa/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi lo tsA ba/ de la slob ma'i
mchog bzhi las/ 'dir se mkhar chu ba/ zhang dgon pa ba/ rje sa chen man sngar dang 'dra'o/ /nye brgyud ni/ rje btsun chen pos/ bla med phyogs ni ris sgyur mig dang bcas/
/rig byed kyis bsal lag pas me la bgos/ /de 'od kun gsal chu gter 'byung bar bcas/ zhes dang / legs 'ongs mig gis yon tan gsal bar byas/ /

zhes te/ biRWa pas sa skya pa chen po la rgyud sde bdun cu rtsa gnyis kyi bshad bka' tshul bzhis gsal bar byas pa gnang ba las gtso bor rgyud gsum gyi brgyud pa la/ bdag med
ma/ biRWa pa/ sa chen/ rtse mo/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ dkon mchog dpal/ bsod nams dpal/ bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan tshul khrims/ chos rje ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ngor
chen kun dga' bang po man gong dang 'dra'o// //de ltar smin grol rgyab brten dang bcas pa 'di dag bdag cag gi drin chen rtsa ba'i bla ma mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen gzigs
chen po byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyis 7.ngor chen rdo rje 'chang gi gsan yig rgya mtsho ltar rtsa ba'i 'chang gzhi dkar chag tu btab pa rtsa bar bzung /
der ma 'khod pa rgyun rnam dag yod nges dag rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rje bla ma mkhyen brtse'i zhabs kyi bka' ltar kun mkhyen rin po che rnam pa gnyis sogs las gsar du zhus
te yid bzhin gyi nor bu lta bu'i rgyud sde chen po rtsod bral 'khrul zad kyi bka' 'di dag snyigs ma'i 'dam rdzab kyi khrod du nub par phongs pas rgyud rgya gzhung gi dgongs
pa bod gangs can pa'i shing rta chen po rnams kyis bkral ba ltar la/ sogs khongs bkrol ba tsam ma gtogs tha na phyag len phra mo tshun chad grub mtha' so so'i bzhed
srol gtsang mar bkod cing / thog mtha' bar gsum gyi dka' gnad rnams 7.rje bla ma rnam gnyis dang / mkhas pa'i dbang po dag la zhus mthar gyis phyogs dang ris su ma chad
par stabs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i bka'i bsdu ba chen po 'di nyid tshang la ma nor ba'i chos kyi phung po chen por bsgrubs pa yin la/ de'ang yig cha phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs

pa tsam du ma zad/ rdo rje 'chang gi bka' lhad med kyi rgyud sde chen po 'di dag rgyu mtshan rtogs pa'i rnam dpyod dang ldan pa lta srid na/ bka' srol zab mo gcig gi rgyun
tsam nub na'ang 'dzam bu'i gling gi dpal dang 'byor pa 'di'i thad na sbun par nges pa'i blo skye bar 'gyur ba ltar/ don che la 'bras bu de tsam du che bar mthong bas deng
nas brtsams te ji srid pa bstan pa rin po che nam gnas kyi bar du mi nyams shing / 'di nyid don du gnyer ba'i skal bzang / nyams su len pa'i rnal 'byor can/ gzhan la spel
ba'i lhag pa'i bsam par 'chang ba su gang dag 'byung bar 'gyur ba la rtsol sgrub kyi ngal bas bsgrub bya lag tu mi lon par bar ma dor chud za ba'i g.yangs las bde blag
tu bsgral te rang nor rang gis spyod pa la tshegs med pa bzhin du 'dod rgur rtsen chog pa'i phyir dang / gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa'i lag rjes ma dag pa rgyun 'byams pas
mthar gyis rdo rje'i gzhung thams cad la nor 'khrul gyi dri mas kun nas bslad par srid pas de spang ba'i phyir dang / rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa rin po che 'jig rten na sangs
rgyas las kyang 'byung bar dkon pa dang mjal ba'i dus 'dir ji mi snyam du mi 'dor bar 'di lta bu'i brtson pa dang ngal ba bdag gir bzhes te gus pa'i sri zhu ci nas kyang
mdzad par rigs so zhes gzhan dag la gsol ba 'debs pa'i phyir dang / legs byas kyi sgo thams cad las phul du byung ba dam pa'i chos kyi phyogs la bya ba byas pa yin pa
dang / smon lam thams cad kyi mdo chos 'dzin pa'i smon lam la 'dus par sangs rgyas nyid kyis gsungs pas na chos kyi snying po rdo rje theg pa la ches mchog tu 'dzin pa
dang bsrung ba la bsod nams kyi mthu rlabs po che 'byung bar nges shes kyis rang gzhan thams cad la thar pa'i sa bon

'debs pa'i phyir dang / khyad par du'ang rtsa ba'i rigs bdag chos kyi dbyings su snyoms par zhugs pa rnams kyi dgongs pa'ang 'di kho nas rdzogs la/ da lta 'tsho zhing gzhes
pa rnams kyi sku tshe mdzad phrin gyi bar chad thams cad kyang 'dis sel zhing / ji ltar bzhed pa'i phrin las thams cad kyang 'dis byed do snyam nas bka' drin gyi byas pa
mtha' gcig tu gzo ba'i phyir dang / gzhan yang nag po'i phyogs kyi sde chos la zhe sdang ba rnams kyis log par lta ba'i blo brtsam pa dang bcas cig car du 'gyur ba sogs
'jig rten gyi rgud pa byung ba thams cad zhi zhing / ma byung ba mi 'byung ba'i rgyu bstan pa rin po che'i dpag bsam ljon pa'i skyabs su skye rgu rnams bde skyid kyi dga'
ston nyams su myong ba bcas kyi ched las/ rang nyid kho na bde ba'i rgyu dang / gzhan la 'gran pa dang / gzhan las khyad du byar 'dod pa dang / rgyu 'di las bsnyen bkur
gyi tshigs su bcad pa thob tu re ba la sogs pa'i bsam pa med cing / rang gzhan thams cad la gnas skabs dang mthar thug kun tu sman pa lhur blangs nas ji ltar 'du bgyis pa'i
yi ge'i tshogs ma lus pa gzhi gcig tu grub na bskal pa'i mthar yang 'dzad du med pa'i ngo mtshar spar gyi 'phrul chen mo mngon par bskrun pa'i legs byas stobs su smin
pas bod gangs can gyi ljongs snyigs ma'i mun pas mog bor byas pa nyid rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa'i nyi ma lnga na med pa shar bas bstan pa dang sems can gyi khams na rdzogs
ldan gyi snang ba gsar pa zhig lhag par gsal bar gyur cig/ //slar smras pa/ rab 'byams dkyil 'khor gtso bo'i ting 'dzin la/ /mnyam par 'jog bzhin zab gsang rdo rje'i lam/
/dmigs med thugs rje'i ljags kyis

'doms mkhas rnams/ /bka' drin dran pas slar yang phyag bgyi'o/ /mgon rnams mi 'phrogs pa yi mkhyen rab dang / /mnyam par 'grogs pa'i gsung gi gsang ba las/ /snyigs ma'i mthar
yang rgyud sde che rnams kyi/ /bstan pa nyin mor mdzad la su mi rangs/ /sa la sangs rgyas dngos su byon pa yi/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa'i tshogs kyis skal bzang bdag /mtshan
tsam thos dka' rdo rje'i lam mchog 'dir/ /bde blag drang ba'i bka' drin gzhal snga min/ /de phyir 'og min zhing du rigs drug pa'i/ /dag pa'i 'khor rnams rjes su bzung ba
bzhin/ /dus dang mi 'tshams chos kyi dga' ston gyi/ /nor bu'i bang mdzod dbang 'di bla ma'i drin/ /rje btsun bla ma rnams kyi thugs bskyed dang / /bdag gi mos dge gtsang
ma'i rten 'byung las/ /'di nas tshe gcig rdo rje 'chang pa'i sar/ /'khrid pa'i lam srol ma tshang med pa thob/ /zab rgu thob pa'i rnam grangs ma nges pa'i/ /the tshom rkang
pa ring po'i gom stabs kyis/ /bsam dpyod yangs pa'i thang chen gzhal ba 'ga'/ /tshul min nam mkhar 'dom gyis 'jal dang mtshungs/ /de phyir yongs 'dzin mkhas pa'i ded dpon
gyis/ /smin grol gdams pa'i nor bu gang stsal ba/ /brjed ngas 'jigs pa'i dgra 'dis bcom dogs nas/ /srung byed yi ge'i khang bzang gsar du bskrun/ /de mthus thub bstan
mdo dang sngags kyi tshul/ /nam mkha' ji srid 'gro ba'i sgron me ru/ /lung rtogs 'od kyi drwa ba 'bum 'gyed bzhin/ /'jig rten khams na 'grib med gsal gyur cig /gangs ri'i
khrod na zab rgyas rgyud sde'i tshogs/ /rdo rje 'chang gi lung bzhin bshad sgrub mkhan/ /dpal

ldan sa skya pa zhes dpyod ldan la/ /grags pa don ldan bstan pa rgyas gyur cig /khyad par gsang chen lam gyi kha 'babs bzhi/ /'phags bod paN grub drin las 'dir thob gang /
/rgyun mi 'chad phyir lhag bsam khur blangs pa'i/ /ngal ba 'bras bcas bstan la sman gyur cig /lta spyod cho ga rnam par dag lam nas/ /skal bzang su dag rnam grol la 'khrid
cing / /mkhas tshul gsum gyis rgyal bstan nges skyong ba/ /rnam 'dren mchog rnams zhabs pad brtan gyur cig yongs rdzogs bstan dang khyad par rdo rje'i theg /gdul bya spyi
dang snyigs ma'i skye rgu la/ /phan mdzad phrin las nyi zla'i snang ba can/ /sngon byon skyes chen dgongs pa rdzogs gyur cig /gsang ba mchog 'di'i bka' yi bsdu ba'i srol/
/thog mar btod pa mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen/ /byams pa kun dga' bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi/ /thugs bskyed bzhed don ji bzhin skong gyur cig /mkhyen brtse'i dkyil 'khor
kun la snyoms pa'i klong / /zab rgyas gdams pa gtan pa med 'jo bas/ /ring nas re ba yid bzhin rdzogs mdzad pa/ /'jam dbyangs bla ma dgyes pa'i dpyid gyur cig /rdo rje'i
lus mchog bskyed dang g.yo ba'i blo/ /dge la rnal du 'god pa'i bshes gnyen sogs/ /gnas skabs mthar thug phan pa'i grogs bgyid pa'i/ /'brel thogs sku bzhi'i sa la 'god
gyur cig /yangs pa'i ljongs kun bde skyid rdzogs ldan gyi/ /dga' ston dpal la rtag tu rol bzhin par/ /dam pa'i lam du zhugs las rtsod pa dang / /'tshe ba kun bral chos bzhin
spyod gyur cig /bdag kyang bstan la gus pa'i bsam sbyor rigs/ /grub pa de srid 'tsho ba bzang pos 'byor/ /

bka' drin gsum bdag dpal ldan bla ma rnams/ /mnyes pa'i sgrub la smon pa 'grub gyur cig /de ltar mngon 'dod don kun 'grub pa dang / /khyad par rdo rje'i bka' rnams gsal bsdus
pa'i/ /phrin las spel la mthu ldan srung ma'i tshogs/ /rgyal bas gnyer du gtad pa don yod mdzod/ /sangs rgyas dkon mchog mchod dang bsnyen bkur dam chos dkon mchog klog
dang sgrub/ /dge 'dun dkon mchog phyogs mthar dar rgyas rin chen gsum gyi mnga' thang dpal/ /'jig rten dge ba'i skyabs kyi gdugs bzang mngon mthor brtan pas khebs pa'i
'og /phan bde'i grib bsil khor yug yangs par rtag tu legs gnas bkra shis shog /ces dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho'i rdo rje'i slob dpon chen po mnyam pa med pa'i thugs rje mnga'
ba rnams kyi bka' drin las/ rdo rje'i theg pa'i rgyud sde rin po che rtsod pa dang bral ba 'di dag gi bka' srol rnam par dag pa'i rgyun bzhugs so 'tshal bsod nams kyi skal
bar nos pa yid bzhin nor bu brgya stong lag tu thob pas dper bya mi bzod pa'i dad 'dun lhag bsam chud ma zos par gyur pa'i spro ba ches cher 'phel ba dang 'phrel/ bstan
par sman du re zhing don du gnyer ba'i skye bo mchog rnams la thog ma'i smin grol gyi sgo 'phang rdzogs par dbye ba'i skabs/ mkhyen rab kyi dbang phyug hor dge 'phel sprul
pa'i sku rin po che snyan grags bstan pa'i dbang phyug dang / nang chen skyil tsha bla ma bslab gsum nor 'chang tshul khrims dbang phyug dpon slob nas brgyud pa'i yi ge
khog bsgrigs gnang 'dug pa la/ lam 'dir rtsol ba chen po'i khur len pa po 'jam dbyangs blo gter dbang pos rang nor rang gces kyi tshul du dpyad cing zhus te rjes

'jug rnams kyi yid brten pher bar gtan la phab pa ste/ rnam rgyal chu stod zla ba'i dkar po nam gru'i 'grub sbyor gyi nyin grub par bgyis pa bstan pa rin po che spyi dang /
bye brag lam 'di'i bka' srol phyogs dus gnas skabs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas pa'i rgyur gyur cig/ //sarba dA ka lyA NaM bha ba tu// //
